Chapter 151: Sixth Elder

Spotless Peak[1] was the elegant residence of Sixth Elder. It was slightly similar to the Moon Laurel Celestial Palace, accepting only female disciples. Among all the beautiful women here, the most stunning one was naturally Sixth Elder. It was also rumored that Sixth Elder and the palace leader of the Moon Laurel Celestial Palace were best friends.

Lu Yang had heard his senior brothers mention Sixth Elder multiple times. They all reminded him that Sixth Elder was a breathtakingly beautiful woman and that he had to maintain his composure when he saw her.

“Lu Yang? What are you doing here?” Tao Yaoye bumped into Lu Yang at the bottom of Spotless Peak.

Tall, youthful, and pretty, Tao Yaoye stood out in the crowd.

Lu Yang took out the ancient text. “Big Senior Sister told me to hand this to Sixth Elder.”

“Shifu is out to take care of some matters and won’t be back for an hour. Do you want to come in and sit for a bit?” Tao Yaoye invited.

Lu Yang revealed an eager yet hesitant expression. “Wouldn’t that be inconvenient? I’m a man...”

“It’s fine. Besides, the two of us have the lowest cultivation on Spotless Peak. Nothing can happen.”

Lu Yang stared at Tao Yaoye silently. Her eyes were clear, as if she was completely oblivious to the psychological trauma her words had just inflicted upon Lu Yang. He could only sigh and follow Tao Yaoye. Unbeknownst to Lu Yang, when Tao Yaoye turned her head to the front, her lips curled into a sly smile.

Lu Yang said, “Oh, right! I still owe you five contribution points. I’ll return them to you now.” He had borrowed the contribution points from Tao Yaoye when he bought the Ten-Buffalo Strength Pill. The pill turned out to be quite effective and was of significant help to Lu Yang.

“You still remember? I had forgotten all about it.” Tao Yaoye chuckled.

Suddenly, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy recalled that Yun Zhi had rewarded her with many contribution points because she was an honorary guest elder of the Dao-Seeking Sect and had also killed a Fusion cultivator. “Speaking of which, don’t I also have a lot of contribution points? Lu Yang, Lu Yang, I want to exchange them! I want to redeem something!”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy made such a racket that Lu Yang could only acquiesce. “After we leave Spotless Peak, I’ll take you to the rewards board. You can buy whatever you want then.”

“That sounds more like it.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy nodded in satisfaction, feeling that Lu Yang was a promising talent.

Tao Yaoye pointed at a pool and warned Lu Yang, “Be careful of that place. You mustn’t go there.”

The pool was shrouded in mist, obscuring the view within, and the melodious sound of laughter that resembled ringing bells could be heard.

“My senior sisters like to bathe there. A few years ago, a senior brother relied on his superior evasion techniques to sneak into Spotless Peak and peek at my senior sisters. Then, his blood-curdling screams could be heard.”

“Where is this senior brother now?”

“He is extremely skilled in escape spells and has vanished without a trace.”

Dang, Spotless Peak is so dangerous... Lu Yang was glad that he was an upright gentleman.

Tao Yaoye led Lu Yang to her usual training ground. “Want to spar a bit?”

“Sure,” Lu Yang accepted and pulled out his Qingfeng Sword.

It was only then that the Everlasting Immortal Fairy remembered that Lu Yang had a Sword Spirit Root and should be using a sword. Ever since my resurrection, I’ve never seen Lu Yang wield a sword.

“Senior Brother Lu, be careful. I’ve learned something new in the last two months.” Tao Yaoye opened a red paper umbrella.

As she flicked her wrist and loosened her grip slightly, the red paper umbrella began spinning. Peach blossom petals fluttered everywhere like rain and snow, blocking Lu Yang’s line of sight.

Sword rays sliced through the air with a whistling sound, aiming to sweep the petals away.

Behind Lu Yang, the peach blossom petals gradually formed a human figure. Tao Yaoye closed her paper umbrella and slashed it down horizontally.

Lu Yang seemed to have anticipated Tao Yaoye’s move. Holding his sword with one hand behind his back, he blocked the attack.

It was unknown what material the red paper umbrella was made of. It met the Qingfeng Sword head-on without a single scratch.

Sword light suddenly flashed, its speed catching Tao Yaoye’s off guard.

“Pointing Word Mantra!” Lu Yang’s gaze sharpened as he thrusted his sword toward Tao Yaoye’s chest without mercy.

Tao Yaoye let out a soft chuckle and retreated backward, the tip of her umbrella colliding with the tip of the sword in an attempt to disrupt Lu Yang’s sword technique. However, Lu Yang’s hand remained steady and pursued Tao Yaoye relentlessly, pointing the sword toward her.

Amidst the rain of peach blossoms, the Qingfeng Sword and red paper umbrella clashed. With their nimble techniques, they danced around each other, their fleeting figures disappearing from sight every now and then. Both of them had won and lost in some aspects, but neither found the opportune moment to deliver a fatal blow.

Suddenly, Lu Yang’s eyes brightened as he found a flaw in Tao Yaoye’s defense. The Qingfeng Sword traversed through the peach blossom rain as smoothly as a swimming fish and rested itself against Tao Yaoye’s neck.

“I admit defeat.” Tao Yaoye put her hands up to surrender.

Lu Yang shifted his moves again, piercing his sword toward an empty place. The real Tao Yaoye was astonished to see the gleaming tip of the sword pointed right at the middle of her forehead.

This time, she truly admitted defeat. The peach blossoms vanished, and so did the “Tao Yaoye” who surrendered—everything had been an illusion.

“How did you tell where the real me was?” Tao Yaoye was not particularly upset about losing once as she was adept at learning from experiences.

“The cultivation technique I practice is the Clear Heart and True Nature Mantra. It can see through all illusions; it is your nemesis.”

“Clear Heart and True Nature Mantra? I’ve never heard of it.”

“I invented it,” Lu Yang said proudly. Writing a cultivation technique by yourself is no small feat.

Tao Yaoye was about to say something else when she noticed a crimson mist soaring overhead. “Shifu is back.”

~~~

Tao Yaoye led Lu Yang to Sixth Elder’s cave abode. Just like the senior male disciples had described, Sixth Elder was extremely gorgeous, different from Yun Zhi’s icy beauty. Sixth Elder wore a gentle smile, resembling a caring elder sister with a warm and comforting vibe.

Wheeze...wheeze...wheeze. Suddenly, Lu Yang found it a bit suffocating, as if all the oxygen around him had disappeared. He desperately tried to gasp for air, attempting to inhale even just a bit of oxygen but to no avail.

“Yaoye, didn’t you tell him about me?”

Tao Yaoye slapped her forehead. “I forgot.”

Tao Yaoye hurriedly pulled Lu Yang away to a safe distance from Sixth Elder.

Lu Yang felt like a fish that had just returned to the sea as he tried his best to breathe. Wheeze...wheeze. “What’s going on?”

Tao Yaoye smiled at him apologetically. “I’m sorry! I forgot to tell you that my shifu has the Immaculate Celestial Physique, so she is unsullied by dust and will automatically expel the surrounding air. She herself can’t control it either, so anyone who gets close to her will feel their breath taken out of them. You just have to hold your breath.”

Lu Yang, “...”

No wonder people say that Sixth Elder is a “breathtakingly” beautiful woman. Is everyone in the Dao-Seeking Sect so honest? You don’t even use adjectives but speak the plain truth?

Lu Yang held his breath and approached Sixth Elder again. For a Foundation Establishment cultivator, as long as they prepared beforehand, holding their breath for a while was no problem. When one reached the Golden Core Stage and could circulate the energy within themselves, it was fine even if they didn’t breathe.

“Greetings, Sixth Elder. I am Lu Yang.” Lu Yang bowed respectfully. “Shifu has mentioned you, telling me that he regards you as his own elder sister.” When they were on the flying carriage, the Taciturn Daoist Priest had spoken of his relationship with Sixth Elder affectionately, almost moving Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou to tears.

Sixth Elder laughed coldly. “Is that so? I have always regarded him as my own grandson.”

Lu Yang was stumped for words. Should I just mention Big Senior Sister’s name in the future? I think I should just forget about Shifu’s embarrassing name which only draws resentment.

1. A more literal translation would be “free of dust.” ☜

Chapter 152: Tree-Planting Mantra

“This is the ancient book Big Senior Sister instructed me to give you.” Lu Yang didn’t bring up his master anymore and took out the book on cultivation insights for the Immaculate Celestial Physique.

Sixth Elder was surprised. “Little Yun is really considerate; to think she found such a good thing.” There aren’t many cultivation insights for celestial physiques, and even fewer suited for me.

A wide smile spread across Sixth Elder’s visage, as if she had just found a cherished book at the bookstore and couldn’t wait to read it back home.

“The Cultivation Diary of Chi Qianqian.

“Year one of cultivation: Shifu told me that my Immaculate Celestial Physique is one in a thousand and that my cultivation speed far surpasses my peers. What great news! I must work hard in my cultivation...

“Year two of cultivation: My cultivation is really fast. Others are still at the Level Nine Qi Training Stage, while I am already at the Foundation Establishment Stage. The characteristics of the Immaculate Celestial Physique are also gradually showing themselves. I can’t disappoint Shifu. I must work hard in my cultivation...

“Year three of cultivation: Advancing through the cultivation stages is faster than drinking water. I am already at the Golden Core Stage, and I’ve even formed the Immaculate Golden Core, a first-class Golden Core unsullied by dust. Shifu said that cultivation knows no bounds and that I should not be complacent. I must work hard in my cultivation...

“Year seven of cultivation: The Nascent Soul Stage...”

Sixth Elder kept flipping through the book, engrossed in reading the life experiences of cultivator Chi Qianqian from the Great Yu Era. It could be described as grand and tumultuous. Finally, she turned to the last page, and a shiver ran through her heart.

The previous page noted that she had just reached the Apex Void Refinement Stage, so she should be at the Fusion Stage from the next page. But why is there only one page of her experience at the Fusion Stage? Could she have met with some mishap?

Sixth Elder suppressed her uneasiness and read the last page. “Year six hundred of cultivation: I have finally reached the Fusion Stage. I won’t get to the Transcendent Tribulation Stage anyway, so I’ll just give up and let it rot!”[1]

End of diary.

Sixth Elder didn’t know what to make of it as she rubbed her temples, trying to internalize what she had just read. I can’t say that it’s completely useless. The records of her cultivation journey from the Qi Training to Void Refinement stages are very detailed and can be of some reference value to me.

“Please thank Little Yun on my behalf. Since Little Yun manages the Dao-Seeking Sect, even if I want to repay her, there’s nothing I have here that would catch her eye. I have heard Little Yun mention that your talent for spells is unique and has the potential to establish a new sect. How about this? Why don’t I give you a spell book?” Sixth Elder smiled warmly as a vacuum field had formed around Sixth Elder, only allowing communication through one’s spiritual consciousness.

Lu Yang agreed.

“However, my attack methods rely on the might of the celestial physique, so I don’t have spells suitable for you.” Sixth Elder pondered what kind of spell would be appropriate for Lu Yang. “Oh right, why don’t I give you the book on the Tree-Planting Mantra?”

“Tree Planting Mantra?” Lu Yang’s expression turned odd. This name sounds so ordinary. What can I do after mastering it? Plant trees all over desolate mountains and promote a new model of green development in the cultivation world? Or will Big Senior Sister award me with small red flowers[2] and confer me the title of “Little Environment Protector” if I plant many trees?

Sixth Elder could easily tell what Lu Yang was thinking. “Don’t underestimate this spell just because of its nondescript name. This is a spell highly coveted by countless cultivators. After mastering this spell, you can promote the growth of spirit plants, and all the large sects would even want to enshrine you.

“Look at Second Senior Brother. Why do you think he can guard the herb garden? It’s because he is the best at the Tree-Planting Mantra in our sect.”

Lu Yang contemplated for a bit and found that it did make sense. If I can master this spell, I’ll lead a life full of comfort. Since all the large sects have their own gardens and plantations, they’ll be fighting over me.

Sixth Elder added, “You may also practice this in your spare time. It can help calm your mood and is beneficial for cultivating the mind and body.

“Yaoye has learned the Tree-Planting Mantra quite well. If there’s anything you don’t understand, you can ask her.”

Lu Yang accepted the book and thanked Sixth Elder before leaving her cave abode with Tao Yaoye. After departing, the two resumed breathing.

Tao Yaoye suggested, “Since it’s still early, why don’t we just study at my place? I can also teach you if necessary.”

Lu Yang nodded.

~~~

The Tree-Planting Mantra was a difficult wood-type spell that used one’s spirit energy to promote the growth of spirit plants. The barrier to entry was high; achieving minor success was challenging, and it was all the more so for perfecting it with major success.

To begin, one first required a calm mind to enter a state similar to the oneness of heaven and human. In this state, one would comprehend and perceive plants and align with their growth patterns, allowing them to flourish naturally yet swiftly.

“When you start out, it’s best to use ordinary seeds. Our spirit energy can easily let seeds grow into trees. The legendary cultivation genius could even make the tree, flower, and fruit grow in one go during their first attempt.

“Willow trees are attuned to human nature and are thus the most ideal for practicing the Tree-Planting Mantra. Senior Brother Lu, this is a willow seed. Hold on to it properly, close your eyes, and see if you can resonate with it.” Tao Yaoye passed a piece of willow fluff to Lu Yang.

He followed the instructions recorded in the Tree-Planting Mantra and combined that with Tao Yaoye’s tips as he earnestly tried to comprehend with his heart.

A gentle breeze brushed past his face, blowing across the lawn. The rays from the sunlight were not overly intense, bathing people in a very comfortable sensation.

Lu Yang gradually emptied his mind, feeling himself drifting between heaven and earth and faintly grasping the life vein patterns of the willow seed.

Sensing the changes in Lu Yang, Tao Yaoye was astonished. It took me three days just to achieve this step, and Shifu already praised my comprehension ability for being exceptional even throughout history.

Yet Senior Brother Lu did it in just an hour!

“I’ve long heard that Senior Brother Lu’s talent in spells is top-tier, even surpassing his swordsmanship, but I didn’t think it was to such a degree. No wonder Big Senior Sister guides him personally. With a talent like his, probably no one else can teach him,” Tao Yaoye mumbled to herself.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy overheard Tao Yaoye’s murmurs and agreed wholeheartedly. Exactly! Even I can’t teach him.

At this moment, Lu Yang gained an epiphany. He placed the willow fluff on the ground, pointed at it, and used his own spirit energy as the growing impetus for the willow fluff.

“Grow!” Lu Yang shouted.

Quite some time passed, but nothing happened.

Tao Yaoye reminded softly, “Umm, Senior Brother Lu, usually when planting trees, people bury the seeds in the ground.”

“That makes sense.” Lu Yang picked up the willow seed and activated the spell “Shrinking Earth,” immediately shrinking into the earth.

Tao Yaoye’s eyes widened. Senior Brother Lu also knows the Earth Escape Spell, one of the Five-Element Escape Spells?

The Earth Escape Spell was the most convenient among the Five-Element Escape Spells and was an excellent choice for attacking, fleeing, and hiding. Tao Yaoye wanted to learn the Earth Escape Spell, but it was too difficult for her, so she eventually gave up.

“But why does Senior Brother Lu’s Earth Escape Spell seem different from the one I learned?” Tao Yaoye mused out loud.

Just then, she saw a willow tree spring up from the ground.

“Successful on the first try?!” Tao Yaoye exclaimed. I wasted four willow seeds before finally succeeding.

“Hmm?” Tao Yaoye rubbed her eyes, thinking that her eyes must be playing tricks on her—the willow tree shot up from the ground with two Lu Yangs hanging from both ends of the tree.

Lu Yang dangled from the tree in utter despondence as if his heart had turned to ashes, swaying back and forth.

Where on earth did I go wrong this time? Why did the tree grow two of me when I only planted one willow seed?

1. The “bailan” movement in China is where people decide to give up and just leave things be. It’s also sometimes known as quiet quitting. ☜

2. It is somewhat of a culture to gift small red flowers to reward someone, such as in schools. ☜

Chapter 153: “Vegetative Person”

Legends said that during the founding of the Great Yu Dynasty, there once was a cultivation genius with a talent that nearly rivaled that of immortals. He possessed an innate affinity for spells, capable of mastering any spell swiftly. This cultivation genius’ progress far surpassed what anyone could have imagined, achieving the cultivation realm every cultivator pursued for a lifetime with record speed. He reached the Transcendent Tribulation Stage, and his title was “Myriad Arts Daoist Lord.”

According to ancient records, the Myriad Arts Daoist Lord learned the Tree-Planting Mantra in his youth, spending only an hour to master what would have taken others days or even months. After the willow seed was planted, it rooted itself to the ground and grew into a sturdy tree that flowered and fruited. For a while, it became a celebrated tale, and its reputation resonated throughout the ages, the story being passed down even to this day.

Tao Yaoye compared the Myriad Arts Daoist Lord to Lu Yang and felt that Lu Yang still had the upper edge. After all, although both of them took an hour to comprehend the Dao and rapidly grew a tree that flowered, Lu Yang had used the Earth Escape Spell to plant the seed and the tree had fruited two Lu Yang instead.

“Senior Brother Lu is still more impressive,” Tao Yaoye mumbled to herself.

Two people were hanging from the tree, and both were Lu Yang. One was Lu Yang’s original form, while the other Lu Yang wore clothes woven from willow leaves at the expense of a completely leafless willow tree; all the leaves had been depleted for the decency of Lu Yang’s clone.

“Which step went wrong?” Lu Yang persistently searched for the crux of the problem.

However, the result was no different from before—he couldn’t figure out the reason.

“Lu Yang, you’ve become a vegetative person!”[1] the Everlasting Immortal Fairy gloated loudly.

“Shut up.” Lu Yang’s face was stormy. “Forget it, let’s get down first.”

Lu Yang wriggled his body and confirmed that nothing would be affected. Then, he severed the willow branch behind his neck and landed on the ground with a grunt.

He looked at his clone and attempted to use his mental power to control the other party. To his surprise, his clone’s fingers did move.

Under Lu Yang’s control, the “vegetative person” also cut off the willow branch behind his neck and landed successfully.

Once both Lu Yangs detached themselves from the willow tree, it swiftly withered, shrinking back to a willow seed, devoid of vitality and unable to germinate anymore.

Lu Yang tried manipulating his clone’s movement and gradually got used to it with practice. Eventually, he could multitask, moving about himself while controlling his clone.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy tried to claim credit. “Hehe, this is all thanks to me! You can control the clone because you have opened up your mental space, resulting in your mental power being much stronger than other Foundation Establishment cultivators. Now, think back, how did you open your mental space in the first place?”

Lu Yang pondered for a bit and replied earnestly, “It’s because you tried to take over my body and forced your way in, which opened my mental space.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s face darkened as she stressed, “It was fake. I’ve told you, I was faking it!”

Judging by the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s intelligence quotient, Lu Yang now believed that she was indeed putting on an act back then.

Lu Yang continued to explore the limits of his clone. It could only move within a twenty-meter radius. Beyond that, he could no longer sense the presence of his clone. In other words, twenty meters was the range of Lu Yang’s mental power.

However, within this twenty-meter radius, only the first ten meters allowed precise control. Between ten to twenty meters, his control would diminish the further the distance was.

Lu Yang’s clone was also not sturdy enough, just like willow wood.

“Is it because willow wood is an ordinary item? That’s why it isn’t very sturdy?”

Lu Yang wanted to give it another attempt with a real spirit plant. However, he hadn’t collected any tree seeds prior to this, so he had nothing suitable.

“Senior Brother Lu, why don’t you try with this peach tree seed? It’s not an ordinary item.” Tao Yaoye noticed Lu Yang’s struggle and kindly handed him another seed.

She observed Lu Yang in excitement. She loved exploring new things and unsolved mysteries, and the most intriguing mystery of them all thus far was Lu Yang.

“That wouldn’t be appropriate. How many contribution points is it? I’ll buy it.” Becoming a spy in the diabolic creed had rewarded Lu Yang with plenty of contribution points, and he still hadn’t finished spending them.

“No need. This peach seed is from Spotless Peak, so it’s free.”

Lu Yang decided to keep Tao Yaoye’s kindhearted gesture in mind and attempted to plant the peach tree. He buried the peach seed in the soil and activated the Tree-Planting Mantra, but nothing happened. He wondered, “Could it be that it requires the Shrinking Earth spell?” I had used Shrinking Earth when I planted the willow seed.

“Shrinking Earth.” Lu Yang shrank into the earth again and activated the Tree-Planting Mantra.

This time, it worked.

Right before Tao Yaoye, a sturdy peach tree burst forth from the soil, producing two Lu Yangs from its branches; one was the real Lu Yang, while the other was the “vegetative person” Lu Yang with a pink blush applied to his cheeks.

Lu Yang’s eyes twitched. “Why does this peach tree even come with dye? Never mind, as long as it works.”

As Lu Yang controlled his clone’s movements, joy surged through him. He could sense that his clone’s physical strength had improved, now achieving seventy to eighty percent of his own. This is already very impressive.

Just imagine! When I use the Tree-Planting Mantra in battle, it will produce two of me, with the other me bearing seventy to eighty percent of my strength while also coordinating with me seamlessly. My combat power will instantly soar, catching my enemies off guard.

Tao Yaoye also had the same line of thought and admired Lu Yang. The Myriad Arts Daoist Lord was a genius, but he simply followed the tried-and-tested methods of predecessors without innovation. But look at Senior Brother Lu! He forcibly transformed it into an offensive spell with formidable power!

Right then, Sixth Elder watched Lu Yang quietly from the sky and turned to leave. She was originally concerned that Tao Yaoye might not be able to answer some of Lu Yang’s queries, so she thought that she could step in to help fulfill her responsibility as an elder. But from the looks of it now, I should just leave this task to Little Yun and not overstep my role.

“Little Yun said that Lu Yang’s talent in spells is adequate to establish his own sect...” Sixth Elder was skeptical. It’s true that his talent is sublime, but can disciples actually learn anything from him if he starts a sect?

Lu Yang was engrossed in his training, becoming increasingly proficient in manipulating the clone. On the other hand, Tao Yaoye observed from the side, gaining a deeper understanding of the Tree-Planting Mantra—naturally, the normal Tree-Planting Mantra.

As the sky gradually turned dark, Lu Yang felt it would be inconvenient for him to linger on Spotless Peak, so he bid goodbye to Tao Yaoye before heading to the Great Mission Hall to exchange for some items. I can’t always use Tao Yaoye’s seeds. I have to buy my own supply as a backup.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy put up both hands in approval. I can finally indulge in a shopping spree!

~~~

After Lu Yang left, Tao Yaoye’s expression changed. She felt an inexplicable pressure that was suffocating.

Danger!

She turned her head helplessly and transmitted an auditory message to her master. “Shifu, when you come over, could you please let me know beforehand? It’s really hard for me to hold my breath every time.”

Sixth Elder stood behind Tao Yaoye with an innocent expression. “I forgot that you are not at the Golden Core Stage yet.” Sixth Elder had subconsciously assumed that all her disciples were at the Golden Core Stage.

Tao Yaoye, “...”

Is this retribution? I teased Senior Brother Lu for his low cultivation in the morning, and now it’s my turn.

Sixth Elder didn’t forget her purpose for coming. “Do you have feelings for Lu Yang?”

Tao Yaoye’s cheeks flushed red. Although she usually appeared easygoing, she was unwilling to discuss this topic with her, regardless of her feelings. “Shifu, what are you talking about? Senior Brother Lu and I have a normal relationship.”

Sixth Elder continued, “Recently, Hongxia keeps asking me what kind of person Lu Yang is. I suspect that she has heard about how outstanding Lu Yang is and wants to introduce her disciple to Lu Yang. You have to be careful if you have feelings for him.” Sixth Elder looked confident, convinced that her guess was spot on.

Luo Hongxia was the palace leader of the Moon Laurel Celestial Palace.

Tao Yaoye rolled her eyes and made no comment.

In the eyes of outsiders, it might be an odd scene of a master and disciple staring at each other in silence. However, if one looked at it from another perspective, it could also be interpreted as the master and disciple sharing a deep connection that needed no words.

1. In Chinese, the term for “plant” is combined with the character for “person” to refer to someone in a vegetative state. ☜

Chapter 154: Huang Doudou Goes Shopping

By the time Lu Yang arrived at the Great Mission Hall, it was already late at night, with only a few people left in the massive hall. From what Lu Yang understood, his senior brothers and sisters had a regular work and rest schedule. They would work hard to complete their missions in the day, slaying demons and devils and safeguarding the righteous path. At night, they would either unwind and have fun or sit down to meditate.

However, “unwinding and having fun” here didn’t have the conventional meaning of drinking and partying but rather making merry while sparring with one another, not neglecting both their rest and cultivation.

Lu Yang scrolled through the rewards list and chose the spirit tree seeds that were of a decent grade but not expensive. “Photinia tree, pomegranate tree, apple tree...” Lu Yang wasn’t very satisfied with the selection of seeds. Although the quality and price were acceptable, they lacked a certain flair.

“Why still bother looking at the price? You can spend my contribution points however you like!” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was as generous as ever. She had just compared her contribution points to the price list and was in high spirits. This mere Dao-Seeking Sect is nothing special.

Lu Yang didn’t have the habit of eating soft rice and living off someone else. Moreover, his conscience also wouldn’t allow him to take advantage of someone so naive.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy puffed up her cheeks as she stared at Lu Yang. Residing in Lu Yang’s mental space, she could vaguely sense some of his thoughts. For a moment just now, Lu Yang was disrespectful to an immortal!

Lu Yang continued browsing through the collection of seeds. “Coconut tree, durian tree...Bodhi tree. Bodhi tree seeds look good!” The Bodhi tree held a special meaning in Buddhism, with traces of it ubiquitous in legends. Lu Yang felt that the Bodhi tree was very fitting for his status as a genius.

“You’re the one then, Bodhi tree seed.” Lu Yang bought ten Bodhi tree seeds.

When it was the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s turn, her eyes shone at the dazzling assortment of items for redemption. She couldn’t decide what to buy.

“What about buying some natural treasures for restoring strength?” If the Everlasting Immortal Fairy could regain her peak, Lu Yang would have a solid backer. With Big Senior Sister and the Everlasting Immortal Fairy as my backers, wouldn’t I be calling the shots in the cultivation world?

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy remarked disdainfully, “What are you talking about? I am an immortal, do you understand? Immortals are the pinnacle of cultivators. How could there be so many natural treasures worthy enough to be used by me?” In other words, there was nothing on the exchange board that could help recover her strength.

“Then what about two Youth-Preservation Pills?”

“Setting aside the fact that my beauty is eternal, flawless, unblemished, and non-aging, I am only sixteen years old. Why would I need a Youth-Preservation Pill?”

Lu Yang thought to himself, Immortal Fairy, did you overstate your age? I’d believe you even if you say that you are six and that you had a growth spurt.

He gave up on offering suggestions. “You can just pick whatever you want then.”

“This blind box[1] seems pretty good! It’s only two hundred contribution points. There’s a chance to obtain precious items such as rare cultivation techniques, spells, and ten-thousand-year-old natural treasures!”

Lu Yang’s eyes twitched. Who came up with this thing? He wanted to dissuade the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, but seeing how excited she was, he reckoned it would probably be futile.

“Lu Yang, let me use your body for a bit. I’m buying fifty blind boxes!” As the Everlasting Immortal Fairy currently existed as a soul, she needed to possess Lu Yang temporarily to purchase anything directly.

Lu Yang could only sigh and lend his body to her.

She spent ten thousand contribution points without batting an eyelid. The total contribution points we earned from painstakingly infiltrating the diabolic creed only amounts to eight thousand five hundred.

Carrying fifty blind boxes in her arms, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy tottered over to a corner of the hall, where she sat down and began opening the boxes. In reality, she could have scanned the contents of the boxes with her immortal consciousness, but she felt that it would ruin the novelty and thrill, so she decided to open each one individually.

“Teddy bear, puppy plushie, lollipop, big iron pot... What’s all this nonsense? Where are the precious treasures?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy felt that she had been scammed.

Lu Yang thought to himself, I knew it would turn out like this.

Perhaps the Everlasting Immortal Fairy was lucky or the creator of the blind box had a guilty conscience, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy did manage to find something good.

“Soul-Restoration Pill: When one soul detaches from the body on the brink of death, ingesting this pill can summon the soul back and save one’s life.”

This was a life-saving pill, but it was of no use to Lu Yang and the Everlasting Immortal Fairy. Even if Lu Yang was on the verge of death and his soul wanted to leave his body, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy could simply grab him by the ankle and pull him back. As for the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, such hypothetical death scenarios didn’t exist.

“It may not be much, but let’s just take it.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy instinctively thought of stowing it away in Lu Yang’s identity jade pendant, but its ability to distinguish souls prevented her from doing so. Technically, she could forcefully open it, but there was no such need. She would just let Lu Yang help her store it when she returned his body.

“Corpse-Destroying Powder: Sprinkle this powder on a corpse, and it will dissolve into liquid. Wash it away with water, and that person will cease to exist in this world.

“Note: it can only destroy corpses at the Golden Core Stage or below.”

Lu Yang’s eyelids twitched again. He repeatedly reminded himself that the Dao-Seeking Sect was a righteous sect. The Corpse-Destroying Powder is for the purpose of defeating the enemies and eliminating potential threats. It’s only to be used as a last resort.

“Mountain and River Visualization Painting: Visualizing[2] this painting can expand one’s mental space and enhance one’s mental power.

“Author: Ji Hongwen.”

Ji Hongwen was Fourth Elder’s disciple, a Confucian cultivator adept in the Dao of Painting, and he belonged to the same cohort as Yun Zhi and Dai Bufan.

Lu Yang’s eyes sparkled. This is good stuff! My mental power has already reached the frontier of the Foundation Establishment Stage. Increasing it further will damage my mental space instead. After I reach the Advanced Foundation Establishment Stage, I’ll be able to augment my mental power.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy pouted, patting the chest with Lu Yang’s body. “What’s the point of visualizing this? It’s inefficient and not useful. When you reach the Advanced Foundation Establishment Stage, you can just visualize me. I’m a bona fide immortal fairy painting. It’ll definitely be more effective than this unknown visualization painting!

“Tight-Lipped Pills: Assuming no honey trap, ingesting this pill will ensure that you will never confess even under torture!

“Automatic Writing Array: If your elders punish you with copying scriptures and cultivation techniques, you can use this array to imitate your handwriting and help you with copying!”

Lu Yang marveled, “Looks like the senior brothers and sisters invented this array to save themselves some trouble.”

“Something’s not right!” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy noticed something unusual. “This Automatic Writing Array has a hidden trap. As soon as it is used, the elders will find out!”

Lu Yang, “...”

Good grief! Was this invented by the elders of the Dao-Seeking Sect to fish out those who harbored such intentions? I knew it! These elders may seem indolent and unhinged on the surface, but when it comes to scheming people, none of them loses out!

After opening all the blind boxes, it could be concluded that the one hundred thousand contribution points were mostly in vain. However, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy didn’t care about that. She liked the teddy bear and dog plushie and was already thinking about simulating them inside the mental space later, where she could conjure anything.

“What interesting things should I buy...” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was very extravagant with her contribution points, wanting to spend all of them at once. “You’re the one! I’ll have three of these!” She immediately decided to buy three vouchers. Just enough to spend my contribution points.

An ominous feeling brewed inside Lu Yang. What kind of vouchers are so expensive? He scrutinized those three vouchers.

Dao-Seeking Sect Leader One-Day Experience

1. A box that comes with a collectible item but the consumer doesn’t know which specific item it is unless they buy and open the box. However, it could be dangerous as some people may keep gambling and buying multiple blind boxes until they get the item they desire. ☜

2. The “visualization” here is in the context of Buddhism, where one observes something to cultivate their mind. ☜

Chapter 155: Isn’t This The Perfect Time?

The “Dao-Seeking Sect Leader One-Day Experience” voucher was the most expensive prize on the rewards board. To date, not a single disciple had accumulated enough contribution points to redeem it.

There were once five male disciples who pooled their contribution points to redeem the prize, but they ended up fighting among themselves over who should become the sect leader and became injured. After recuperating at the Pill Cauldron Peak, they found the whole incident overly embarrassing and set off to the outside world for long-term missions. Up until now, none of them had returned.

Naturally, disciples like Dai Bufan could afford it. However, due to his special status as the one overseeing the Great Mission Hall in First Elder’s stead, he wasn’t eligible.

Lu Yang tried to dissuade her with kind intentions, “Immortal Fairy, what about considering another prize?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy raised her delicate brows. “What, the Taciturn Daoist Priest can be the sect leader but I can’t?

“Let me tell you, I wielded tremendous power back in the ancient era, and countless tribes worshiped me. How difficult could managing a mere Dao-Seeking Sect be?”

“No, that’s not it. What I meant was that Big Senior Sister is currently in charge of the Dao-Seeking Sect. If you want to be the sect leader for three days, you will need her approval.”

“Can I ask for a refund now? Wait a minute, I mean, so what? As if I’d be scared of a little lass!” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy flinched a bit, but her pride as an immortal quickly got the better of her fear and imbued her with confidence.

Controlling Lu Yang’s body, she turned to head back to Heaven’s Gate Peak.

~~~

After arriving at Heaven’s Gate Peak, Lu Yang kindly reminded her, “Big Senior Sister is in the other direction. This is the direction back to my cave abode.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy frowned. “And you still call yourself her junior brother? You’re not the least bit considerate of her at all! That poor lass works so hard every day, and it’s already so late. How could we disturb her? We’ll talk about it tomorrow!”

Lu Yang thought to himself, Big Senior Sister has long transcended the three realms and five elements. What concept of day and night could she possibly have?

~~~

“Little la...Bi-Big Senior Sister, I would like to become the sect leader for three days. Please approve my request.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy submitted the application letter she had spent all night writing.

Yun Zhi was in the middle of handling the affairs of the sect, exuding an aloof aura that warned others from approaching. She glanced at Lu Yang and immediately recognized that the Everlasting Immortal Fairy was borrowing Lu Yang’s body.

She said flatly, “Senior, as one of the ancient five immortals, you are the most senior in the cultivation world. How can you address me as Big Senior Sister? You can just call me Yun Zhi.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy sized her up cautiously and confirmed that Yun Zhi’s words were not out of sarcasm or anger before saying, “Yun Zhi, I want to be the sect leader for three days. I spent all my contribution points to redeem these vouchers. The Dao-Seeking Sect is built on integrity. You cannot just go back on—”

“Sure,” Yun Zhi interrupted the Everlasting Immortal Fairy.

“Really?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was prepared to coerce Yun Zhi with the rules and was surprised that it was completely unnecessary.

“Really, you can. Rules are rules. I naturally have to abide by them. Otherwise, how can I command respect? Which days would you like to be the sect leader?”

“Let’s start from tomorrow then.”

“Alright.” Yun Zhi’s tone was still as calm as ever, but Lu Yang noticed a slight smile at the corner of her mouth.

Something is up!

Yun Zhi handed the matter she was dealing with to the Everlasting Immortal Fairy. “In that case, I’ll have to trouble you with the task of hosting the Five-Elements Sect, Senior.”

The Five-Elements Sect was one of the Five Great Immortal Sects.

“Fi-Five-Elements Sect?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy looked down at the paper Yun Zhi had passed to her. It was a greeting card from the Five-Elements Sect, stating they would visit the Dao-Seeking Sect three days later to facilitate exchanges between their members. A list of attendees was also appended. The paper underneath the greeting card was the hosting plan Yun Zhi had drafted—Yun Zhi had just written the title.

Lu Yang had long heard that it was a tradition of the Five Great Immortal Sects to pay visits to one another. Although it was called a “visit,” it was essentially a contest among the disciples. Rewards were secondary; the main point was to not be defeated and lose face.

This was one of the reasons for Yun Zhi rescuing Lu Yang from the clutches of the Taciturn Daoist Priest. She was hoping to let the new promising talent, Lu Yang, compete against the outstanding disciples of the Five-Elements Sect to gain experience.

Huang Doudou was dumbstruck. She thought she had it all planned out nicely. There isn’t much going on at the Dao-Seeking Sect, so I assumed I could just have fun and get a taste of authority for three days. I wasn’t expecting a brother sect to be visiting.

She wanted to back out. I’ve never organized something on such a big scale. The most I did in ancient times was to gather with the four other immortals and make merry together.

But immortals have an immortal’s pride to uphold! I must stand by my word!

Isn’t it just being the sect leader? How hard can it be?

“Even if anything goes wrong, Lu Yang will be the one embarrassed!”

“Hey, hey! Immortal Fairy, you just said your inner thoughts out loud!” Lu Yang protested angrily.

Lu Yang suddenly thought of another issue. “Big Senior Sister, the Immortal Fairy’s existence must be kept a secret, so how are we going to explain it to the outside world? How did I get so many contribution points to become the sect leader?”

“What's the problem? You found your shifu who has been missing for ten years. That’s a major meritorious achievement.” Yun Zhi’s tone was as dull as always, making Lu Yang unsure if she was being serious or sarcastic.

In any case, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy would be the acting sect leader from tomorrow onward for three days. Coincidentally, her last day in office would be the day the Five-Elements Sect visited.

After the Everlasting Immortal Fairy returned Lu Yang’s body, he felt a warmth at his waist. What’s going on?

It’s the branch leader’s bone tablet! When it flashes three times, it means that my handler, Tang Yunsheng, is looking for me.

The meeting place had been determined before “infiltrating” the Dao-Seeking Sect.

“Oh? Will I finally get to meet one of my devotees?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was gleeful.

Lu Yang informed Yun Zhi, and her response was straightforward. “Go meet him then. I’ll be watching from the shadows.”

That reassured Lu Yang.

~~~

At the entrance of the Dao-Seeking Sect, he met Meng Jingzhou and Man Gu, indicating that Tang Yunsheng had summoned all three of them.

Meng Jingzhou asked, “Do we go over directly?” He wanted to know Lu Yang’s opinion.

Lu Yang clasped his fists and raised them above his head. “Big Senior Sister is nearby.”

“Then that’s no problem.”

~~~

There were many towns in the vicinity of the Dao-Seeking Sect, and one of them was the meeting point Tang Yunsheng had chosen.

Tang Yunsheng was dressed in black robes and appeared mysterious, but in reality, he was extremely conspicuous in the town, as if he was afraid that others wouldn’t know he was trying to conceal his identity. A few passers-by even considered reporting him to the Dao-Seeking Sect—he looked too suspicious.

Tang Yunsheng gazed at the three of them with satisfaction. “The Dao-Seeking Sect’s merchant recruiting list has your names on it, stating that you have opened a barbeque shop in the sect. Good job! You have finally infiltrated the Dao-Seeking Sect!”

No doubt this was the fake name list Dai Bufan had arranged.

“There are finally spies from the Everlasting Creed in the Dao-Seeking Sect!” Tang Yunsheng exclaimed with overwhelming emotions, as if he had fulfilled a lifelong dream. “Even the creed leader didn’t expect things to go so smoothly!”

He then shifted his tone and sighed. “It’s a pity things haven’t been going well in the other three immortal sects.”

“What happened with the three other immortal sects?” Lu Yang asked.

“I also have no idea, but those three immortal sects suddenly became perceptive, even ferreting out every last one of our spies by borrowing the Everlasting Immortal’s name. They are so vicious that it caught us completely off guard! The three other diabolic creeds are not faring much better either. They also lost quite a few spies.”

“What should we do now?” Lu Yang was slightly anxious. As a branch leader, I am partly responsible for the capture of so many people from the Everlasting Creed.

“No worries, we have to look ahead. A temporary setback is nothing.” He tried to spur them on. “The last message from a spy in the Five-Elements Sect mentioned that they’d visit the Dao-Seeking Sect in three days. This is our opportunity!

“The creed leader said that he senses the Everlasting Immortal reviving. The rise of the Everlasting Creed is imminent. We can leverage this opportunity to stir up trouble during the exchange contest and let the Five Great Immortal Sects know that the Everlasting Creed is not a pushover!

“With the three of you as our mole, this plan is sure to succeed!”

Lu Yang and the other two nodded.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy in his mental space nodded.

Yun Zhi in the shadows also nodded.

Chapter 156: The Cautious Man Gu

When the righteous and diabolic paths could find common ground, any resistive force would become a driving force—the real person managing the Dao-Seeking Sect and the upcoming event had agreed to Tang Yunsheng’s proposal.

The plan was sure to succeed.

“What should we do? Do we reach out to the other three diabolic creeds, whip out all our carefully stored immortal treasures, raise a rebellion army, turn the Dao-Seeking Sect’s lair upside down, capture their eight elders, control the whole Dao-Seeking Sect, then sweep through the Four Great Immortal Sects and the Great Xia Dynasty, unify the Central Continent, following which we plot against the other three diabolic creeds, merge all four diabolic creeds into one single Everlasting Immortal Creed, dominate the Battle of the Great Era, ascend to immortals and ancestors, and lead a carefree life?” Lu Yang enthusiastically suggested.

As the creed leader of the Everlasting Creed, I have to keep the big picture in mind and meticulously plan every detail to chart a promising future for the Everlasting Creed.

“Hey, aren’t you just a branch leader?” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy clamored from within his mental space.

“That’s not quite right. Think about it, Immortal Fairy, between me and the current Everlasting Creed Leader, who would you choose as the creed leader?”

“I’ll choose you,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy answered without hesitation. Of course, I have to pick someone I know as the creed leader.

“You see? As the origin of our faith, you acknowledge me as the creed leader, which proves that I am the legitimate creed leader, while the current one is an imposter.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy nodded. “That makes sense. I hereby proclaim you as the creed leader of the Everlasting Creed!”

Meanwhile, Tang Yunsheng was flabbergasted by Lu Yang’s plan. This kid really dares to imagine. “No no no, it’s not that extreme. The Everlasting Creed hasn’t planned that far ahead. Besides, the operation this time only involves our creed.”

Lu Yang openly expressed his disappointment. The Everlasting Creed lacks charismatic courage.

Meng Jingzhou asked, “Then how are we going to stir things up in the Dao-Seeking Sect?”

Tang Yunsheng pondered for a moment. “We still don’t know the exact outline of the Dao-Seeking’s plan for receiving the Five-Elements Sect. However, I can roughly guess the itinerary. The first segment would definitely be the welcoming ceremony, likely involving speeches by both sect leaders, some performances, food, drinks, and all that...”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy quickly pulled out a small notebook to jot it down. I’ve been fretting over how I can plan the reception, and now, someone is delivering it right into my hands.

Good devotee! I’ll confer you as vice creed leader.

“Vice Creed Leader” Tang Yunsheng continued, “After that, it would be the contest. Both parties will send their elite disciples to compete, where they’ll determine the competition’s rules, area, and prizes.

“Lastly, there would be a closing ceremony. This will be our opportunity! After the welcoming ceremony and contest between elite disciples, the people will be exhausted and subconsciously lower their guard. At this opportune moment, if we strike together with our hidden operatives to sabotage the Dao-Seeking Sect, we’ll show the righteous path how powerful we are and amplify the might of the Everlasting Immortal!”

Lu Yang was startled. “From what I know, the eight elders of the Dao-Seeking Sect are either at the Advanced Fusion or Apex Fusion stages, with hardly any opponents at their level who can rival them. And that’s just the Dao-Seeking Sect. We haven’t even considered the experts from the Five-Elements Sect. Faced with enemies of such caliber, can we really launch an ambush successfully? Could it be that the creed leader will be personally making a move?!”

Tang Yunsheng shook his head. “The creed leader oversees the whole situation but will not be making a move personally. The organizers and executors of this plan are the two vice creed leaders and five higher-ups. They will be using the immortal treasure, the Yellow Millet Dream Pillow, to pull everyone into a dreamscape. Once that happens, we will control the dreamscape where we can play with them as we wish!”

Apart from the creed leader, the Everlasting Creed also had three vice creed leaders.

In truth, Tang Yunsheng had heard that the creed leader was severely injured and currently recuperating, which rendered him unable to handle other affairs, including the plan to ambush the Dao-Seeking Sect. However, there’s no need to tell these three something that will only undermine morale.

At that thought, Tang Yunsheng revealed a slight smirk. Once the Dao-Seeking Sect and Five-Elements Sect enter the dreamscape, they will be entirely at our mercy! Even if we can’t injure the elders and disciples with high cultivation, it’s more than enough to slaughter a batch of promising elite disciples!

“Yellow Millet Dream Pillow? Isn’t that the pillow I used for sleeping?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was surprised. This bunch of people are really my true devotees. They even have my relics in their possession.

Lu Yang was even more surprised than the Everlasting Immortal Fairy. “Immortals still need to sleep?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was displeased. “Why can’t immortals sleep? Since I’ve already cultivated to the pinnacle, sitting in meditation is not going to accumulate more power, so why can’t I enjoy some proper rest?”

Lu Yang was taken aback that he found her reasoning to actually be convincing.

Meng Jingzhou continued to ask, “Then how will the vice leaders and other higher-ups enter the Dao-Seeking Sect?”

Tang Yunsheng had already come up with a solution. “You shall inform the steward that your barbeque business will be too busy during the sects’ exchange and that you need a few temporary staff from outside to alleviate the load. I have already checked. This kind of arrangement often happened during past exchanges, so they will usually approve.

“The vice leaders and higher-ups will be carrying a type of talisman that can temporarily conceal their cultivation, and that is enough to fool the Dao-Seeking Sect!”

The trio nodded. The Everlasting Creed’s plan is really thorough.

However, a specific question suddenly struck Man Gu. “In that case, do the vice creed leaders and the rest know how to barbecue?”

Tang Yunsheng froze. I haven’t considered this. But I mustn't show that in front of these three. Hence, he nodded calmly. “Not bad, you are very thorough. However, the vice creed leaders and the rest are highly skilled. There is nothing they can’t do, and that includes barbecuing, scrubbing the plates, and washing the dishes. Your concerns are redundant.”

The four continued discussing some details, all of them related to possible scenarios during the exchange event.

Meanwhile, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy nodded repeatedly as she listened in and gained inspiration on how she could organize the event.

After watching the trio leave, Tang Yunsheng also turned and left, running for about four to six hours until he arrived at a secret base.

~~~

“Little Tang, you’re back. How did things go?” A man smiled at him. Despite his youthful appearance, he was actually old enough to be Tang Yunsheng’s ancestor.

“Vice Creed Leader Liu, I have passed on all the instructions. It looks like those three have fit in well in the Dao-Seeking Sect and have gathered a lot of useful intelligence. However, one of them called Man Gu spotted a minor loophole.”

“What is it?” Vice Creed Leader Liu frowned. We have simulated this plan for an entire night. There shouldn’t be any loopholes.

Tang Yunsheng raised his head to observe Vice Creed Leader Liu’s reaction as he cautiously said, “It seems that you and the others don’t know how to barbecue.”

Vice Creed Leader Liu flew into a rage, emanating a frightening aura. “Nonsense! With our status, are you honestly expecting us to barbecue?!”

Tang Yunsheng exhorted, “But think about it! Our base in the Dao-Seeking Sect is a barbeque shop, and we are also entering under the guise of helpers. Not being able to barbecue may very well expose us!”

Vice Creed Leader Liu calmed down and thought that Tang Yunsheng had a point, so he muttered in a low voice, “Go buy some meat, bamboo skewers, charcoal, and other barbeque supplies, then find a barbeque teacher. We will learn a bit.”

“Yes.”

After Tang Yunsheng left, the corners of Vice Creed Leader Liu’s mouth twisted into a cruel smile. “I heard that the trio’s barbeque shop in Yanjiang Commandery was a big hit. Hmph, it’s only because I’m not willing to learn. If I did take it seriously, how hard could barbecuing possibly be?”

Chapter 157: How Did the Five-Elements Sect Lose Last Time?

After the meeting with Tang Yunsheng, Yun Zhi said nothing on the way back to the Dao-Seeking Sect. Perhaps it was because she deemed it unnecessary to trouble herself over such a matter and had decided to delegate full authority to the Everlasting Immortal Fairy and Lu Yang.

Meng Jingzhou and Man Gu also didn’t ask anything. They felt that nothing could possibly go wrong with Yun Zhi bringing up the rear.

~~~

Upon returning to the Dao-Seeking Sect, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy focused on drawing out the arrangements for the reception.

“Speeches by the sect leaders during the welcoming ceremony...so troublesome. Lu Yang, do you know how to write this? If you can help me, I’ll teach you an immortal spell.” Sensing a headache coming on, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy sought assistance from her capable assistant, Lu Yang.

Lu Yang chuckled awkwardly. “You can forget it if you want to teach me the culinary compendium.”

“Brat, watch your words! What’s wrong with my cooking skills?!”

Lu Yang simply rolled his eyes, expressing his firm stance on this matter.

Out of options, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy would only hunker down and write it herself. After expending much effort and time, she forced herself to come up with two lines. “We would like to warmly welcome the Five-Elements Sect. Everyone is free to move around.”

Lu Yang acquiesced, “...Never mind, I’ll help you write it.” He was compelled to help; otherwise, he would be the one embarrassed when the time came.

“Really?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s eyes twinkled. She handed the matter of the speech over to Lu Yang, while she shifted her attention to ideas on what food to serve.

“This is my first time organizing such a large event, so it needs to be more grand! To show how much I value this event, I shall personally cook the meals!” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was imbued with fighting spirit. My culinary skills are comparable to a Transcendent Tribulation spirit chef, so I, Huang Doudou, have to demonstrate it to the world!

The bar was extremely low for Lu Yang. He only prayed that her skills wouldn’t be comparable to a Transcendent Tribulation poison cultivator.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy even designed a proposal to deal with the Everlasting Creed. “As my followers, it’s one thing if they don’t help me, but they still dare to cause trouble! None of them will escape!”

After working hard the whole day, they finally drafted the event proposal for Yun Zhi to review.

~~~

Yun Zhi didn’t raise any objections, simply commenting that it was acceptable. “From today onward, Senior, you will be the acting sect leader of the Dao-Seeking Sect. I have informed the eight elders, and they have agreed to cooperate with Lu Yang’s work.”

After all, the elders were not aware of the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s existence.

And thus, Lu Yang summoned the eight elders to discuss the flow of the welcoming ceremony.

~~~

“Am I the sect leader or is she the sect leader?” Lu Yang felt that he had also put in considerable work.

“What is there to be dissatisfied about? If it weren’t for me, would you even have the chance to redeem the “Dao-Seeking Sect Leader One-Day Experience” vouchers? I am benevolent to bestow you with a fortuitous opportunity, I mean, an immortal opportunity!

“In ancient times, everyone wanted to be a leader. The other immortals controlled at least tens of thousands of stars, and this doesn’t even include the mineral stars, gravity stars, dead stars, and other stars with various uses! They fought violently in their quest to conquer more stars, and I had to mediate the dispute several times!”

“So how many life stars did you control?”

“One.”

“...And why did you only have one?”

“I’m just not good at managing people. It was only because the other four immortals told me that it was embarrassing for immortals not to have their own territory and forcefully gave me a star. Only then did I reluctantly accept it.

“After receiving the star, I found a cultivator with strong management skills to oversee the star. I would just head to the mortal realm occasionally to check on how it’s doing.”

Lu Yang asked, “So what did you do after becoming an immortal?”

“Shopping, visiting friends, cooking, and sleeping,” she listed.

“So are you human or a lazy salted fish[1] demon spirit?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was unhappy. “Have you ever seen such a beautiful salted fish demon spirit?!”

“I have now,” Lu Yang muttered.

“I also often follow the four of them secretly to keep an eye on their actions and scope of activities.”

Lu Yang thought to himself, It finally feels somewhat like the ancient Great Era. Is she trying to ambush them to reduce the number of immortals?

He asked, “What were you planning to do?”

“I was trying to avoid running into them. For instance, when I attended auctions, some arrogant and ignorant person would brag about being the son of some tribe chief and claim that competing with him would be a form of disrespect to his tribe. At that moment, I’d stand up and reveal my identity as an immortal, scaring him until he trembles like a leaf.

“Alternatively, two tribes might be in conflict, and I would step in to mediate. Since both parties don’t know me, they would point at me in contempt and say, ‘Who do you think you are?’ Then, I would release my aura waves as an immortal, and it would work wonders. Both sides invited me to their tribes as a guest.

“Perhaps someone could also have provoked me and I had sent them flying with a palm strike. He would find his backer, and his backer would find an army to surround me. At this moment, their ancestor would recognize my identity and exclaim, ‘You...you are the Everlasting Immortal Fairy!’ Then, he would fall to his knees with a thud and beseech me for my forgiveness.

“Based on my experience, in such cases, having only one immortal present would have the best effect.”

Lu Yang’s eyelids twitched. The Immortal Fairy’s life as an immortal is really enriching and exciting. She can’t be a salted fish demon spirit.

While the two were speaking, the eight elders had walked in one after another. Lu Yang paid particular attention to Eighth Elder; this was his first time meeting him.

“We pay our respects to the acting sect leader.” The eight elders bowed.

“Come on, let me preside over the meeting!” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy shoved Lu Yang to one side and occupied his body.

This is precisely the reason I wanted to be the sect leader! It’s because of exciting moments like this!

“Dear subjects, please rise,” she announced.

Lu Yang wanted to cover his face. I shouldn’t have called out the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s real name back then. I had thought that the Everlasting Immortal Fairy would be a golden finger and my cheat, but now, I’ve realized that the things she does best are recounting embarrassing stories from ancient times and embarrassing me.

The eight elders were somewhat unaccustomed to Lu Yang’s current demeanor. However, once they remembered that he was the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s disciple, all the dots seemed to be connected.

“Acting sect leader, let me pour you some tea.” A cold and familiar voice from behind frightened the Everlasting Immortal Fairy such that she broke out in a cold sweat.

Yun Zhi carried a teapot and poured some tea, her posture impeccable and making everyone marvel at how she was perfect in everything she did. When she bent down, she cast a cold glance at the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, who hurriedly nodded to acknowledge that she would behave and not stir up any trouble.

The whole exchange didn’t even require them to use their spiritual consciousness; only their eyes were enough.

With the Everlasting Immortal Fairy now obedient, she cleared her throat and said, “As all of you should already know, the Five-Elements Sect will be visiting our sect the day after tomorrow. I have summoned everyone here for this reason. What are your thoughts on this matter?”

First Elder was the most composed. “Visitors with hostile intentions.”

“Why do you say that?”

“The Five-Elements Sect has already visited us once. According to customs, we should be visiting them in return, yet they went against the customs to come knocking on our door again. There is only one explanation. They want to wash away their past humiliation and defeat us on our home turf!”

This was something the Everlasting Immortal Fairy hadn’t considered. “In that case, what does everyone think we should do?”

Second Elder made a gesture across his throat. “We can ambush them on the road, cover their heads, and give them a beating so that they voluntarily back out! Don’t worry, I have experience. I leave no loose ends, so they can’t trace it back to me.”

The other elders nodded in agreement.

“I have long found the Five-Elements Sect an eyesore. After they lost the previous time, they even claimed that the Dao-Seeking Sect was not part of the five elements! What nonsense is that!”

“Take them down! Show them who’s boss! Let them see how powerful the Dao-Seeking Sect is!”

“That brat Old Qiu has changed ever since he became the sect leader. I reckon he’s forgotten the consequences of provoking the Dao-Seeking Nine when he was young!”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was intrigued. “How did the Five-Elements Sect lose last time?”

Eighth Elder replied, “Oh, it’s very simple. The last time they came over, they said that elders cannot intervene in the contest between disciples. They suggested having a match between the best disciples of both sects.”

“And then?”

“And then Little Yun stepped forth.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy immediately turned to look at the expressionless Yun Zhi. I almost forgot that you are also considered a disciple.

First Elder sighed, “Perhaps Little Yun was so strong that Old Qiu forgot she isn’t from our generation but Old Nine’s disciple.”

1. The slang xianyu or “salted fish” refers to someone lazy. ☜

Chapter 158: The Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s Golden Finger Cheat

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy pitied the Five-Elements Sect’s defeat, considering how unjust the battle was for them. No one knew the extent of Yun Zhi’s capabilities better than her. Even when I have fully regained my strength, Yun Zhi is still qualified to be my opponent, and the outcome might very well be fifty-fifty.

You sent someone like that to contest against the Five-Elements Sect? Isn’t that no different from thrashing your own grandson? I’ll be surprised if the Five-Elements Sect can take that lying down.

Lu Yang thought to himself, Immortal Fairy, please stop boasting. If you were so capable, with the Heaven Mandate Immortal and the Nine-Layers Immortal qualified to be your opponents, how did you die back then?

As the Everlasting Immortal Fairy was reveling in the feeling of being the sect leader, she didn’t notice Lu Yang’s expression.

She tried to assuage everyone’s mood. “It’s said that the Five Great Immortal Sects have a close-knit relationship like hands and legs. I feel that we don’t have to treat the Five-Elements Sect so harshly.”

Second Elder sneered. “Right, we are the hands, and the Five-Elements Sect is the legs. The hands and legs are not connected, so where is this close-knit relationship?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy discreetly asked Sixth Elder, Feng Ya. “Does Second Elder have some sort of grudge with the Five-Elements Sect?”

As Sixth Elder had appeared as just a projection, there was no need to hold one’s breath when communicating with her through the mind.

She contemplated for a bit and reckoned that although it was a private matter, she saw no reason to hide it from the acting sect leader. “When Second Senior Brother was young, he liked a woman called Shangguan Yu and even confessed to her. However, she rejected him outright.

“Subsequently, he happened to catch sight of Shangguan Yu and Qiu Jin’an whispering to each other in an intimate manner, looking like they were making a lifelong vow to be together. From then on, Second Senior Brother has found the Five-Elements Sect distasteful.”

Qiu Jin’an was the current sect leader of the Five-Elements Sect.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy knitted her brow. Something like this is indeed tricky to handle. She cleared her throat and said, “Since we are still the hosts and the Five-Elements Sect our guests, we should still observe the relevant etiquette and protocol. I have drafted a basic event proposal, and I would require everyone’s cooperation.

“The welcoming ceremony will be held in the Martial Plaza. It’s spacious, allows room for standing, and is close to our mountain peaks.”

The core area of the Dao-Seeking Sect consisted of nine mountain peaks, one for the sect leader and one for each of the eight elders. These nine peaks were positioned in the shape of a lotus, with the center being the most bustling place. It housed large businesses such as restaurants, bookstores, and clothing stores for the disciples’ recreation. There were also trial grounds and puppet arenas for disciples to train their physical form, and the biggest of them all was the Martial Plaza.

The Martial Plaza was primarily used for sparring among disciples. Its entire platform had been refined such that it was sturdy and indestructible. Furthermore, it was shielded by layers of arrays, preventing damage from intense collisions. Even if it were damaged, it could repair itself automatically. The array also ensured that the duels between disciples wouldn’t affect bystanders. This place was practically perfect.

“Fourth Elder, you are the most attentive and have an understanding of arrays. Please check the arrays at the Martial Plaza for any loopholes or gaps and whether they can withstand the force from continuous high-intensity collisions.”

“Understood.”

“After both parties have delivered their speeches, it should be around noon. It would be a great chance to bond over a meal. I happened to acquire an immortal’s personal journal which records rare methods of preparing meals. I will be leveraging this opportunity to demonstrate it to everyone.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy took it upon herself to undertake the task of cooking.

“Next would be the sparring segment. My initial plan is to carry it out according to cultivation stages: the Foundation Establishment, Golden Core, Nascent Soul, and Divine Transfiguration stages.”

The division was very reasonable; at the very least, the bloody history of Yun Zhi dominating the arena wouldn’t repeat itself.

“First Elder, with the Five-Elements Sect visiting, places like restaurants may observe an increase in customer traffic, leading to potential price gouging. When the time comes, please assign people to patrol these venues to prevent such incidents from occurring.

“In addition, some disciples like gambling and may use this opportunity to set up underground casinos. First Elder, please also keep an eye on that. Shut down any illegal operations and mete out punishments as necessary.

“Third Elder, during the exchange, there will be a large flow of people, and conflicts will inevitably arise. You will need to send some disciples to maintain order on-site.

“Fifth Elder, please craft four wooden boards to broadcast the contest at the Martial Plaza in real-time so that everyone can watch it.”

The elders nodded, finding the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s arrangements reasonable and thorough. The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was able to delegate the tasks orderly because of her entire night’s efforts—mostly spent pleading Lu Yang to lend a helping hand.

Lu Yang had no choice but to act as the temporary acting sect leader’s external brain, providing her ideas and advice. He was truly Huang Doudou’s golden finger cheat, offering her timely assistance at critical junctures.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy continued assigning the tasks. “Seventh Elder, please concoct more pills, mainly those for saving lives, healing injuries, and detoxification.”

Seventh Elder hesitated for a bit before nodding. “Certainly, but disciples typically show restraint in their duels, so such pills may not come in handy.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy also agreed, so she asked Lu Yang within the mental space. “Why did you ask him to concoct those pills?”

“Because I’m worried about food poisoning.”

She let out an “oh” before withdrawing her consciousness from the mental space, and she repeated it to the Seventh Elder, “I’m worried about food poisoning...wait...” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy caught on and glared at Lu Yang, who shrugged innocently.

“After the exchange between disciples, according to plan, the Everlasting Creed will ambush us.”

The elders were stunned. What do you mean by “according to plan?” Are you the one setting the plan?

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy put on a solemn expression. “We have planted a mole within the Everlasting Creed, someone with a rather high position who knows part of their plans.”

Lu Yang remarked to himself, Yeah right, the mole has already become their faith.

“According to reliable sources, the Everlasting Creed will dispatch two vice creed leaders and five higher-ups.”

Although the vice creed leaders were at the Fusion Stage, they wouldn’t be able to stir up trouble in the Dao-Seeking Sect without immortal treasures. As for the Fusion cultivators of the Dao-Seeking Sect, they naturally didn’t consist of only the sect leader and eight elders. The Dao-Seeking Nine were the nine most outstanding people in that generation—it didn’t mean there were only nine people in their generation. The rest were either away on missions or guarding treasure grounds somewhere within the Dao-Seeking Sect; some were also uninterested in working and in a semi-retired state, rarely showing up.

“When the time comes, I will arrange for someone to monitor the Everlasting Creed. If someone shouts “take action,” all of us will take action together and seize them. Try to take it easy and capture them alive,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy added.

~~~

After the meeting ended, the elders went about their own tasks.

On the other hand, Lu Yang left the Dao-Seeking Sect with the event plan and met with Tang Yunsheng again.

“Inspecting Officer Tang, I have brought the Dao-Seeking Sect’s event plan with me. This is all public information, so it’s very easy to obtain.”

Tang Yunsheng was overjoyed. However, he looked slightly puzzled after browsing through the event plan. “Why does it seem so similar to the event plan I imagined?”

“This just means that you are on point with your predictions!”

Tang Yunsheng didn’t think much of it and assumed it was purely a coincidence.

Lu Yang continued, “I think that we should decide on a signal for our operation. For instance, the vice creed leader could shout ‘take action,’ then all of us can act together, catching the Dao-Seeking Sect off guard!”

Tang Yunsheng nodded, approving Lu Yang’s suggestion.

Chapter 159: Finally Found the One Who Sold the Fake Exam Questions Back Then

After Lu Yang returned to the sect, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy occupied his body again to handle the affairs of the sect. There was no lack of matters to deal with in the sect every day, but the Five-Elements Sect’s visit took precedence. Now that the tasks had been assigned, it was time to address the normal issues.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy sat on the sect leader’s seat, her heart filled with elation. “Let me see what matters require my decision.

“The Great Xia Dynasty has strongly condemned the Dao-Seeking Sect for building tombs anywhere they wish. First Elder of the Dao-Seeking Sect has built tombs outside the grounds of the sect numerous times, disrupting the archaeological work of the Great Xia Dynasty.”

An elaborate explanation followed, mentioning that an old farmer accidentally discovered a tomb. Subsequently, the court dispatched personnel to investigate. They thought that the tomb’s design and structure were reminiscent of the Great Yu Dynasty and that a Fusion cultivator had built it.

Along with constant archaeological efforts, the major discovery of items in the tomb revolutionized people’s perceptions of them. After extensive excavation, the Great Xia Dynasty finally unearthed the tomb—that was when they saw First Elder sleeping right inside the coffin.

In spite of all that effort, it was just a tomb that replicated the design from the Great Yu Dynasty, illegally built by First Elder. It infuriated the Great Xia Dynasty so much that their noses almost went askew.

“The husband-and-wife earthworm pair in the herb garden have divided themselves into two, and the resulting four earthworms each believe they are independent entities that shouldn't be tied down by their original relationship, so they want to get married at the same time. The males will be the husband and concubinus, while the females will be the wife and the concubine.[1] All four of them plan to hold a grand wedding ceremony in the herb garden.”

Gasp! The Everlasting Immortal Fairy leaned backward. Are all the earthworms now like this? They really know how to play! The earthworm tribe from ancient times never engaged in such things.

She cast aside the matter of the earthworms for the time being and read the other documents. “The Blue-Eyed Water Buffalo Tribe states that since the world is a perilous place nowadays, they may run into vicious people when returning home to visit their relatives. Therefore, they propose the invention of a ‘Third Elder Strength Pill’ so that they can summon Third Elder in critical moments to resolve the danger.”

Next one.

“The sect disciples are jointly recommending for Third Elder's actions to be restricted. Mountain peaks have owners, and he shouldn't move the peaks as he wishes just for exercise.”

Lu Yang had heard of this before. Third Elder liked to move mountains when tempering his body. One could turn a blind eye to him moving the mountains around, but the problem was that he would forget the original position of the peaks. Numerous disciples returned to the sect upon the completion of their missions, only to find their homes gone.

“Hmm? The Pill Cauldron Peak claims that they have discovered a method for long-distance communication.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy looked like she had chanced upon a treasure. I didn't expect them to possess such innovative prowess. In ancient times, only cultivation experts had the means to communicate regardless of distance, yet the Pill Cauldron Peak has already found a way to make it accessible to the masses?

The Pill Cauldron Peak had outlined the proposal they had in mind. “First, concoct two Lovesick Moon Pills.”

Lu Yang recalled that the ginseng doll had briefly introduced this item to him before. The Lovesick Moon Pill could allow a pair of lovers to overcome space and time to communicate with each other.

“Then, concoct two Gut-Wrenching Heartbreak Pills, which can force two people to fall in love with each other. When both people ingest the Gut-Wrenching Heartbreak Pill and the Lovesick Moon Pill, they will be able to communicate with each other across long distances.

“After they have finished communicating, they can consume the Love-Forgetting Potion, a potion in the preliminary phase of development at the Pill Cauldron Peak. It can negate the effects of the Gut-Wrenching Heartbreak Pill.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy, “...”

Lu Yang could only remark, “...What a maverick genius...”

There’s a reason the pill-concoction community doesn’t acknowledge the Pill Cauldron Peak. With how unbridled you are with your research methods, they would be the mavericks for recognizing you!

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy wrote a uniform directive for all these issues: Reviewed.

“...And what’s your response?” Lu Yang grumbled.

“Well, I don’t know how to solve them.” A troubled expression plagued the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s visage. I’ve never been adept at solving problems, much less solving the Dao-Seeking Sect’s problems.

She had a different perspective. “Think about it. These issues aren’t very urgent. Once the three days have passed, it will be that lass Yun Zhi handling these problems again. I won’t have to worry about them anymore.”

Lu Yang found that the Everlasting Immortal Fairy did make a teeny bit of sense. “Immortal Fairy, are you forgetting one thing?”

“What?”

“Big Senior Sister has been standing behind us all this while.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy broke out in cold sweat. She felt as if a pair of frosty eyes bore into her, and she didn’t dare to turn around.

“Sect Leader, Meng Jingzhou is outside the door; he has something to report!” The owner of those frosty eyes said without a trace of emotion.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy shuddered, but she was slightly reassured upon remembering that she was now the sect leader. “Let him in.”

Then, she saw Meng Jingzhou furiously dragging someone in—it was none other than Eighth Elder.
