Lu Yang quickly regained control of his body and propped up his legs. “Ah, it’s Little Meng.” He said in an affable manner, “Little Meng, don’t be afraid. Whatever problems you have met with, you can tell them all to me. As your elder, it’s only right to help out my junior.”

Meng Jingzhou’s eyes twitched. Lu Yang, you rascal! You’ve grown quite the guts. Just wait until I redeem the Sect Leader One-Day Experience voucher someday.

He had heard that Lu Yang could exchange for the voucher to become sect leader because he had found the Taciturn Daoist Priest, who had been missing for ten years. Since Lu Yang could do that, I can also seal the Taciturn Daoist Priest to prevent him from causing trouble in the outside world. Ridding the cultivation world of one scourge should earn me an enormous number of contribution points. However, it’s now not the time to bicker with Little Lu.

“I want to report Eighth Elder,” Meng Jingzhou declared with conviction as he demanded justice.

Eighth Elder tried to defend himself, thinking that Meng Jingzhou had some misunderstanding toward him. “Dear nephew, this is all a misunderstanding. I didn’t know it was you back then.”

“What’s wrong with Eighth Elder?” Lu Yang wasn’t very familiar with him.

“Do you still remember when we first met, I said that I had bought the Dao-Seeking Sect’s real exam questions?”

Lu Yang nodded; the matter left a deep impression. When I first got onto the carriage, Meng Jingzhou didn’t divulge that he had obtained the real questions. However, when Big Senior Sister boarded the carriage later, he was completely smitten and practically dug his own grave by admitting that he had gotten his hands on the real exam questions. We even discussed how to pass the tests right in front of Big Senior Sister. It was fortunate that she didn’t hold it against us.

Oh, that’s because we eventually learned that Meng Jingzhou did get the real questions, but they were from twenty years ago.

Meng Jingzhou pointed at Eighth Elder. “It was him! Back then, he patted his chest and swore that these were real questions, swindling me out of so many spirit stones!”

In an instant, Big Senior Sister, Lu Yang, and Meng Jingzhou had their eyes drilling holes into Eighth Elder.

Yun Zhi had long known about Eighth Elder’s character and suspected that it was his doing, but she simply didn’t have the evidence.

Eighth Elder was unperturbed. “You can’t say that. Aren’t the questions I sold you real? Do you know how many people wanted to buy this set of real questions from me twenty years ago? But I didn’t sell it to anyone!”

Chapter 160: The Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s “Law Follows Words”

“Aren’t real questions from twenty years ago still real questions? Young man, you shouldn’t be so narrow and limited in your thinking.

“Haven’t you heard that the older an item is, the more valuable it becomes? Back when I raided tombs with Old Nine, we always chose the most ancient items. We even found a treasure that belonged to a Transcendent Tribulation giant demon from the early Great Qian Dynasty.”

Yun Zhi had heard a little about this. From what Shifu mentioned, when he and Eighth Elder went tomb raiding, they found a treasure from the early Great Qian Dynasty that could contain the water of the eight rivers. It was of such immense value that both of them fought over it on the spot.

After an appraisal, they found that it was the chamber pot of some Transcendent Tribulation giant demon.

Eighth Elder continued, “Go outside and ask around if the Dao-Seeking Sect’s real questions are priceless. You should already be thankful that I sold you the real questions. Don’t be so picky. Do you know how much risk I took just to sell this set of questions? This is all for the sake of generating income for the Dao-Seeking Sect!”

Eighth Elder spoke with so much conviction that Lu Yang nodded repeatedly. “What Eighth Elder said makes sense. In that case, let’s also issue your salary twenty years later, Eighth Elder.”

Eighth Elder got anxious. “That won’t do.”

“Don’t worry, Eighth Elder. It’s not like we aren’t issuing you your salary. It’s just delayed by twenty years. Isn't a salary given twenty years in the future still a salary? Or are you volunteering to forgo your salary because you feel that the sect is going through challenging times? If you have such noble intentions, I will definitely commend you publicly and encourage others to learn from your spirit.”

Yun Zhi said, “Eighth Elder, considering that you are Shifu’s dubious friends, as long as you return to Meng Jingzhou the spirit stones you swindled from him, I will let this matter pass.”

Eighth Elder could only pinch his nose as he begrudgingly returned his hard-earned spirit stones.

Meng Jingzhou was overjoyed to have the spirit stones back in his possession.

Suddenly, Yun Zhi said, “Meng Jingzhou, you are also in the wrong for purchasing the real questions. As long as you hand in the spirit stones for buying the real questions to the sect, I will let this matter pass.”

Meng Jingzhou was slightly dumbstruck. I thought you were on my side, Big Senior Sister...

Without a choice, Meng Jingzhou handed over the spirit stones to the sect before he could even warm them with his hands.

“Hold on, what about Lu Yang? This rascal even discussed with me how to tackle the exam questions. He clearly had malicious intentions!” Meng Jingzhou was bent on dragging Lu Yang down with him.

Lu Yang scoffed. “Go report me to the sect leader then! Since the sect leader isn’t around, you can report me to the acting sect leader. I believe that the acting sect leader is a strict and impartial person who wouldn’t take sides.”

“You motherf*cker...” Meng Jingzhou gnashed his teeth as he glared at Lu Yang. Just wait until I become the sect leader. I’ll show you then!

After Eighth Elder and Meng Jingzhou left, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy occupied Lu Yang’s body again. Staring at all the matters that needed to be handled, she finally felt that being the sect leader was not all sunshine and rainbows.

“The Heaven Mandate Immortal and the others were roughly on par with me when it came to dealing with problems. How did they control those planets?”

Yun Zhi sighed softly and reminded, “Just like how you delegated the eight elders their respective tasks, the sect leader also has the authority to command disciples. You can review the tasks and assign them to the experienced disciples.”

“Oh, right.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy realized that she could let her golden finger, Lu Yang, settle these matters.

Lu Yang inhaled two deep breaths. “Shouldn’t you be thinking that Big Senior Sister is hinting that you should let her handle these affairs?”

After going around in circles, they still had to count on the reliable Yun Zhi to solve these messy matters. Sometimes, Lu Yang would think about how lucky the Dao-Seeking Sect was to have Yun Zhi. Otherwise, this sect will be doomed sooner or later.

“I wonder how the outside world sees the Dao-Seeking Sect.”

~~~

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy watched the Martial Plaza with her hands behind her back, nodding frequently like a supervisor going to the countryside for inspection.

Near the Martial Plaza were many smaller platforms for disciples to spar. The Dao-Seeking Sect placed great emphasis on practical training through actual combat so that their disciples wouldn’t be bullied when they went outside the sect.

However, Lu Yang felt that the Dao-Seeking Sect was worrying too much.

At the moment, there were two Golden Core disciples, one male and one female, battling it out on a platform.

Lu Yang recognized the two of them. The male disciple, Luo Hai, had the Daytime Vast Sea Core, which was a first-class Golden Core. His water-type spells and techniques were sublime, and he had slain several Nascent Soul diabolic cultivators. Even among the countless talents in the Dao-Seeking Sect, he still stood out.

The female disciple was Yi Jing, who was from the Yi Family in the imperial city. Although her family was not as prestigious as Meng Jingzhou’s family, they were still a prominent ancestral clan on the Central Continent. With the experience she had amassed, she compared the Yi Family’s ancestral cultivation techniques with those in the scripture library and altered these cultivation techniques to suit herself better.

Neither of them were nondescript. Many people observed their duel from beneath the stage, hoping to gain some inspiration that would aid them in their future cultivation.

Just then, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy strutted over, attracting some people’s attention. For those not in the loop, Lu Yang was the first disciple to redeem the Sect Leader One-Day voucher, giving everyone’s morale a boost. However, most people were focused on the battle on stage and did not notice the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s presence.

“Let me demonstrate to you what it means to battle beyond one’s level!” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy told Lu Yang, who immediately had a bad premonition.

“Wait, what are you planning to...” Before Lu Yang could finish speaking, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy had taken control of Lu Yang’s body and leaped onto the stage.

The two on the stage were surprised to see the “Everlasting Immortal Fairy” on the stage as they weren’t sure what their junior male disciple was up to.

“I want to challenge the two of you.”

Luo Hai and Yi Jing froze. Then they were shocked. And then the crowd was in an uproar. Lu Yang is only at the Foundation Establishment Stage, yet he wants to challenge two Apex Golden Core cultivators?

However, Luo Hai and Yi Jing wouldn’t refuse “his” wish to challenge them.

The two stood opposite the Everlasting Immortal Fairy. “Junior Brother, you go first.”

The lips of the Everlasting Immortal Fairy curled into a slight smile. “In the name of the acting sect leader, I order you both to jump off the stage.”

Lu Yang, “...”

Luo Hai, “...”

Yi Jing, “...”

The audience, “...”

Is this how the acting sect leader’s authority is supposed to be used?

Since they had to follow the words of the acting sect leader, the two of them jumped off the arena without hesitation, effectively losing the competition.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s antics quickly piqued the interest of many disciples.

“Senior Brother Ma, hurry up and go take a look at the stage over there. I heard that Junior Brother Lu Yang has mastered Law Follows Words and defeated several Golden Core disciples. He even declared that he wants to challenge those at the Nascent Soul Stage.”

“Are you sure?” Excitement immediately spread across Ma Tianyang’s face.

Ma Tianyang was at the Apex Nascent Soul Stage and a disciple of the Artifact Refinement Peak. He was adept at using fire to forge weapons. Once, he stunned people by crafting weapons while fighting a Divine Transfiguration cultivator, where he had to forcefully rely on his constant stream of spirit treasures to defeat his opponent.

“Let’s go take a look.”

The male disciple who had instigated Ma Tianyang to head over revealed a sly smile, celebrating the success of his scheme.

Just as Ma Tianyang approached the arena, he heard the Everlasting Immortal Fairy boasting loudly, “Hahaha, I’m already invincible among Golden Core cultivators! Time for a Nascent Soul cultivator!”

At her cue, Ma Tianyang jumped onto the stage and witnessed the Everlasting Immortal’s “Law Follows Words.”

That day, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy battled beyond her level and defeated cultivators at the Golden Core, Nascent Soul, and Divine Transfiguration stages with a mere Foundation Establishment cultivation, making a name for herself.

That day, Lu Yang wished he could bury himself in the ground.

Chapter 161: The Five-Elements Sect Visits

The flying vessel of the Luodi Merchant Guild traversed through the clouds. The passengers on board were basking in sunlight on the deck, enjoying this moment of serenity.

All of a sudden, a gigantic shadow loomed over them.

They looked up in surprise and saw an exceptionally massive flying vessel above them. The Luodi Merchant Guild’s flying vessel was already extremely large, but it was as tiny as an infant in comparison to this flying vessel. The exterior of the latter was adorned with colorful gemstones that dazzled brilliantly. It was clear at one glance that the flying vessel was not any ordinary one.

“Whose flying vessel is this?” the passengers whispered among themselves, having never seen such a huge flying vessel before.

A sharp-eyed person noticed something. “Look at the emblem on the side of the flying vessel. This belongs to the Five-Elements Sect!”

“Five-Elements Sect?”

Most people had only heard of the name before but rarely saw the Five-Elements Sect traveling out of the sect, especially in such a grandiose manner.

“Could it be that some unparalleled great devil has appeared, so the Five-Elements Sect’s elders have to head over there together and eliminate the threat?”

In the cultivation world, the reputation of the Five-Elements Sect was leagues above that of the Dao-Seeking Sect.

“Judging by the direction, it seems like they’re headed for the Dao-Seeking Sect?”

“So are they going to annihilate a great devil or visit the Dao-Seeking Sect?”

~~~

“The purpose of this visit is to root out those bunch of demons and devils in the Dao-Seeking Sect and show them the power of the Five-Elements Sect!” On board the flying vessel of the Five-Elements Sect, the sect leader, Qiu Jin’an spurred the crowd on. “Last time, it was a mistake on my part. I forgot that Yun Zhi was the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s disciple and was eligible to participate in the contest. That was why we lost just a little bit!

“But this time, it will be different! I have already asked around. That brat Taciturn Daoist Priest has disappeared, and Yun Zhi has officially become the acting sect leader, so she is considered to be in the same generation as I am. That means that she is no longer eligible to participate in events restricted to disciples!

“This is an opportunity! Without the threat of Yun Zhi, a mere Dao-Seeking Sect won’t amount to anything! We have slept on firewood and tasted bitterness, enduring hardships and brushing up on ourselves all for today’s victory and for the glory of the Five-Elements Sect!”

Qiu Jin’an was bent on taking revenge this time to wipe away his past humiliation. In order to show off before the Dao-Seeking Sect, he even specifically drove the sect’s most luxurious flying vessel over.

On board the flying vessel, as each and every one of the talented disciples listened to Qiu Jin’an’s speech, their eyes ignited with the flames of battle. Handpicked by the Five-Elements Sect, each was a genius in their own right, possessing unique insights into elemental techniques. Peers were usually not their match.

Since they were young, the elders had taught them to avoid interacting with the Dao-Seeking Sect as much as possible when they left the sect for their missions. They were warned that those from the Dao-Seeking Sect were extremely tricky to deal with and couldn’t be understood through conventional means.

However, youths had their rebellious streak. Now that they finally had the chance to duel with the Dao-Seeking Sect, they were determined to shine and show the Dao-Seeking Sect what true geniuses looked like.

Among them were disciples who had also participated in the previous exchange, but only Yun Zhi had effectively participated at the time, so it wasn’t representative of the Dao-Seeking Sect’s overall strength.

A young girl with bright eyes stared at Qiu Jin’an, her gaze almost burning. She clenched her fists and shouted, “For the glory of the Five-Elements Sect!”

Her words were like a stone dropped onto the calm surface of a lake, creating a ripple effect through the disciples.

“For the glory of the Five-Elements Sect!”

“For the glory of the Five-Elements Sect!”

Qiu Jin’an’s expression shifted drastically upon noticing the young girl. “Why are you here? You’re not on the name list!”

The girl feigned anger. “Why can’t I be here? We finally got an opportunity to visit the Dao-Seeking Sect. How could you not invite me to something so fun?!”

“How can you describe visiting the Dao-Seeking Sect as ‘fun?’ The correct term is ‘dangerous!’” Qiu Jin’an corrected the girl.

Some of the younger disciples didn’t recognize the girl and secretly transmitted auditory messages to their senior male disciples. “Senior Brother, who is she?”

“I only know that her name is Shangguan Yu. She was already by the sect leader’s side before I joined the sect. There are rumors saying she was favored by the previous sect leader and is his illegitimate daughter—in other words, the sect leader’s younger half-sister. The sect leader is very indulgent toward her.”

As they were almost at the Dao-Seeking Sect, Qiu Jin’an couldn’t possibly chase Shangguan Yu back now. Moreover, it was very likely that she wouldn’t listen to him. Rather than losing face in front of everyone, I shall concede by a step instead.

In the middle of their conversations, the flying vessel arrived at the entrance of the Dao-Seeking Sect and docked to the side.

~~~

At the entrance, the acting sect leader who was the Everlasting Immortal Fairy and the eight elders had already unscrolled a banner to welcome the Five-Elements Sect.

Qiu Jin’an led everyone off the flying vessel, an almost indiscernible smile hanging at the corners of his mouth as he observed the Dao-Seeking Sect. This bunch of people have definitely never seen such a luxurious flying vessel.

First Elder stepped forward and wanted to extend his hand toward Qiu Jin’an. Just as the latter was about to shake his hand, he heard First Elder say, “Docking fee.”

First Elder had extended his hand not for a handshake but to ask for payment of fees.

Usually, when the Five Great Immortal Sects visited one another, the leader would use their own power to create mist or clouds that would dissipate upon arriving at their destination, which was a much more convenient method. It was rare to travel by a flying vessel like Qiu Jin’an had.

With such a big flying vessel docked in front of the Dao-Seeking Sect, there certainly has to be a fee. It’s not like this is a free parking or docking lot.

Qiu Jin’an said in a low voice, “I’m representing the Five-Elements Sect on this visit.”

First Elder pondered for a bit and found Qiu Jin’an’s words to be valid. “We will give you a 20% discount then.”

Qiu Jin’an inhaled a deep breath. I’m a magnanimous person. I won’t hold it against this bunch of lunatics from the Dao-Seeking Sect.

As Qiu Jin’an’s flying vessel was too huge, the docking fee was dozens of times more than that of an average flying vessel. He could feel his heart bleeding.

However, once he thought of how they would flaunt in front of the Dao-Seeking Sect later, he decided not to fuss over such minor details.

Then, Qiu Jin’an saw the people from the Dao-Seeking Sect and the horizontal banner hanging above them. With an immortal writing on this banner personally, the welcome displayed for the Five-Elements Sect could be considered grand; it was one of its kind.

Although Huang Doudou seemed eccentric and unreliable, her handwriting was beautiful. The strokes were flamboyant and bold, dancing across the banner like dragons and phoenixes, imbued with spirit and grandeur.

In fact, the words written were actually very simple—”Welcome to the Five-Elements Sect.” However, they were not based on the current writing system.

Qiu Jin’an squinted his eyes and recognized that they were ancient characters. Is the Dao-Seeking Sect flaunting their cultural richness?

Ridiculous! Don’t they know that there was a period of time when I was enthralled with the ancient era and had studied their culture in great detail?

Qiu Jin’an laughed and spoke a string of difficult and obscure words. They were actually in the language of the ancient era, which few understood.

Even if characters from the ancient era could still be traced, the pronunciation would be much harder to understand or even totally incomprehensible. After all, writings could be passed down, but pronunciations couldn’t.

This was a remnant sound he had obtained by chance in an ancient ruin. Based on the arrangement of the surrounding items and the scripts passed down, he deduced that it should be a ritual site for worshiping ancient immortals and that immortals enjoyed the ritual process.

The remnant sound was grand and ancient, so he believed that it was the praise the immortal gave to the priests after enjoying the rituals. This explained why the sound could be passed down—it belonged to an immortal. Qiu Jin’an found the phrase to be extremely apt for the current occasion.

Lu Yang quietly asked the Everlasting Immortal Fairy what Qiu Jin’an had said.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was wreathed in confusion. “His accent is so thick. I can’t quite make it out. I think he said, ‘O Great Immortal, please accept your servant’s most humble offering.’

“Could he have seen through my identity?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was a little pleased. Someone has finally recognized that I am an immortal. He has such a humble attitude, much better than Yun Zhi and Lu Yang.

I’ll confer him as the Everlasting Creed’s vice creed leader.

Qiu Jin’an noticed the crowd’s baffled expressions and nodded in satisfaction. You can’t understand what I’m saying, can you?

Chapter 162: Heaven Mandate Immortal Work

Back in those distant years, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s immortal name resonated throughout the world. As one of the five ancient immortals, everyone was aware of her existence. The ancient forebears and demon clans would often build altars with precious items and valuable artifacts as offerings to worship the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, seeking her compassion and blessings. Some tribes even regarded her as their totem, a goddess that protected the tribe, and they would organize grand ritual ceremonies yearly. For some time, she was basked in unmatched splendor.

Unfortunately, ever since her resurrection, times had changed. She became destitute, and only a dimwitted creed worshiped her, yet they didn’t even know her name and gender. With no refuge other than within Lu Yang, she had to endure both Yun Zhi’s intimidation and Lu Yang’s occasional sarcasm.

Life is really too miserable for me. Even Transcendent Tribulation cultivators deserve better treatment than this.

Now, someone has finally opened their heavenly eye and recognized my status, and they are even praying for me to accept such a gigantic flying vessel as an offering.

Look at these gemstones embedded in the vessel’s walls! Look at this colossal frame! This is how one should treat an immortal!

Inside his mental space, Lu Yang cast a sidelong glance at the Everlasting Immortal Fairy. He thought to himself, You seem to be pretty happy with your time as sect leader the past two days. A Foundation Establishment cultivator defeating a Divine Transfiguration cultivator in a split second? There has never been such a feat in history. Any genius would feel ashamed in the face of such battle achievements. It’s not an exaggeration to say that you have made history.

“Showing up is enough, yet you even brought along such a big gift.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy beamed as she replied in ancient language, extending her hand toward Qiu Jin’an for the magical treasure to control the flying vessel.

“What are you doing?” Qiu Jin’an looked at “Lu Yang,” who was smiling goofily. He was a little stumped, not understanding what was just said. All he knew was that one sentence in ancient language.

He sized Lu Yang up. Who is this person? His cultivation isn’t high, yet he seems to be a central figure based on where he is standing. In fact, he’s standing in the sect leader’s position.

Most importantly...he seems a bit effeminate?

“Didn’t you just say ‘O Great Immortal, please accept your servant’s most humble offering?’ Is the offering not the flying vessel?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was also a little stumped. You’re going back on your words just for something like this? Do you still want to be the vice creed leader?

This time, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy had spoken in the common language. Qiu Jin’an’s eyelids were twitching non-stop as he finally understood the meaning of that sentence in ancient language. I didn’t expect to encounter a cultivator well-versed in the ancient tongue.

He eyed the Everlasting Immortal Fairy suspiciously. “Do you really understand the ancient civilization?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy pondered for a bit and replied bluntly, “Better than you do.”

Qiu Jin’an found it laughable despite his anger. “Young one, don’t think that you understand the ancient civilization just because you have read a book or two. Let me test you!

“Do you know the concept of the ‘Heavenly Court’ system from ancient times? The Heavenly Court divided immortals into several ranks. Do you know what ranks there were?”

Recently, when Qiu Jin’an was exploring an ancient ruin, he accidentally came across an ancient text written by an immortal. It detailed the grandeur of the ancient era, and the “Heavenly Court” was mentioned as one of the main points.

“Are you talking about Human Immortal, Earthly Immortal, Heavenly Immortal, Supreme Golden Immortal, and Genesis Immortal? Or are you talking about Human Immortal, Earthly Immortal, Immortal King, Immortal Lord, and Immortal Emperor? The first set was fabricated by the Heaven Mandate Immortal, while the latter was fabricated by the Qilin Immortal.

“What I fabricated back then was Tier-One Immortal, Tier-Two Immortal, Tier-Three Immortal, Tier-Four Immortal, and Tier-Five Immortal.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy scratched her head. We made up quite a few versions back then. I’m not sure which one Qiu Jin’an found.

Qiu Jin’an was incensed. “Stop spouting nonsense! This is the work of an immortal! How could you say that it was fabricated?!”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was bewildered, but realization soon dawned upon her. “Is there a rule stating that immortals must speak the truth? Oh, I know! You must have seen the version by the Heaven Mandate Immortal. His version was the most comprehensive and could easily hoodwink people.

“I’m telling you, the Heaven Mandate Immortal’s words cannot be trusted. He is full of lies. Before he became an immortal, he would often lie to me, and I beat him like he was my grandson.”

Qiu Jin’an was stunned, thinking that the Everlasting Immortal Fairy was just babbling nonsense. But the ancient text I found did belong to the Heaven Mandate Immortal. “You have seen that book?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy nodded. “Of course! Apart from the Heaven Mandate Immortal, does it also mention the Hawking Immortal?”

Lu Yang wondered, Why does it sound like Stephen Hawking? Am I imagining things?

“If you don’t believe me, take that book out. I’ll tell you how to discern if it’s real.”

Qiu Jin’an pulled out the ancient text skeptically. Its name sounded very grandiose—Imprisoning Heaven.

He pointed at the cover. “Look, it’s clearly written here. ‘Heaven Mandate Immortal Work.’ It’s written by the Heaven Mandate Immortal.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy shook her head. “Didn’t you notice the small gap between ‘Mandate’ and ‘Immortal?’”

“What about it?”

“You’ve read it wrongly. You read it as ‘Heaven Mandate Immortal Work,’ but it should be read as ‘Heaven Mandate, Immortal Work,’ so this is a book by a person called ‘Heaven Mandate,’ not the Heaven Mandate Immortal.”

The elders of the Dao-Seeking Sect couldn’t hold back their laughter at Qiu Jin’an’s embarrassment.

“Hahahaha, Qiu Jin’an, I’ve told you long ago. Don’t brag all the time with your level of skill.” The elders tried to stifle their laughter, while Shangguan Yu, who was standing behind Qiu Jin’an, laughed out loud, completely disregarding his stormy face.

Shangguan Yu addressed the members of the Dao-Seeking Sect in an apologetic tone. “I’m sorry. You know what Jin’an is like. He is thick-skinned and never admits that he is wrong. It’s because he didn’t understand the original meaning in the ancient language that such a misunderstanding happened. Apologies, everyone. Please accept these gifts.”

The disciples of the Five-Elements Sect began unloading the magical treasures, ores and minerals, pills, and cultivation techniques from the vessel. Any one of these could be the highlight of an auction.

The most precious of them all was the specialty of the Five-Elements Sect, the Five-Elements Ores. They were distinguished by their colors, each corresponding to one of the five elements. Every one of them represented the pinnacle of each element, and they were highly coveted raw materials for artifact-refining masters.

At the sight of the Five-Elements Ores, Fifth Elder Zhou Xin’s eyes gleamed, like the green eyes of a wolf spotting its prey at night.

When the Five Great Immortal Sects paid each other a visit, they would always bring some gifts.

For instance, the Moon Laurel Celestial Palace would often bring the moon laurel branches and moon essence as gifts.

The Hanging Monastery would prepare Buddhist scriptures and consecrated Buddhist treasures.

The Prison Suppression Sect would offer the demons and monsters they had tamed.

As for the Dao-Seeking Sect, they were a bit special, or rather, more casual, especially when the Taciturn Daoist Priest was still around.

They once gifted the Moon Laurel Celestial Palace a top-notch physique refinement technique. When mastered, one would achieve muscles like steel, bones like iron, and skin as tough as molten iron that it couldn’t even be pinched, allowing them to sweep through all obstacles in their path.

The Moon Laurel Celestial Palace was so furious that they wanted to beat them up. How could you let a female cultivator cultivate something like this?!

On another occasion, the Dao-Seeking Sect sent the Hanging Monastery the long-lost Mouth-Shut Chan Meditation[1] cultivation technique, which the Taciturn Daoist Priest claimed to have cultivated with excellent results.

At the time, the abbot had chuckled, thinking to himself, If you bastard can master it, why would you still be called ‘Taciturn?’

With the Taciturn Daoist Priest insisting that it was authentic, the abbot of the Hanging Monastery decided to give him the benefit of the doubt and practiced it once.

Then, he found that his breath would stink like garlic every time he spoke, and the people around him would beg him to shut his mouth.

The Taciturn Daoist Priest’s explanation was: “Isn’t the Mouth-Shut Chan Meditation about others asking you to keep your mouth shut?”

The abbot was so enraged that he transformed into Acalanatha, the Immovable Vidyaraja,[2] to subdue the “evil creature” that was the Taciturn Daoist Priest.

1. Chan Buddhism is where Zen Buddhism originated from, and the same Chinese character is used, though the Japanese version has one extra stroke or dot. ☜

2. Acalanatha embodies compassion while being firm and immovable. He is portrayed as fierce, purging evil when the need arises. ☜

Chapter 163: Dao-Seeking Sect, You Are Going Too Far!

After Yun Zhi had assumed the role of acting sect leader, she visited the other four great immortal sects as per custom, bringing a very special gift along with her—she announced to them that the Taciturn Daoist Priest had gone into seclusion and that she was now in charge of the Dao-Seeking Sect.

The four other immortal sects were over the moon upon learning of the news. They finally didn’t have to deal with a lunatic. Moreover, Yun Zhi’s new position implied that she would no longer participate in the events restricted to disciples.

Every now and then, the Five Great Immortal Sects would organize activities for disciples and have them explore ancient cave domains. However, ever since Yun Zhi appeared out of nowhere, they reckoned it would be much more time-saving to hand the rewards directly to Yun Zhi.

Second Elder couldn’t shift his eyes away from Shangguan Yu, the captivating woman of his dreams. Although she had once rejected him, his memory of the pure and beautiful Shangguan Yu had left an indelible mark in his mind.

Noticing Second Elder’s fixed stares, Qiu Jin’an stepped forward and blocked his view with a stormy expression. “When does the contest start?”

First Elder replied, “According to the plan, we will begin with an opening ceremony, eat, and then it will be the contest.”

Qiu Jin’an remarked inwardly, That’s quite standard. As expected of Yun Zhi’s arrangement. She’s so much better than that bastard Taciturn Daoist Priest.

The last time he had visited the Dao-Seeking Sect, the Taciturn Daoist Priest had come up to him and immediately threw an arm over his neck, saying, “Brother, let’s go play at the brothel! My treat.”

Qiu Jin’an had shoved the Taciturn Daoist Priest away on the spot.

How could he have said something like that out loud? Shangguan Yu was still looking at him!

“Mmm? Where’s that young fellow who knows about the ancient civilization?” He was hoping to discuss some secrets from the ancient era with Lu Yang, such as how the expert who mastered Law Follows Swords died and whether the Heaven Mandate Immortal got his name because he was born on a day with sublime weather.

First Elder explained, “He went off to prepare the meals.”

“Oh.” Qiu Jin’an didn’t think much of it.

As the opening ceremony commenced, the disciples from the Dao-Seeking Sect and the Five-Elements Sect stood together and watched the higher-ups deliver their speeches.

Soon, they were dozing off.

First Elder recited his speech based on the script Lu Yang had written. “In order to implement the policy of moving forward together as the Five Great Immortal Sects, foster friendly exchanges between the Dao-Seeking Sect and Five-Elements Sect, promote the profound appreciation of the unity and camaraderie among the five sects, and build a strong foundation for mutual prosperity, I have five points I would like to expound on regarding the theme of this exchange.

“Firstly, implementing the policy of moving forward together as the Five Great Immortal Sects is both a historical necessity and a practical imperative. With the imminent arrival of the Ancient Great Era, ancient cultivators are awakening one after another. In the face of such grim challenges and unpredictable risks, the Five-Elements Sect should, and must, unite as one...”

Qiu Jin’an was flabbergasted. Although he had expected a vastly different speech this time, he didn’t expect such a prodigious disparity.

Last time, the Taciturn Daoist Priest had only said two sentences. “We would like to warmly welcome the Five-Elements Sect. Everyone is free to move around.”

When it was Qiu Jin’an’s turn to address the audience, he cleared his throat and spoke in a bright voice, “In this season where the sun shines brightly and all things are reborn, the Five-Elements Sect is very honored to be here at the Dao-Seeking Sect and witness the most advanced ideologies and theories in the cultivation world, which has been truly inspiring...”

After the leaders were done with their respective speeches, sparse and fragmented sounds of applause could be heard from the audience below, or as Eighth Elder put it, it was like “they couldn’t empty their bladder.”

On the stage, the leaders from both sides shook hands.

“Sect Leader Qiu, we will be looking forward to your guidance during this exchange.”

“You jest, First Elder. I hope the Dao-Seeking Sect will show us mercy.”

Both First Elder and Qiu Jin’an wore benign smiles on their visage, preventing bystanders from having any clues that they were secretly communicating with their spiritual consciousness.

“Qiu Jin’an, get back to the Five-Elements Sect! The Dao-Seeking Sect does not welcome you. Look at how hypocritical you are. Have you forgotten how we, the Dao-Seeking Nine, beat you up in the past?”

“Nine of you against one of me? Does the Dao-Seeking Sect not care about saving face anymore? Do you really think I care to come to your sect, the gathering place for a bunch of demons, devils, and ghosts? Just wait until I subdue demons and exterminate devils and spread my news of victory throughout the cultivation world!”

In the real world, both of them were smiling sincerely all this while.

“Sect Leader Qiu, shall we go for lunch together?”

“Haha, I’ve long heard that nothing compares to the food in the Dao-Seeking Sect. This will surely be an eye-opening experience.”

As the group made their way to the dining hall, Qiu Jin’an saw a disciple using a youtiao to hammer nails, each strike producing a resounding clang and sparks everywhere.

Then, he saw a disciple toss a jianbing into the air, where it instantly grew so big that it blocked out the sky.

He also saw a disciple preparing egg soup. The silver pot turned black and began to melt, while the egg soup condensed into a single green droplet.

In a way, it was indeed eye-opening.

Surely the Dao-Seeking Sect won’t be making me eat something like this, right? Qiu Jin’an was on tenterhooks as he tried to comfort himself that he wasn’t a sinner who deserved such punishment.

Finally, the group arrived at a luxurious restaurant. A delightful aroma assailed their nostrils even from a distance. Laid before Qiu Jin’an was a spread of dishes rich in color, fragrance, and flavor.

“Looks like I’ve wrongfully blamed the Dao-Seeking Sect.” Qiu Jin’an sighed in relief.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy donned a white apron and a tall hat, looking the part.

She introduced the dishes. “This is fermented tofu, carefully prepared from the finest loin of Ice Plains Elephants and morning dew from the herb garden. I have combined them both with an ancient secret technique for extraordinary results.” She was eager to see their reactions. “Why don’t you have a taste?”

Qiu Jin’an lifted the lid from the plate, and a golden light shot into the sky, almost blinding him as immortal music echoed in his ears ceaselessly. He turned around and saw a group of people performing a music ensemble. “What’s going on?”

“Musical performance. For the ambiance,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy explained.

Qiu Jin’an didn’t think much of it as he picked up a pair of chopsticks and grabbed a piece of tofu. Just as he was about to place it in his mouth, he saw wisps of smoke emitting from where his chopsticks touched the tofu, which was melting at an alarming rate.

Plop! The tofu fell back down.

Qiu Jin’an blinked, wondering if he was hallucinating.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy urged him by the side, “You need to eat it quickly, else the fermented tofu will soon burn through the plate and table.”

Qiu Jin’an suppressed the urge to flip the table and decided to try another dish.

He lifted the lid of a small tea bowl, revealing a milky white fish soup, garnished with two green leaves that made it look even more appetizing.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy introduced, “In our sect’s Tai Lake, there is a fish called the Blue-Water Fish that dates back to ancient times. It must be cooked immediately after it leaves the water, or it will turn bad after six hours. I fished it up from Tai Lake at dawn, and with my meticulous culinary skills, I have preserved the maximum freshness possible. Give it a try.”

Then, Qiu Jin’an saw a small green fish swimming in the soup, even leaping out and leaping back in, sending ripples across the surface of the soup. A drop of fish soup even splashed onto his face.

“...Isn’t your fish meat a bit lively?” Qiu Jin’an suppressed his urge to flip the table once again.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy explained, “The fish you saw isn’t actually alive. It’s a fish spirit crafted from the Blue-Water Fish’s skeletal frame with ancient techniques. Just poke it with a spoon and it will dissolve.”

Qiu Jin’an cautiously prodded the small green fish with a spoon, and sure enough, it dissolved into the soup, enhancing its flavor by another level.

So I did wrongfully blame him after all, Qiu Jin’an thought.

He took a small sip and immediately spat it out. “It’s so salty? How much salt did you add?!”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy gave it a serious thought. “Twenty seconds.”

Qiu Jin’an slammed the table. Shooting to his feet, he roared, “Dao-Seeking Sect, you are going too far!”

Chapter 164: Dao-Seeking Sect, Show Your Most Outstanding Disciple!

“Dao-Seeking Sect, you are going too far!” Qiu Jin’an bellowed as he flipped the table in a fit of wrath.

As the dishes smashed to the ground, the sizzling sound of the corroding floorboard filled the air, causing people’s eyes to twitch.

All this time, Qiu Jin’an had maintained the image of a refined gentleman who could hold amicable conversations with ordinary people and cultivators alike. In fact, he was genuinely someone like that. However, he felt that the Dao-Seeking Sect was his natural nemesis, capable of provoking his emotions.

In a sense, the Dao-Seeking Sect had extended Qiu Jin’an a supreme treatment that was befitting for the four ancient immortals—after all, only the four ancient immortals were fit to witness Huang Doudou’s culinary skills.

Inside his mental space, Lu Yang felt his scalp tingling. There’s a reason the four ancient immortals didn’t eat your cooking.

When the Everlasting Immortal Fairy was preparing the meals, she had blocked Lu Yang’s vision with the excuse, “This is an ancient secret. I can’t let you learn it.”

At that time, Lu Yang already had a sense of foreboding, and indeed, it had proven true.

This was just the prelude. The Everlasting Immortal Fairy had prepared eight dishes. Lu Yang didn’t dare imagine what other atrocities and monstrosities lay ahead.

But that’s not the biggest issue! The main problem is that the Everlasting Immortal Fairy has been doing all this with my face! Everyone else will think that I’m the culprit!

Her shenanigans of using the acting sect leader’s authority to wantonly challenge those above her level since two days ago have already attracted a wave of hatred toward me, and here’s another wave today.

What sins did I commit to have called out the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s true name and resurrected her?

Lu Yang felt that the karma of reviving an immortal was as heavy as a mountain that he was about to crumble beneath its weight.

The mastermind behind the scenes didn’t want to personally resurrect the Everlasting Immortal Fairy for a reason!

On the other hand, the elders of the Dao-Seeking Sect secretly let out a sigh of relief at Qiu Jin’an’s outburst, transmitting auditory messages among themselves.

“Fortunately, the Dao-Seeking Sect adhered to etiquette and let the Five-Elements eat first. Otherwise, we would have been the unlucky ones instead.”

“Little Lu is so thoughtful. Although he doesn’t bear hostility toward the Five-Elements Sect, once he heard about the enmity between us, he immediately took action and taught Qiu Jin’an a lesson. What a good kid!”

Those from the Five-Elements Sect were similarly lamenting over the matter.

“In the past, I scoffed at the idea of etiquette, finding it outdated. But from the looks of it now, I realize that the ancient people had a point. Elders should eat first.”

“The elders eat first, and if there’s no poison, we can eat. This is the wisdom of the ancients!”

“The sect leader sacrificed himself to test for poison. This is a spirit we should learn from.”

“I have long heard the sect leader mention that the Dao-Seeking Sect’s pills and poisons are exceptional. I have broadened my horizons today.”

“Others add poison to food, while they make food from poison.”

While Qiu Jin’an was eating, Second Elder showed his concern to Shangguan Yu. “Fairy Yu, it’s been a long time since we last met. You’re still as beautiful as ever.”

Shangguan Yu looked at Second Elder calmly. “Little Ba, it’s impossible between us, and neither is it meant to be. You should give up.”

Second Elder got a little anxious. “Is it because there is something wrong with me? I can change!”

Shangguan Yu shook her head wordlessly, simply moving herself a little further away from Second Elder.

Qiu Jin’an decided to discard all attempts at superficial pleasantries. “All of us have already managed to abstain from eating, so there’s no need to partake of this meal. They are all convoluted formalities. Let’s have the disciples compete directly!” He revealed the true purpose of his trip.

First Elder concurred, “That’s how it should be. We plan to divide the contest into four stages: Foundation Establishment, Golden Core, Nascent Soul, and Divine Transfiguration.”

Qiu Jin’an sneered. As I thought, the Dao-Seeking is organizing the contest by cultivation stages. This eliminates the possibility of Yun Zhi competing.

With a wave of his hand, he announced, “I only have one request. Let the best disciples of both sects compete in one decisive battle. How’s that!”

First Elder was a little hesitant, afraid that another classic scene of Yun Zhi one-sidedly crushing the Five-Elements Sect would unfold. “That may not be such a good idea. We have already planned everything. What if you lose terribly? It would be hard to save face then!”

We can’t afford to make Qiu Jin’an so angry that something happens to him. At the very least, we can’t let anything happen to him within the Dao-Seeking Sect.

First Elder’s reaction only further convinced Qiu Jin’an of his speculations. “Face? Cultivators speak with strength. A loss is a loss, and a win is a win. What face is there to speak of?!” Qiu Jin’an waved his hand, beckoning for his eldest disciple behind him to step forward.

“This is my eldest disciple, Lin Shaoyou, also the most outstanding disciple of the Five-Elements Sect. He has a wood-type Single Spirit Root and is at the Basic Fusion Stage. Most wood-type Single Spirit Root cultivators are suited for healing and recovery and not adept at combat, but that's not the case for him!

“Shaoyou has also thoroughly internalized the Five-Elements Sect’s philosophy of the mutual generation and restraint of the Five Elements, where wood generates fire, fire generates earth, and earth generates metal. He has successfully cultivated both fire- and metal-type spells, the Six Ding Divine Fire[1] and Berserk Devil Golden Body. On top of that, he also turned them into forbidden spells with immense destructive power!

“Shaoyou has balanced the continuous aura flow of a Wood Spirit Root and mastery of extreme offensive spells. His combat power is far beyond that of a Basic Fusion cultivator. Just a few days ago, he defeated the grand elder of a first-class sect whose cultivation was at the Advanced Fusion Stage!”

Lin Shaoyou’s attire resembled that of a well-read literati. With a pleasant smile and elegant demeanor, he exuded an aura of sheer confidence.

And his qualifications did back him up. Among his peers, he could hardly find a worthy opponent. His sight was already set on the previous generation and even those from two generations ago.

“Is my opponent Dai Bufan or Ji Hongwen?” In his opinion, only the two were qualified to be his opponent.

Last time, he had encountered Yun Zhi, so he didn’t get to unleash his arsenal of techniques. This time, I must showcase all of them and earn glory for Shifu!

“It’s me.” A placid voice tinged with coldness sounded, sending chills down people’s spines.

Yun Zhi stepped forward after keeping silent all this while, causing the hearts of Qiu Jin’an and his eldest disciple to stop beating momentarily.

Qiu Jin’an forced a cold laugh. “Don’t try to scare me. I’ve already heard that Yun Zhi is the acting sect leader and cannot participate in the battle. The most outstanding disciple should be either Dai Bufan or Ji Hongwen!”

Yun Zhi took out an official piece of document with black ink clearly stating that Lu Yang was the acting sect leader for three days. She pointed at Lu Yang and said, “This is the current acting sect leader. I am now just an ordinary disciple of the Dao-Seeking Sect.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy bounced up and down. “That’s right, that’s right! I am the acting sect leader now!”

Qiu Jin’an shouted furiously, “Are you joking with me? How can a Foundation Establishment cultivator be the acting sect leader?!”

First Elder shook his head. “That is not quite right. Sect Leader Lu is a genius among geniuses. Although he is only at the Foundation Establishment Stage, he can already defeat opponents beyond his level, including those at the Golden Core, Nascent Soul, and Divine Transfiguration stages!”

Everyone from the Five-Elements Sect turned their gazes to “Lu Yang” all at once. A Foundation Establishment cultivator defeating a Divine Transfiguration cultivator? That’s still as absurd as a fairy tale even with external help. It’s just impossible. Even myths don’t dare to fabricate such a stothe ry!

Despite Dao-Seeking Sect’s poor reputation, they had never lied, especially about matters like this. Qiu Jin’an’s expression grew grave, not expecting such a terrifying genius from the Dao-Seeking Sect.

Compared to this guy, all the geniuses throughout history paled in comparison!

The Dao-Seeking Sect is truly shrewd. They’ve already anticipated my move and made arrangements beforehand to let Yun Zhi fight.

Qiu Jin’an felt that he was in between a rock and a hard place. I have already talked so big. If we don’t fight, we will lose so much face!

While Qiu Jin’an was in a dilemma, Lin Shaoyou took a step forward, an action that deeply moved Qiu Jin’an. As expected of my eldest disciple. He dares to step forth at such a moment and face the pressure from Yun Zhi directly.

Lin Shaoyou inhaled a deep breath of air and adjusted his breathing and state of mind. Staring straight at Yun Zhi, he spoke in a sonorous voice, “In that case, I shall no longer be a disciple of the Five-Elements Sect!”

1. The “Six Ding and Six Jia” are deities in Daoism. ☜

Chapter 165: A Trial From The Everlasting Immortal Fairy

Lin Shaoyou was unflinching. “I feel that the Dao-Seeking Sect is a good place. The harmonious relationship between the disciples is something I look forward to. I am willing to join the Dao-Seeking Sect!”

Qiu Jin’an looked like he was about to pass out from anger. He trembled as he pointed at Lin Shaoyou, only managing to utter two words after a long while. “Rebellious disciple!”

Lin Shaoyou turned around to face his master. “Shifu, didn’t you just say that cultivators don’t care about face?”

Qiu Jin’an erupted in rage. “Come back here!”

“Oh.”

Lin Shaoyou obediently returned to his position behind Qiu Jin’an, exchanging glances as they passed each other.

“Shifu, did I act well?”

“You went a bit overboard. You need more practice.”

Qiu Jin’an coughed and gradually calmed down. “Since Shaoyou isn’t willing to participate in the contest, as elders, we can’t force him, right?”

Since Lin Shaoyou would not compete with Yun Zhi, Qiu Jin’an could naturally suggest that they proceed with the Dao-Seeking Sect’s plan.

With a valid reason, we won’t lose face.

As the eldest disciple, Lin Shaoyou often had experience taking the hit for his master.

This time, Qiu Jin’an had planned to give the Dao-Seeking Sect a beating from top to bottom, so he had deliberately brought his personal disciples all the way from the Foundation Establishment to the Divine Transfiguration stages. All of them were luminous talents confident that they were unmatched within their own cultivation realm.

“Old Two Ba, stay away from her!” Qiu Jin’an noticed that Second Elder was still persistently pestering Shangguan Yu, so he grabbed her hand and pulled her over protectively.

“Jin’an, Little Ba means no harm to me.”

Qiu Jin’an glared. “That all the more spells problem!”

Not allowing her to explain further, he led Shangguan Yu and those from the Five-Elements Sect to the Martial Plaza. He gave them a brief rundown of the entry sequence before turning toward the spectator stand.

At the moment, the disciples of the Dao-Seeking Sect were gathered around the Martial Plaza with smiles on their visages, eager to enjoy the spectacle. Lu Yang never knew that the Dao-Seeking Sect had so many disciples.

The restaurants within the Dao-Seeking Sect had managed to uncover business opportunities with this. They sold viewing spots in the restaurants or carried large crates of fruits for sale. It wouldn’t be an exaggeration to say that they were raking in buckets of gold by the day.

~~~

At the spectator stand, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy and Qiu Jin’an sat side by side, while Yun Zhi, First Elder, Shangguan Yu, and Lin Shaoyou sat on either side.

Inside the mental space, Lu Yang and the Everlasting Immortal Fairy were discussing a matter of life and death.

“Immortal Fairy, have you ever considered getting yourself killed by Big Senior Sister and then resurrecting a few hundred thousand years later?”

“Eh? Why are you so cruel to me?!” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was floored, not thinking she had done anything wrong.

“Wait a minute, are you angry because I didn’t teach you the ancient culinary skills? Let me tell you, this is what they mean by ‘techniques cannot be passed on lightly.’ You and I are not shifu and disciple. Imparting teachings is an extremely serious matter; it is not to be carried out casually!”

Lu Yang remarked inwardly, Immortal Fairy, how do you have the face to think that your culinary skills are amazing? Is it because the four ancient immortals didn’t die from your poisoning?

His expression was wreathed in pain. “Immortal Fairy, think about it. Ever since you became the acting sect leader, how much hatred have you drawn my way? I can’t withstand it even if I were made of iron!” Lu Yang could guarantee that those Golden Core, Nascent Soul, and Divine Transfiguration senior disciples, who the Everlasting Immortal Fairy had challenged, were all waiting for the day to be over so that they could teach him a lesson.

Lu Yang’s words made the Everlasting Immortal Fairy realize how much trouble her unbridled playful behavior had caused Lu Yang. However, she was reluctant to admit that it was her fault. “How could you call that drawing hatred? This is a trial from an immortal. Once you pass my test, you will receive my legacy.”

If it were the Heaven Mandate Immortal’s legacy, Lu Yang might be a little tempted, but since it was the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s legacy, Lu Yang was worried that it would lower his intelligence after learning it.

“This is an immortal’s legacy, the dreams of countless people.”

“What does your legacy comprise?” Lu Yang looked at the Everlasting Immortal Fairy suspiciously.

“There’s plenty. I shall not go into spatial spells like Shrinking Earth To Inches and Close Horizon From Cliff since you have already learned those. Apart from them, I can teach you time-related spells!”

Now, Lu Yang was tempted. Temporal spells are some of the most precious. There are hardly any of them in the Dao-Seeking Sect’s scripture library. There is something to the Everlasting Immortal Fairy after all.

“One of them is called the Play-Dead Technique. Casting this spell will make you appear like a dead person from the inside out. You can even adjust the time your corpse rots and the rate it decays. I guarantee that no one will be able to tell!

“What do you do if you can’t beat an enemy? Just play dead!” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy seemed very experienced, making one wonder how many times she had played dead.

Lu Yang suspected that he was getting converted by the Everlasting Immortal Fairy. To think that I found her very reliable for a split second then.

“There’s also the Water-Repelling Mantra which allows you to freely enter and exit lakes and seas!”

Lu Yang’s interest was piqued again. Many experts had fallen in battles, and with their bodies and relics sunk into the lakes and seas, these water bodies could be said to be natural treasure beds. If one could go down to explore, they might reap a big harvest.

“However, remember to use the Water-Repelling Mantra quickly as it has a time limit.”

“What time limit?”

“My Water-Repelling Mantra is very holistic. Not only can it repel the water around you, it can also repel the water within you. If you use it too long, you might die from dehydration.”

Lu Yang retorted, “...You can keep your legacy and let it gather dust.”

“Hey, how could you say that?!” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy stomped her foot in annoyance.

Meanwhile, on the outside, Qiu Jin’an interrupted their conversation as he asked the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, “Sect Leader Lu, you seem to know a lot about matters of the ancient. I was wondering if I could consult you regarding some questions?” He didn’t look down on Lu Yang simply because of his young age. Since he is the acting sect leader, I should treat him with the same respect in accordance with his status.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy approved of Qiu Jin’an’s attitude. “Sure, but after I answer your questions, you have to tell me where you got the book on the Heaven Mandate Immortal.”

Lu Yang could understand where the Everlasting Immortal Fairy was coming from. The book by the Heaven Mandate Immortal likely came from an ancient ruin. She probably wants to find clues about herself and the ancient era there.

“Alright.” Qiu Jin’an began, “I heard that there was an extraordinary person who didn’t die even with the head chopped off. They used their breasts as eyes and navel as their mouth.”

“Yes, there was such a person.”

“I would like to know: did he wear upper garments?” Qiu Jin’an was very intrigued by these kinds of ancient legends.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy pondered for a bit. “He didn’t wear upper garments and went bare-chested most of the time, but this caused him some problems.

“For example, some large tribes were more particular and didn’t allow those indecently dressed to enter. As he was bare-chested and looked like a wild person, he couldn’t enter. However, when he wore clothes, he would become a masked bandit, and he was still not allowed to enter, so he was trapped in a dilemma.

“Eventually, he got smarter. He attached a fake head to himself and then wore clothes. That way, people wouldn’t recognize him anymore. One day, however, he attached his head the wrong way around, frightening the people around him into thinking that his neck had been wrung and that he was a jiangshi wandering the streets.”

Chapter 166: Match Commentary

“I heard that the Heaven Mandate Immortal got his name because he was born under the mandate of Heaven. Is that true?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy waved her hand. “Aiya, that’s just him bragging. That fellow Heaven Mandate Immortal was born from a humble tribe. In ancient times, much emphasis was placed on one’s background. Even when the Heaven Mandate Immortal showed talent at a young age, people still whispered behind his back, denigrating his background and fate profile, claiming that he was just a flash in the pan and that his eventual downfall was inevitable.

“Hence, the Heaven Mandate Immortal made up the story of being born under Heaven's mandate, and it did sound quite believable.

“When the Qilin Immortal heard that he went by the name “Heaven Mandate,” he wasn’t happy about it. As Qilin was the favored child of heaven and earth, he could also be considered a son of Heaven, so he got into a conflict with the Heaven Mandate Immortal. The two even got into a fight over it.

“The Qilin Immortal disparaged the Heaven Mandate Immortal, saying that he was born from cesarean section and that his birth was not at all smooth, which implied that Heaven didn’t wish for him to exist at all.

“The Heaven Mandate Immortal retorted, calling the Qilin Immortal an unruly brat with a mother who raised him but didn’t teach him manners. Of course, in some way, the Heaven Mandate Immortal was speaking the truth.”

A strange expression stretched across Lu Yang’s face. Immortals are supposed to be noble figures, but why do the words from your mouth make them sound like petty thugs?

“No winner could be determined, so I had to step in and mediate. I told them, ‘Why are you fighting during a festival? Come eat at my place instead.’ To give me face, they instantly stopped fighting when they heard me.

“Their tussle also bloomed into a friendship. After fighting all that while, they decided that since they were born of the same mother, they might as well become sworn brothers.”

Qiu Jin’an automatically ignored the part where the Everlasting Immortal Fairy praised herself, assuming that it was nonsense, and pressed further, “Then they became sworn brothers afterward?”

“No, then they fought again, this time over who should be the elder brother.”

Qiu Jin’an, “...”

He had long heard about the dissonant relationship between the Heaven Mandate Immortal and the Qilin Immortal. They fought each other numerous times, and the reasons for their battles varied widely. However, the mainstream view was that their conflict arose from struggles over the Great Dao and Immortal Dao that originated from a vague yet profound theory of all things, which resulted in irreconcilable strife.

The ancient texts even recorded that the two clashed in the cosmos without holding back, erasing an entire region where the stars and spirit qi disappeared.

But the truth is that they fought over matters like this? Why does this account not match the splendor of the ancient era I had imagined?

While the two sect leaders exchanged knowledge on ancient affairs, the disciples from both sides began their competition.

~~~

~Match Commentary~

First up, representing the Dao-Seeking Sect is Meng Jingzhou, and facing him from the Five-Elements Sect is Du Xueyi!

Contestant Du Xueyi is not to be underestimated. According to insider information from the Five-Elements Sect, he possesses a Metal Spirit Root and a body tempered to the strength of steel through relentless training. He has even mastered the Storming Thunder Fist Technique where his indestructible iron fists swing around like the wind and pour down like the rain.

Contestant Meng Jingzhou is not to be outmatched. According to Sect Leader Lu Yang, who wasn’t willing to divulge his name, Meng Jingzhou possesses a once-in-a-century Single’s Spirit Root. Although he frequents brothels, he is a paragon of remaining unsullied despite his handicap—truly admirable!

Coincidentally, Contestant Meng Jingzhou is a physique cultivator and a disciple of the renowned physique cultivator, Third Elder. Who knows what spectacular performance these two athletes have in store for us today? Let us stay tuned!

Both contestants have already taken their places on the stage, staring each other down. One party holds an arrogant gaze, while the other’s eyes contain a philistine glint. Contestant Du Xueyi is evidently faltering under his opponent’s philistine gaze and has already lost some ground.

In their first confrontation, Contestant Meng Jingzhou pulls ahead by a slim margin, relying on his shameless aura to secure a small victory!

The match is about to begin, yet Contestant Meng Jingzhou is walking toward the referee. What is he planning to do?

He takes out a top-grade spirit stone and is brazenly trying to bribe the referee in front of everyone!

The referee refuses Contestant Meng Jingzhou’s bribery attempt and issues him a yellow card as a warning!

Contestant Meng Jingzhou seems to have misunderstood the referee’s actions and thinks that the referee wants to exchange his spirit stone with a yellow card.

The referee has struck! The referee has tried to attack Contestant Meng Jingzhou!

It appears that the referee is aware that he cannot strike a contestant, so he has given himself a red card and disqualified himself.

This match is truly full of twists and turns. It has yet to begin, and there is already a change of referee!

Contestant Meng Jingzhou is not discouraged by his failure. He pushes on and has chosen to bribe Contestant Du Xueyi!

Contestant Du Xueyi has clearly never encountered a scenario like this before, and he seems to be at a loss for what to do. Fortunately, Sect Leader Qiu Jin’an’s gaze brings him back to his senses, and he decisively rejects Contestant Meng Jingzhou’s unreasonable request.

The new referee appears to be more experienced and issues another yellow card to Contestant Meng Jingzhou.

Finally, Contestant Meng Jingzhou obediently begins the match.

Right as the match kicks off, Contestant Du Xueyi unleashes a flurry of attacks. With his fists hammering down like rain and emitting the sound of thunder, he forces Contestant Meng Jingzhou to backpedal and scramble to cover his head like a scurrying mouse.

Meng Jingzhou, you brat deserve it...Sorry, the commentator got a bit personal there. We seek everyone’s forgiveness.

Contestant Meng Jingzhou seems to be at a disadvantage but largely unharmed. Instead, it looks like Contestant Du Xueyi is panting after his barrage of the Storming Thunder Fist Technique.

This is an opportunity that Contestant Meng Jingzhou swiftly seizes. He launches a fierce counterattack and unleashes Third Elder’s signature ultimate move, the Heaven-Shaking Six Forms, gaining the upper hand!

Contestant Du Xueyi is caught off guard by Contestant Meng Jingzhou’s surprisingly intense counterattack and has lost control of the battle. He is now forced into a passive position to defend himself!

However, Contestant Meng Jingzhou charges like a ferocious tiger descending the mountain and roaring through the forest. His fist strikes are fierce, powerful yet steady, and overwhelming, sending Contestant Du Xueyi reeling with blood splattering from the impact!

Despite his injury, Contestant Du Xueyi takes another heavy punch from his opponent and nimbly retreats to recover.

Contestant Meng Jingzhou is not letting his chance slip by. He pursues Contestant Du Xueyi relentlessly, closing in on him with a brutal strike. Contestant Du Xueyi seems to have gradually adapted to Contestant Meng Jingzhou’s combat style, colliding his fists and feet with his opponent’s and producing a sharp, deafening sound!

As the onslaught rages on, both parties appear locked in a stalemate.

Contestant Meng Jingzhou is the first to break the impasse. He takes half a step forward and rams his head into Contestant Meng Xueyi’s head!

What an unexpected move! Could Contestant Meng Jingzhou have practiced the Iron Head Art... Hold on, that doesn’t look like it!

It was not Contestant Meng Jingzhou’s head but his hair that had knocked into Contestant Du Xueyi’s head! As a physique cultivator, Contestant Meng Jingzhou has reinforced his hair to be as tough as his body! Furthermore, hair doesn’t feel pain!

What brilliant thinking! It’s incredibly remarkable!

Contestant Du Xueyi is stunned by the blow and clutches his head as he staggers back. This is precisely what Contestant Meng Jingzhou is hoping for!

Grasping this opportunity, Contestant Meng Jingzhou grabbed his opponent’s clothes and flung him out of the arena.

Contestant Meng Jingzhou wins!

With a Sound Amplification Array, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy announced, “I hereby declare that the winner of the first round in the Foundation Establishment category is Meng Jingzhou!”

Right afterward, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy asked Lu Yang in the mental space, “You were rambling on for a long while just now. What was that all about?”

Chapter 167: A Confucian Cultivator Against a Confucian Cultivator

Qiu Jin’an shook his head, seemingly unbothered by Du Xueyi’s disappointing performance. “The kid still lacks combat experience. He should take this defeat as a lesson.”

Lu Yang thought, Sect Leader Qiu, you don’t have to keep up the pretense. You have already crushed a teacup, yet you’re still saying that one defeat is nothing.

It had been Lu Yang’s idea to let Meng Jingzhou appear in the first round so that the latter could assert dominance right off the gate.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy hesitated before commenting, “Sect Leader Qiu, with how Meng Jingzhou managed to temper even his hair and ram it into his opponent’s head, I don’t think that ‘lacking combat experience’ is an apt description.” At the very least, I’ve never seen such an absurd method of reinforcing the body in ancient times.

Could this be what new-generation physique cultivators are like?

Qiu Jin’an almost choked because of her blunt words. Can I get someone else to sit next to me?

He put on an indifferent expression. “I let Du Xueyi go up first just as a warm-up for the audience. The next person won’t be as easy to deal with.”

An elegant Confucian cultivator donned in light blue Confucian robes appeared at the Martial Plaza. He wore a silk cap and held a paper fan, his demeanor unruffled.

“This is our sect’s most outstanding Confucian cultivator at the Foundation Establishment Stage. His name is Fang Hao.” In spite of what Qiu Jin’an had said, those from the Five-Elements Sect knew that Fang Hao’s level was not much different from Du Xueyi’s.

“What a coincidence, I am also a Confucian cultivator.” Man Gu made a late entrance from the other side of the Martial Plaza, walking over while carrying a large hammer.

Initially, Man Gu planned to drag Meng Jingzhou over, but the referee wouldn’t allow it, stating that Meng Jingzhou was not a weapon. Therefore, Man Gu could only settle for the next best option—the Dark Sand Iron Hammer he had redeemed.

The handle of the hammer was stuck with talismans capable of reciting the entirety of Words of Sages.

“The sages once said, ‘Is learning and regularly practicing something not a form of joy...’”

Man Gu slowly advanced toward Fang Hao, his face twisted with malevolence. The voice from the recital of Words of Sages reverberated throughout the Martial Plaza, sounding like a murderer chanting the Rebirth Requiem after slaughtering a family of twenty-eight and not even sparing the rats. No matter how others looked at it, the contrast was jarring.

As soon as the match began, Man Gu swung the Dark Sand Iron Hammer toward Fang Hao. The latter stepped to the side, dodging the attack in a graceful fashion.

Man Gu exerted force with his wrist, abruptly changing the hammer’s trajectory and sweeping it horizontally at Fang Hao.

Not expecting such a brute strike from Man Gu, Fang Hao couldn’t evade in time and used his paper fan to block it. However, it shattered upon impact, and he was swept off his feet.

The paper fan was a magical treasure that shielded the user from one fatal blow, so Fang Hao remained unscathed. However, he now retracted his smile, realizing that Man Gu was no easy opponent.

A miniature whirlwind swirled around Fang Hao. After it dissipated, an invisible force enveloped him.

“Vast Righteous Qi?”[1] the Everlasting Immortal Fairy exclaimed. This was her first time witnessing it since her resurrection.

Since Fang Hao was a proper Confucian cultivator, the invisible force was naturally the Vast Righteous Qi.

Lu Yang asked, “There were also Confucian cultivators and Vast Righteous Qi in ancient times?”

“Of course. The author of Words of Sages appeared much earlier than you might think.”

“So did Confucius become an immortal?”

“I don’t know.”

“You don't know?”

“‘Sage’ isn’t a cultivation realm but a state of mind based on ‘benevolence.’ A person who spends their whole life embodying the concept of ‘benevolence’ achieves the realm of the sages.

“There are many interpretations of ‘benevolence.’ I could talk for three days and three nights and still not finish sharing everything. That said, with my level, I can’t talk for that long either.” Clearly, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy was well aware of the limits of her knowledge.

Fang Hao used his Vast Righteous Qi as ink and wrote with a brush made from weasel bristle in the air—The gentleman goes no further; the path ahead is forbidden.

Man Gu was charging toward Fang Hao when he involuntarily halted in his tracks upon seeing the words, as if his body was no longer under his control.

This was the Theory and Practice as One Technique, very rare among Confucian cultivators. It could coerce the other party to act according to the words written, achieving the unity of theory and practice.

Naturally, this spell was not without constraints. Even someone as talented as Fang Hao could only employ it on one person at the same cultivation stage at any one time, while those at a higher cultivation realm would be immune.

However, it is just enough to deal with Man Gu.

Fang Hao wrote some words again—Don't do unto others what you don't want done unto you.

The phrase meant that one shouldn’t impose what they do not wish for onto others. With this phrase, if Man Gu wanted to hit Fang Hao, he would have to hit himself first.

Surprisingly, Man Gu saw that the restraining command halting him in his tracks disappeared, and he smashed his giant hammer in Fang Hao’s direction, giving the latter a huge fright.

“How did you break free of my control?!”

“Control?” Man Gu didn’t really understand what Fang Hao was getting at. “Doesn’t the phrase mean that whatever I don’t want, I absolutely won’t give it to you? That doesn’t restrict my freedom, right?”

Fang Hao almost vomited blood from anger. The prerequisite for the Theory and Practice as One Technique to work is that the other party must understand the meaning of the phrase. But my opponent is a pure savage!

In a moment of carelessness, Fang Hao was grazed by Man Gu’s hammer, and blood flowed profusely. He hurriedly retreated to dodge Man Gu’s large hammer, then held his brush to write again—If you want to attack me, you’ll have to attack yourself first.

Although the effect of vernacular is worse than the classical language, now’s not the time to bother about it.

Man Gu continued swinging his hammer toward Fang Hao, still not getting affected by the control.

Fang Hao was in disbelief. Does this savage not even know how to read?!

When Man Gu leaped to strike his hammer toward Fang Hao’s head, he finally noticed that Man Gu was fighting with his eyes closed!

After learning from Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou for a month, Man Gu’s mind had become more nimble. Through his exchanges with his opponent, he realized that as long as he didn’t look at Fang Hao’s words, he wouldn’t fall into his trap.

In that case, I can just close my eyes!

Before Man Gu’s hammer was about to land, the referee intervened and deflected the attack. If it had smashed into Fang Hao, he would have to give up on picking up a brush ever again.

“Round Two, Man Gu wins.”

Qiu Jin’an’s expression was getting unpleasant, something he was not unfamiliar with considering his experience of getting bullied by the Dao-Seeking Nine since he was young.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy remarked, “As expected of the Ancient Barbarian Tribe. They are a naturally born warrior race. He could even pull off something like fighting with his eyes closed.”

Lu Yang asked, “Do you know a lot about the Ancient Barbarian Tribe?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was overflowing with confidence. “That’s a given! You could even say that I was their teacher.

“You know those barbarians. Their minds aren’t the sharpest. By some coincidence, they heard that I was intelligent and stood out even among immortals, so they invited me to teach their people.

“It wasn’t easy to teach them. They would forget whatever they learned the next day. Fortunately, with my incredible perseverance and patience, I eventually learned the meaning of giving up from the Barbarian Tribe.

“Afterward, I changed my strategy. I would enlighten them directly by pouring my wisdom into their minds and bloodline. That way, their intelligence will rise to a level just below mine!”

Lu Yang sharply inhaled a cold breath of air. Immortal Fairy, you poisoned them irreparably for ten thousand years.

Suddenly, Lu Yang realized something. Despite the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s enormous contributions to the Ancient Barbarian Tribe, Man Gu has never heard anything about her.

“Was there a gap in the passing down of the Ancient Barbarian Tribe’s legacy, or did someone deliberately erase the traces of her existence?”

To make an immortal fade from the entire world’s memory—what an absurd undertaking that must have been!

1. A concept of a grand upright spirit in Confucianism. ☜

Chapter 168: Lu Yang Takes the Field

“Up next, Li Haoran of the Dao-Seeking Sect versus Long Xiang of the Five-Elements Sect.”

“Li Haoran has a Fire Spirit Root?” Qiu Jin’an suddenly asked.

“Yes, what about it?”

“That’s interesting then. Our sect’s Long Xiang has a Water Spirit Root. This will be a round of fire against water.”

On the stage, Li Haoran and Long Xiang cupped their fists in salute.

“Please show me the way.”

“You flatter me.”

The two then fell completely silent.

Once the match began, Long Xiang took the initiative, like a dragon leaping into the perilous seas. The two ice blades he wielded emitted waves of frosty air, causing the temperature of the entire Martial Plaza to plummet.

“Flying Dragon Strike!”

Long Xiang roared, but what greeted him was Li Haoran’s fist.

Lu Yang frowned. Li Haoran is not a physique cultivator. Why is he fighting with his bare fists? Even Man Gu knows to use weapons when fighting.

Since Long Xiang was unaware of Li Haoran’s capabilities, he didn’t notice anything amiss and slashed at him with his blades.

Rings of fire burst from Li Haoran. Pointing at Long Xiang, he commanded, “Go.” The fire rings immediately flew toward Long Xiang and encircled him.

“Water, rise, Raging Waves!” Long Xiang conjured the phantom of surging waves behind him, and the audience below the stage could vaguely hear the sound of crashing waves.

The phantom waves dispersed the fire rings.

Li Haoran strode forward, landing layers of red fist seals on Long Xiang.

Molten lava gushed under Li Haoran’s feet—this was the result of immersing himself in lava for a year.

The lava collided with the waves. Despite the waves being just a shadow image, they emitted vapor upon impact with the lava. As a dense mist shrouded the venue, it obscured the figures of the contestants, leaving only the sounds of their clashes audible.

Li Haoran’s fist technique was astonishing, a stark contrast to the impression he usually gave. Long Xiang was not adept at close combat. He was struggling to keep up and suffered several blows. Fortunately for him, Li Haoran’s offensive power was insufficient to inflict significant injuries on him.

Long Xiang raised his hand, gathering the surrounding mist into a column of water, which he hurled at Li Haoran.

Unable to dodge, Li Haoran was soaked from head to toe by the water pillar. He engaged Long Xiang again, but this time, the latter gained the upper hand. For some reason, Li Haoran’s movements had become sluggish.

Li Haoran knitted his brow, realizing the source of the problem.

Long Xiang laughed out loud. “Brother Li, you are very smart to notice my trap so quickly, but it’s too late. You have been drenched by the water column. I can manipulate the weight of water to make you fight with a heavy load, so of course, your movements won’t be as nimble as before. You’ve lost!”

To Long Xiang's surprise, Li Haoran revealed a faint smile. “Is that so? I beg to differ.”

Long Xiang wanted to raise his hand to attack, but he found that he couldn’t move at all. “What did you do?!” He widened his eyes, utterly clueless about what had happened.

Flames soared from Li Haoran, evaporating the vapor around him as he leisurely strolled up to Long Xiang. “Your shirt has been refined by me.”
