Only then did realization dawn upon Long Xiang. The several fists Li Haoran had landed on him earlier weren’t meant to attack him but to refine his clothes into a metal prison. I, Long Xiang, am now the prey in this metal trap, with no chance of escape.

Are all the combat methods from the Dao-Seeking Sect this bizarre? Is this something a human can come up with?!

Li Haoran explained, “I heard from Senior Brother Lu Yang that you could use a storage ring to strip an enemy of their clothes, and that got me thinking. Since you can take away an opponent’s clothes, why can’t you refine them? From the looks of it now, my line of thinking was right.”

Qiu Jin’an was appalled as he stared at Lu Yang. How did you come up with such a shameless combat strategy?

“Oh, right, this is the Dao-Seeking Sect. That explains everything.”

With three wins out of three matches, the victory of the Foundation Establishment category was already in the bag. However, since this contest was supposed to be for the purpose of friendly exchange, the remaining two matches still had to proceed even if the outcome was already determined.

Tao Yaoye was up for the fourth round. Her Metamorphic Celestial Physique was rarer than a Single Spirit Root, demonstrating stunning power. In terms of one-on-one combat, she was also slightly stronger than Li Haoran.

To everyone’s surprise, Tao Yaoye ended up losing.

The one who defeated her was a young man in white robes. He was at the Intermediate Foundation Establishment Stage and a year older than Tao Yaoye.

On the other hand, Tao Yaoye was still at the Basic Foundation Establishment Stage, so her powers and combat experience paled in comparison to him.

“Next,” the young man in white robes said coldly. He didn’t leave the arena, instead opting to continue fighting.

Upon witnessing his overwhelming strength, the fifth disciple, whom Qiu Jin’an had chosen to take the stage next, voluntarily forfeited his spot, aware of the young man’s reputation.

Tao Yaoye was slightly indignant about the defeat. She had always been in first place since she was young. However, her opponent’s skills were so sublime that she lost before she could even exhibit the qualities of her Metamorphic Celestial Physique.

Someone from behind Tao Yaoye patted her on the shoulder.

She turned around, and tears welled in her eyes when she saw who it was. “Senior Brother, I lost.”

That person wiped her tears away and consoled her, “Your cultivation and experience still have room for improvement, and you are also a year younger than your opponent. Besides, Big Senior Sister told me that the strengths of the Metamorphic Celestial Physique aren’t apparent in its early stages.

“Since you call me senior brother, I have to defeat him, no matter what.”

~~~

Qiu Jin’an was pleased to see that they had finally clinched a victory, and he smilingly introduced, “This is my youngest disciple, Bai Ming, also my pride and joy. He has mastered three of the Five-Elements spells, and his fire-type spells are close to producing true fire. During our sect’s tournament, he wiped the floor with the Foundation Establishment category and attained first place.”

Cultivating Five-Elements spells was notoriously difficult. The spells often conflicted with one another, and one misstep could ruin one’s entire cultivation. It was extremely rare for a Foundation Establishment cultivator like Bai Ming to be proficient in three elements.

Bai Ming’s presence bolstered Qiu Jin’an’s confidence. “I’m just saying, but it doesn’t matter who you send.” Despite losing the first three matches, Bai Ming’s crushing victory brought a wide grin to Qiu Jin’an’s face. “May I know who your sect will send for the next match?”

“Me.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy volunteered on Lu Yang’s behalf.

On the stage of the Martial Plaza, a figure sauntered forward with steady steps, and it was none other than Lu Yang.

However, this Lu Yang was poles apart from the usual Lu Yang—he had a shiny bald head and his face radiated benevolence.

Bai Ming’s cold expression cracked into one of disbelief, as if he had seen a ghost. Of course, I know Lu Yang. He is the Dao-Seeking Sect’s acting sect leader who is supposed to be sitting at the spectator stand. Then who on earth is this person in front of me?!

“A clone!” Qiu Jin’an’s keen eye immediately discerned the origin of this “Lu Yang” on the stage. But that’s even more impossible. Lu Yang is only at the Foundation Establishment Stage. How could he have a clone?

To my knowledge, there is no cultivation technique or spell that can achieve something like that!

“To be precise, it’s a Bodhi tree clone,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy added.

Lu Yang had used the Tree-Planting Mantra to plant himself, and the Bodhi tree fruited two people—one was his true self, and the other was his bald clone.

“A clone from the Seventy-Two Mighty Abilities?!” Qiu Jin’an’s was flabbergasted. Apart from Yun Zhi, how could anyone at the Foundation Establishment Stage master a spell like this?

“No, wait, it’s a wood-type clone!” Turbulent waves roiled in Qiu Jin’an’s heart. I’ve never seen a spell like this before... This is a newly invented spell!

Who was it?!

Was it Yun Zhi, or perhaps...

Qiu Jin’an’s gaze shifted to Lu Yang, his eyelids twitching. Earlier, he had heard of Lu Yang challenging those beyond his level from the people of the Dao-Seeking Sect, but he had simply assumed that it was due to some trick.

But if this technique was really invented by him, then perhaps the matter of him challenging beyond his level is not without substance!

Chapter 169: Clash of the Five-Elements Spells

“Dao-Seeking Sect, Lu Yang.”

“Five-Elements Sect, Bai Ming.”

Bai Ming tensed up as if facing a formidable opponent. Though Qiu Jin’an's expression shifted, he showed no intention of halting the match. This means that the Lu Yang before me goes against common sense but doesn’t go against the rules and is not considered cheating.

That’s truly terrifying.

Swoosh! The sound of a spear slicing through the air marked the commencement of the battle.

Bai Ming wielded a silver spear that shone brilliantly under the sunlight. He made the first move to attack Lu Yang, which the latter calmly tackled by sidestepping to his right. His Qingfeng sword scratched the spear, igniting sparks in all directions. With this momentum, he slid across the spear to slash at Bai Ming’s hands.

Bai Ming flicked his wrists. The spear vibrated and deflected the Qingfeng Sword’s strike.

Rays of sword descended like rain, morphing into a river that continuously cascaded downward, while the spear was bold and aggressive, moving in wide arcs. It remained unflinching in the face of Lu Yang’s sword technique, choosing to meet it head-on.

The sword and spear clashed, the whole display dazzling the audience’s eyes. It seemed as if the outcome could be determined at any second. The disciples of the Five-Elements Sect were astonished; they had never seen anyone at the same cultivation stage tie with Bai Ming in a weapon duel.

“A tie?” Meng Jingzhou scoffed. From the beginning, Lu Yang has only been using the most basic sword moves. It’s just that he joined them so seamlessly that the Foundation Establishment cultivators from the Five-Elements Sect couldn’t discern anything.

Meng Jingzhou knew best how powerful Lu Yang’s sword technique was. Up until now, Lu Yang had yet to showcase any complex sword technique. Although Lu Yang rarely unsheathes his sword, that doesn’t signify that his swordsmanship is weak. After all, with a Sword Spirit Root, how could his sword technique be anything but strong?

Tao Yaoye’s fiery gaze was fixed on Lu Yang’s figure in battle, but she was thinking of another matter. She had been right by Lu Yang’s side when he learned the Tree-Planting Mantra. I clearly remember that the maximum distance between Lu Yang and the vegetative person is only twenty meters. But no matter how I look at it, the distance between the spectator stand and the Martial Plaza’s stage is much more than twenty meters.

What Tao Yaoye didn’t know was that Lu Yang had obtained a spell to command ghost servants after defeating the tiger demon. However, it turned into an Out-Of-Body Soul Technique when he tried to learn it. Therefore, upon creating the Bodhi tree clone, Lu Yang had his soul leave his body and enter his clone. That way, he didn’t have to worry about the distance between his original body and his clone.

In other words, Lu Yang’s soul was on the battle stage, while the Lu Yang at the spectator stand was fully controlled by the Everlasting Immortal Fairy.

In the arena, Lu Yang seized an opportunity to flip himself. While he was spinning in mid-air, he raised his right leg and channeled all his power toward it, stomping down on the head of the silver spear. Bai Ming tried to pull his spear free, but Lu Yang’s body weighed down like a mountain.

The Qingfeng sword drew an arc through the air and broke the sound barrier as it aimed straight at Bai Ming.

The crowd erupted in gasps, but a disciple from the Five-Elements Sect quickly collected themselves. “Don’t panic. Don’t forget that Senior Brother Bai Ming’s strength lies in his Five-Elements spells. His spear technique is just a distraction!”

Bai Ming released his grip on the spear and swiftly retreated while forming a hand seal. A gigantic earth serpent surged forth from the ground.

The Martial Plaza was not constructed with stone bricks but with loess, a unique yellow soil, and was stabilized by an array.

“It’s the Earth Dragon from the Five-Elements spells!” Long Xiang of the Five-Elements Sect cried out.

The form of a dragon held special significance in the cultivation world. At Bai Ming’s current stage, he was still unable to transform the earth into a dragon, so he could only create an earth serpent. Even so, easily summoning an earth serpent was not something any ordinary Foundation Establishment cultivator could achieve!

Lu Yang appeared unperturbed. He softly muttered two words and passed through the earth serpent. “Shrinking Earth.”

Bai Ming’s pupils constricted. What spell is this? A Five-Elements spell? I didn’t expect Lu Yang to be capable of using Five-Elements spells too, and not just any, but the extremely difficult Earth Escape Technique! Even I have only scratched the surface of this highly demanding spell!

Could his talent in spells be above mine?! But how could that be? I possess the Five-Elements Celestial Physique, just like the founder of the Five-Elements Sect! I’m born to excel in the Five Elements!

Qiu Jin’an was visibly moved. “No, this isn’t the Earth Escape Technique!” He knew what the Five-Elements spells comprised and how they should be cast better than anyone. However, the spell Lu Yang unleashed didn’t match any of the spells he recognized.

A completely new spell yet again?!

“How did you invent this?” Qiu Jin’an turned to ask the Everlasting Immortal Fairy.

She replied dispassionately, “Learned it while learning Shrinking Earth To Inches.”

“Huh?” Qiu Jin’an’s mind still couldn’t process what he had just heard. How are these two spells related?

Back in the arena, the tides had turned once again. Bai Ming switched from defense to offense. As he formed a seal with his hand, a murderous aura of metal congealed on the stage. Dozens of small daggers flew out from his robe, moving at his command.

“It’s the Metal Manipulation Technique!” Fang Hao of the Five-Elements Sect shouted.

The Metal Manipulation Technique allowed one to mobilize anything made of metal. At advanced stages, one could even control the opponent’s magical artifacts, which was a truly terrifying prospect.

However, Bai Ming could only command his own magical treasure for now, similar to the Object Manipulation Technique, though his version was more combat-oriented.

The dozens of daggers were like murderous weapons demanding their target’s life as they were shot from all directions, aiming right at Lu Yang’s vital points.

Unable to avoid the attacks, Lu Yang pulled out the Golden Light Incantation and stuck it to himself, emitting an intense golden light that formed a protective barrier around him. He had purchased it with the contribution points awarded by Dai Bufan when he just returned to the Dao-Seeking Sect from Yanjiang Commandery.

As soon as the daggers hit Lu Yang, they were deflected away.

Bai Ming sneered. “Hmph, it’s just a talisman with limited use and duration. How many times can it save you?”

Hearing this, Lu Yang removed the Golden Light Incantation.

Bai Ming continued to snigger, “Giving up already...”

Lu Yang stuck the talisman back on, and he flared with intense golden light. Then, he removed it and stuck it back, repeating this over and over. The jarring transitions from the flickering rays of light almost blinded Bai Ming’s eyes.

Bai Ming never imagined that the Golden Light Incantation could be used in this manner.

As it was his first time encountering such a situation, his eyelids instinctively tried to close. However, when he realized that closing his eyes now would render him vulnerable to Lu Yang’s attack, he struggled against his body’s natural instinct and squinted his eyes.

In that moment, as he fought against his natural instincts, Lu Yang dove into the ground and suddenly emerged beneath Bai Ming, delivering a solid punch to Bai Ming’s jaw and knocking out a tooth!

“Jinwu Crow Flame!”[1] Bai Ming unleashed his most powerful attack in a bid to end the fight with one decisive strike.

Crimson gold flames rampaged as faint cries of the jinwu crow echoed from within. The scorching blaze instantly increased the temperature of the entire Martial Plaza by more than twenty degrees. Even the audience below the stage could feel the flames assaulting their senses.

The person with the most intense reaction to the jinwu crow was Long Xiang, whose Water Spirit Root was incompatible with fire. The appearance of the jinwu crow gave off a suffocating feeling, and he even felt that the circulation of spirit energy within him had slowed down slightly.

~~~

Someone commented, “Is this the Jinwu Crow Flame that established Senior Brother Bai’s status as the number one person among those at the Foundation Establishment Stage? It’s indeed very powerful!”

“I heard the sect leader say that Senior Brother Bai’s Jinwu Crow Flame is evolving into the more advanced version, that is, the Sun True Fire. Once he reaches the Golden Core Stage, the Jinwu Crow Flame will smoothly transform into the Sun True Fire. Able to wield true fire right after one enters the Golden Core Stage? That’s terrifying!”

Long Xiang turned his head and was very surprised to see that Li Haoran was not the least bit concerned about Lu Yang. As someone with a Fire Spirit Root, he should be well aware of how frightening the Jinwu Crow Flame is.

“Aren’t you worried about Lu Yang?”

Li Haoran flashed a smile, not giving a direct answer to his question. “Senior Brother Lu once commissioned me to craft a flying carriage. We worked together for three days and finally achieved results.

“During the whole crafting process, Senior Brother Lu was responsible for supplying the flames. Do you know what kind of fire that was?”

“What was it?”

“Three Esse True Fire.”

~~~

Meanwhile, on the battle stage, Bai Ming suddenly felt uneasy despite feeling certain of his victory just a moment ago. However, the Jinwu Crow Flame had blocked his vision of Lu Yang.

Suddenly, his expression completely changed. He sensed a much more fierce and domineering fire emanating from Lu Yang’s direction.

This sensation...it’s true fire!

1. Jinwu, sometimes known as the “Golden Crow,” is the three-legged crow. It resides in the sun and is the spirit of the sun in Chinese mythology. ☜

Chapter 170: Water-Repelling Mantra

The Great Void Pill Scripture was the most renowned and publicly recognized classic text.

The work began by stating the premier method of concocting pills: The Great Void[1] as the cauldron, the Supreme Ultimate as the furnace, purity as the pill base, doctrine of inaction as the dantian, life as lead and mercury, and the five organs as fire.

This was how the Three Esse True Fire came to be and why it was revered by pill-concocting masters as their most prized treasure. The Three Esse True Fire could refine natural treasures from heaven and earth. In some sense, cultivators could also be considered as such treasures. If a cultivator encountered the Three Esse True Fire, one could only imagine the consequences.

Although Lu Yang’s Three Flavored True Fire was born from the Three Esse True Fire and slightly paled in comparison, it was still not to be underestimated.

On the battle stage, Lu Yang’s Three Flavored True Fire was fast and furious as it gushed forward, transforming into a fire dragon that bit into the jinwu crow and forcefully ripped it apart.

Bai Ming couldn’t believe his eyes. Someone actually mastered True Fire at just the Foundation Establishment Stage, and it’s even the famous and legendary Three Esse True Fire at that?

For someone who had been showered with admiration and praise since childhood, he found it hard to accept what was unfolding before him.

At the spectator stand, Qiu Jin’an had originally slapped his thigh in joy upon seeing his disciple unleash the Jinwu Crow Flame in a brilliant display. However, his flame of excitement was soon doused when he saw Lu Yang casting his true fire.

“This is the Three Esse True Fire? Wait, it’s not, but it’s very close!” Qiu Jin’an searched through the repository of true fires in his head, but none seemed to match.

A terrifying thought began to burgeon in his mind. This can’t be a fire beyond the 108 True Fires, right? Was it previously not recorded and discovered, or has it just been invented by someone?

“Sect Leader Lu, what kind of true fire is this?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy impassively replied, “It’s nothing, just a flame for barbecuing skewers. You don’t have to be so alarmed, Sect Leader Qiu.”

Her attitude only further reinforced Qiu Jin’an’s conjecture, causing him to gasp inwardly. How is this person so powerful? Not only is he proficient in wood, earth, and fire-type spells like Bai Ming, he can even create new spells and techniques!

Inventing spells is one thing, but inventing true fire?

Bai Ming got burned by the Three Flavored True Fire. Lu Yang quickly followed up with a punch to his chest, sending Bai Ming flying with a mix of sweet, salty, and spicy flavors in his mouth and his breathing almost imperceptible. As he flew backward, it dawned upon him that the battle was over, and there was no hope of turning the tide.

Should I gracefully admit defeat, or should I stubbornly wait for the result to be announced?

A myriad of scenes flashed through Bai Ming’s mind.

At a young age, his shifu had brought him up the mountain, and he grew up under the care of his senior brothers and sisters, reading books diligently and training assiduously. During his training in cultivation, his shifu would become stern and chastise him to correct his attitude and posture. After training ended, however, his shifu would apply medicine for him and encourage him to persevere in his cultivation.

Despite tirelessly training until he was drenched in sweat, he never slacked off, comprehending spells and enduring the cold, heat, and loneliness. His accumulated efforts paid off, and he rapidly grew, advancing from the Qi Training to the Intermediate Foundation Establishment stage without losing a single battle.

Bai Ming closed his eyes, comprehending and reflecting on his battle with Lu Yang. He felt as if something was about to sprout in his heart.

Landing steadily, he brought his palms together like he was in prayer and stood on one leg, his breathing growing stronger and more sturdy. When he opened his eyes, he radiated a power that surpassed his own.

“He has broken through to the Advanced Foundation Establishment Stage?” Qiu Jin’an was euphoric to see his disciple break through. Bai Ming has been at the Intermediate Foundation Establishment Stage for several months, so it is about time for him to break through. I just didn’t expect it to happen now.

In the audience, the disciples of the Five-Elements Sect buzzed among themselves at the new turn of events.

Meanwhile, Lu Yang didn’t know where to start venting. I was on the brink of victory, and you just had to break through in the middle of battle right then?

Shouldn’t something like this happen to me instead?

“Never mind, I’ll just continue fighting then.” Lu Yang raised his Qingfeng Sword. I haven’t showcased my real abilities yet. Neither the Slashing Word Mantra nor the Breaking Sword Mantra have been used. I’ll forget about the Animal Form Fist. That is overkill.

Lu Yang felt that he still had a shred of conscience within him.

“Lu Yang, Lu Yang, let me, let me!” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy called out to him. Watching Lu Yang’s exciting battle, she was itching to join the fun.

Since she was in the state of a soul, the twenty-meter restriction didn’t apply to her. As long as Lu Yang agreed, she could separate a wisp of her mental power and infuse it in Lu Yang’s clone anytime.

Lu Yang was a bit skeptical. Can the Everlasting Immortal Fairy be counted on?

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy placed her hands on her hips and pointed at Lu Yang, “I am the sect leader. You have to listen to me!”

Lu Yang sighed helplessly. Fine then, I’ll go along with her. She has even pulled out the acting sect leader card. If things don’t look optimistic, I’ll just reclaim control of my body.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy gleefully took control of the bald Lu Yang clone as she had wished. When she raised her right hand and extended a finger, she appeared rather coquettish.

Bai Ming cast a peculiar look at Lu Yang. If the Lu Yang a moment ago resembled a monk, he now looks like...a nun?

Does he have a split personality disorder?

Bai Ming had heard of a saying in the cultivation world: “No insanity, no victory.”[2] There are countless cultivators throughout history who cultivated until they developed a split personality disorder, and those who made it into the annals of history were undoubtedly extraordinary.

“Could Lu Yang’s crazy strength come from a split personality disorder?” The more Bai Ming thought about it, the more plausible he felt his theory was.

Just then, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy slowly lifted her finger. An immortal spell twined around her fingertip as she softly chanted, “Water-Repelling Mantra.”

An invisible barrier spread outward with the Everlasting Immortal Fairy at its center, expelling all moisture within its range. The remaining moisture had already thinned from the two rounds of flames clashing. Now, not even a drop remained around the Everlasting Immortal Fairy.

This was not the most terrifying. The truly horrifying part was that there was also water within Bai Ming, and it was rapidly leaving his body!

Although Lu Yang’s body also contained water, as the spell caster, the rate of his bodily water loss was much slower than Bai Ming’s!

Bai Ming stared at his gradually desiccating body in horror and was at a loss for what to do. He had no way to stop the spell; it was far beyond his realm of understanding.

The Water-Repelling Mantra exhibited no visible effect when it was cast. To bystanders, it appeared as if nothing had happened. Only those experiencing it firsthand could fathom just how terrifying this spell was!

“We concede!” Qiu Jin’an personally stepped in and halted the water loss from Bai Ming’s body, quickly feeding him a pill for his body to recover.

He cast a meaningful look at Lu Yang. As expected of someone who could become the acting sect leader. Not only is he well-versed in four of the five elements, but he can even use a water-type spell that is recorded as a forbidden mighty ability in the ancient texts!

Lu Yang’s eyes widened. So this is the Water-Repelling Mantra the Everlasting Immortal Fairy had described? Its effects are actually this terrifying?

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy giggled. “Hehe, it’s nothing special. Unfortunately, your cultivation realm is too low. Your senior brothers and sisters are at the Golden Core Stage, and their moisture is locked within their bodies, so this move won’t work on them. Once you have reached the Golden Core Stage, I’ll use your body to cast the spell, and none of them will be my match!”

“Can you teach me?” Lu Yang rubbed his hands together, eager to learn the technique.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy turned her head away. “Hmph, that’s what you get for looking down on my legacy! Not teaching!”

“Teach me, please, Immortal Fairy-jiejie.”[3]

“Not teaching! I said no, and I meant it!”

~~~

When Qiu Jin’an returned to the spectator stand, he found that Lu Yang was gone, the seat beside him now taken by Yun Zhi. Although I did say that I want someone else to sit beside me, it’s anyone but Yun Zhi!

He felt as if the surrounding temperature had dropped by a few degrees.

“Miss Yun Zhi, where did Sect Leader Lu go?” Qiu Jin’an tried to strike up a conversation, unable to stand the frigid atmosphere.

“There are some guests outside the entrance who are adept at barbecuing. He’s gone to receive them.”

“Huh?”

1. Taixu refers to the primordial state of the universe in ancient Chinese philosophy. ☜

2. The original quote is common in Beijing Opera, where it refers to how only those eccentric individuals who are mad and obsessed with their craft accomplish great things. I tried to make it rhyme since it does rhyme in the original Chinese version. ☜

3. ”Jiejie” means elder sister in Chinese and is also a form of endearment. It sounds more informal and occasionally “cute” compared to when only “jie” is used. ☜

Chapter 171: This Mission Has the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s Protection

Outside the Dao-Seeking Sect, eight men dressed in plain clothes were in the middle of a discussion.

“These rich dogs from the Five-Elements Sect really have so many spirit stones that they have nowhere else to spend them. They built such a colossal flying vessel with a bunch of useless designs! If we had this many spirit stones, most of our plans could have been realized!” One of the higher-ups from the Everlasting Creed was drooling at the flying vessel docked outside the Dao-Seeking Sect as temptations to steal it budded in his mind.

Vice Creed Leader Liu lambasted him for his ignorance. “Calm down! Look at you, acting like you’ve never seen the world. If this mission of ours goes smoothly, we can put the Dao-Seeking Sect to sleep and plunder to our heart’s desire. What’s a mere flying vessel then?”

Another higher-up expressed some concern for the future. “But can our plan succeed? After all, we have never set foot in the Dao-Seeking Sect before!”

The Dao-Seeking Sect was undoubtedly no different from a den of dragons and tigers for them.

“Please rest assured, everyone,” Tang Yunsheng spoke, “Our spies within the Dao-Seeking Sect have provided us with the event schedule and a map of the relevant zones within the sect. It will definitely be safe this time!” As an inspecting officer, even branch leaders had to bow to him. However, among the group right here, he had instead the lowest-ranking position and cultivation.

“Mmm, Little Tang is right,” affirmed Gao Zhenglai, the other vice creed leader at the Basic Fusion Stage. “Besides, we are all followers of the Everlasting Immortal, who is the embodiment of wisdom, power, and fortune. With the Everlasting Immortal’s protection, this mission will surely succeed!”

“May the Everlasting Immortal bless us!”

“May the Everlasting Immortal bless us!”

The eight of them whispered, afraid that someone would hear them.

“Sorry to keep you waiting,” Lu Yang greeted as he arrived to welcome his “subordinates.” On the surface, he was the acting sect leader of the Dao-Seeking Sect, but in secret, he was the “creed leader” of the Everlasting Creed, mingling with both good and evil factions.

“This is Branch Leader Lu Yang, an outstanding follower who has successfully infiltrated the ranks of the Dao-Seeking Sect,” Tang Yunsheng introduced Lu Yang to the others, then whispered, “What about the other two?”

All the leaders are here. How can there only be one person receiving them?

Lu Yang explained, “Meng Jingzhou and Man Gu are busy with the barbeque and have their hands tied.”

Tang Yunsheng then introduced the seven higher-ups, including the two vice-creed leaders, Liu and Gao, as well as five elders.

As Tang Yunsheng was only responsible for the coordination of personnel, he was not involved in the infiltration mission. After all, with his Nascent Soul cultivation, he wouldn’t even be able to stir up a ripple in the Dao-Seeking Sect, so there was no need to bring him along.

Lu Yang reminded his seven subordinates, “Your Excellencies, the Dao-Seeking Sect is a place fraught with perils for us, so I would like to request that all of you follow my instructions. If anything goes wrong, all of us will die without a place to bury our bodies!”

The seven of them frowned, instinctively averse to following the orders of a Foundation Establishment cultivator. However, considering that the visitors in a mental hospital must listen to the guide to avoid being attacked by the patients, they accepted the arrangement.

“Lead the way.”

When the disciple on gatekeeper duty saw the acting sect leader walk into the sect, he simply let the group pass.

Vice Creed Leader Liu was very astonished. We entered the Dao-Seeking Sect so easily?

Lu Yang smiled as he explained, “The disciples of the Dao-Seeking often come to eat skewers at our place, and over time, we’ve gotten familiar with one another. If I have some business, they usually wouldn’t make things difficult for me.”

Vice Creed Leader Liu patted Lu Yang on the shoulder. “I never expected you to integrate into the Dao-Seeking Sect so well. This is something many cultivators fail to do, even when they become lunatics themselves. You have done a great job. It’s a pity your cultivation is too low right now, else I’ll certainly insist on promoting you!”

Lu Yang remarked to himself, If I get promoted again, I can only become the creed founder.

Hmm? Hold on, what is a creed founder? Isn’t it just the founder of a creed? I resurrected the Everlasting Immortal Fairy and gave them faith, precisely what a creed founder does!

Lu Yang felt it was perfectly reasonable and justified for him to become the creed founder. I don’t have to compete with the false creed leader for the position anymore.

Now, the hierarchy of the Everlasting Creed is clear. At the top is the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, followed by Creed Founder Lu Yang, and only then are the minor figures like the creed leader and vice creed leaders.

Given that the Everlasting Immortal Fairy is already the Dao-Seeking Sect’s honored guest elder and temporary acting sect leader for three days, it’s also possible to view the Everlasting Creed as a subsidiary of the Dao-Seeking Sect.

When Vice Creed Leader Liu and the others entered the Dao-Seeking Sect, they were filled with curiosity, but they dared not release their spiritual consciousness, only observing the surroundings with their eyes. They were on edge the entire way, fearing that the people from the Dao-Seeking Sect might detect something amiss.

Fortunately for them, the worrisome matters had already happened, so worrying about them now was too late.

~~~

At the Martial Plaza, the first match of the Golden Core category had begun. Representing the Dao-Seeking Sect was Luo Hai, one of the disciples the Everlasting Immortal Fairy had challenged.

Luo Hai was adept at water-type spells, and so was his opponent. As the two parties engaged in battle, waves of water collided with the ceaseless sounds of tides, the spectacle far surpassing what one would associate with Golden Core cultivators.

~~~

“We’re here. This is our base!” Lu Yang arrived at a barbeque shop with a large signboard that read “One More Time.”

This was the shop Dai Bufan had arranged long ago. All this while, others had managed it. During the exchange event, it was to be temporarily handed over to Lu Yang and his two companions.

There were only a few people inside the large shop. Man Gu was tending to the fire and grilling the skewers with practiced movements.

Around this time, the other shops also began opening for business.

Out of the four main categories in the competition between the two sects, only the Foundation Establishment category had concluded. The three remaining categories would comprise longer battles and more notable methods and strategies, which made them more engaging. This was the true highlight of the exchange event.

As such, the shops chose to open their business at this time.

“Greetings, Vice Creed Leader...” Man Gu put aside what he was doing and was about to bow when Vice Creed Leader Liu stopped him.

“We are in a den of dragons and tigers. You may discard all formalities.”

“Yes, please take a seat,” Man Gu invited the seven of them to sit.

“Where’s Meng Jingzhou?” Lu Yang scanned the place but couldn’t find him.

“Oh, Brother Meng said that he is visiting the other shops to check on what their business is like and whether we need to develop a strategy.”

Lu Yang furrowed his brow and wanted to reproach Meng Jingzhou for neglecting his proper duties. The success of the Everlasting Creed hinges on this. How could he be distracted by trivial matters?

Vice Creed Leader Liu stopped Lu Yang. “Hey, no need to get angry. As the saying goes, ‘If you’re going to act, you should see it through.’ Little Meng’s actions are typical of a barbeque shop worker. It’s understandable.

“However, one person less is still one person less. Little Man, get Meng Jingzhou back. The three of you are the most familiar with the Dao-Seeking Sect, so let’s discuss our operation together.”

“Understood!” Man Gu sprinted out of the barbeque shop.

Before leaving, Man Gu said, “Brother Lu, someone ordered our skewers in advance. I’m almost done with them. Remember to deliver them in a bit.”

“Alright.”

Lu Yang took over Man Gu’s job and continued to grill the skewers with ease, looking just like a veteran worker with thirty years under his belt.

Vice Creed Leader Liu nodded at Lu Yang’s precise movements. Hmm, not much different from what I’ve learned.

After Lu Yang was done, he said, “Please wait a moment, Your Excellencies. I’ll go deliver the meal.”

“Wait, where are you going? I’ll send someone else to deliver it for you,” Vice Creed Leader Liu called out to Lu Yang. Once Lu Yang was gone, only the seven of them would be left in the barbeque shop.

Lu Yang pointed at the spectator stand in the distance. “The big shots at the spectator stand ordered it.”

Vice Creed Leader Liu was rendered speechless. The higher-ups of the Dao-Seeking Sect and Five-Elements Sect were at the spectator stand, and all of them were minimally at the Fusion Stage. If they were to head over there to deliver the meal, their identities could easily be exposed.

“Go ahead then! Come back quickly!” Vice Creed Leader Liu waved his hand.

Lu Yang grabbed the meal box and walked out briskly.

Not long after Lu Yang left, a pure and beautiful young woman noticed the shop. “Hmm? One More Time Barbeque Shop? What an interesting name! Hey, you all have business! I’ll have twenty lamb skewers. If they taste good, I’ll order more!”

The visitor was none other than Shangguan Yu.

Chapter 172: The Higher-Ups of the Everlasting Creed Are Dedicated to Their Work

“Lamb skewers?” Vice Creed Leader Liu frowned. We are here to show the Dao-Seeking Sect who’s boss, not to work.

“Hey, you don’t even take orders when business comes knocking?” Shangguan Yu was a bit perplexed. The shops in the Dao-Seeking Sect are also very special. They’re open but not for business?

Second Elder was behind Shangguan Yu. When he saw Vice Creed Leader Liu’s group, he asked them in a suspicious tone, “All of you look unfamiliar. I’ve never seen you in the Dao-Seeking Sect before. Could you be...”

Vice Creed Leader Liu recognized Second Elder, Ba Yan, with just one glance. This is a high-ranking and influential figure in the Dao-Seeking Sect, and he is at the Apex Fusion Stage. If someone like him grows suspicious of us, we could easily give ourselves away.

He plastered on a smiling face and gestured for the other six to get up and attend to the customers. “The shop manager is away, and we are temporary staff brought in to help. Did you say you want twenty lamb skewers? Please wait a moment. They’ll be ready soon.”

As members of a diabolic creed, wearing a cruel smile was an essential skill, but the ability to effortlessly switch between different types of smiles was just as important.

Vice Creed Leader Liu rolled up his sleeves and put on the white and black apron hanging on the wall before taking out twenty-five lamb skewers. “Since you are our first customer today, we will give you five extra skewers.”

A few flies flew over, drawn by the smell of meat, but Vice Creed Leader Liu quickly drove them away.

Second Elder was still not fully convinced. “Your shop doesn’t look very clean...”

Vice Creed Leader Liu hurriedly ordered, “Old Gao, take out the array!”

Vice Creed Leader Liu pulled out an array from his storage ring and laid it on the ground. Instantly, the flies fled the barbeque shop.

Since those who opened shops in the Dao-Seeking Sect were not mortals, using storage rings and arrays wouldn’t raise suspicions.

Vice Creed Leader Liu smilingly explained, “Cleanliness is guaranteed! This is a Pest-Repelling Array we brought from outside.” He was always rigorous with his work.

While one hand flipped and shook the lamb skewers, the other sprinkled seasoning with a rub of his fingertips. When the seasoning landed on the lamb skewers, the meaty aroma ignited by the charcoal fire was so irresistible that it could make one’s teeth fall out.

Vice Creed Leader Liu’s practiced skill appeared to be no less impressive than Lu Yang's.

The seven of us had specifically sought out the best local barbeque master and toiled through three grueling days to learn it—all for this moment!

“Do you like it spicy?”

Shangguan Yu thought for a bit. She couldn’t handle much spice, but not having spice would feel like something was missing. “Mild spiciness then.”[1]”

“Gotcha!”

As Vice Creed Leader Liu continued grilling the skewers, he began calling out to draw in potential customers. “Come and take a look! Fresh tender lamb from the grasslands, slaughtered on the spot! Juicy meat, chewy tendons, and an unforgettable savory taste!”

This was a catchphrase they had learned from their mortal barbeque shifu. He had even advised them that the louder they shouted, the more customers they could attract. Perhaps it was because they had heard their barbeque master yell it so many times that Vice Creed Leader Liu couldn’t help but shout it out himself as he got lost in the moment.

It was indeed effective. One after another, disciples of the Dao-Seeking Sect gathered around.

“Here, your skewers.” Vice Creed Leader Liu handed the lamb skewers to Shangguan Yu.

“How much is it?”

How would Vice Creed Leader Liu know how much it cost? He glanced at the price list on the wall and got quite a fright.

Are prices in the Dao-Seeking Sect so high?

What Vice Creed Leader Liu didn’t know was that prices in the Dao-Seeking Sect were usually not this high; they were temporarily hiked up because of the event.

Shangguan Yu took a small bite. The rich aroma of the meat permeated her senses as the juice flowed throughout her mouth, preventing her from distinguishing between her saliva and the juices.

“Delicious, delicious! Give me fifty more skewers! And two roasted pig trotters.”

The best part about eating as a cultivator was that they would never feel full no matter how much they ate. As long as there was something they wanted to eat, they could eat it to their heart’s content.

Naturally, there was no chance for them to make use of this special trait during the banquet prepared by the Everlasting Immortal Fairy.

When the people around Shangguan Yu saw her eating so blissfully, they couldn’t help but drool and begin clamoring for skewers.

Vice Creed Leader Gao called out from inside the shop. “There’s space inside, plenty of space! Everyone, don’t crowd outside. You can come in and place your orders!”

The five guest elders also quickly got to work and received the customers.

At the Martial Plaza, the first match of the Golden Core category had just finished, and there was still some time until the second match. Many disciples from both sects decided that they could eat while spectating the matches.

They noticed a barbeque shop that stood out as its business was unusually good.

“Let’s go check it out.”

As more and more disciples came over to order their skewers, Vice Creed Leader Liu felt imbued with unprecedented self-confidence. “Didn’t I previously say that it’s no big deal for Lu Yang and the other two to open a barbeque shop in Yanjiang Commandery? That’s because I haven’t shown my hand yet. If I had stepped in, what business would Lu Yang have?”

“Old Gao, there are too many orders! I can’t handle them all, you set up a booth too!”

“Alright!”

Surprisingly, Vice Creed Leader Gao’s barbecue skills were no less impressive than Vice Creed Leader Liu’s!

~~~

At the spectator stand, Lu Yang delivered the skewers to Yun Zhi, only to be met with an astonished look from Qiu Jin’an.

Why did Sect Leader Lu end up selling skewers? It hasn’t been that long. What happened during this time? Qiu Jin’an couldn’t make sense of it.

Yun Zhi asked, “How’s the preparation going?”

“There are only seven customers left in the shop. According to the plan, there will be disciples going there to place their orders, so there shouldn’t be any accidents.”

“Got it, you may go back.”

Before leaving, Lu Yang took a glance at the Martial Plaza. The second match had just begun, and representing the Dao-Seeking Sect was Yi Jing, also someone the Everlasting Immortal Fairy had challenged.

That was when he noticed the disciples in the audience holding many skewers and was taken aback. Even Bai Ming had grabbed a big bunch of skewers and was digging into them merrily despite having just lost.

What on earth is going on?

~~~

By the time Lu Yang returned to the barbeque shop, Meng Jingzhou and Man Gu were already back. In fact, they were busy assisting the two vice creed leaders.

The people who were secretly assigned to buy the skewers couldn’t even join in the line. When they saw Lu Yang, they could only shrug helplessly.

Second Elder was eating by the roadside, his mouth full of grease. Upon seeing Lu Yang, he beckoned him over. “Where did you find these people? Their barbecue skills are top-notch.”

Beside him was Shangguan Yu. She also mentioned that she had to come by the Dao-Seeking Sect more often.

Lu Yang, “...”

“Excuse me, please let me through!” Lu Yang hollered, wanting to go inside to check on the situation.

Someone he had just jostled against frowned. “What’s with the pushing? Don’t you know how to queue?!”

“I’m a shop assistant!”

When the person saw that it was Lu Yang, he could only twitch his mouth and make way for Lu Yang. He suddenly remembered his shifu reminding him that there would be diabolic creed members infiltrating the exchange event and that Lu Yang was preparing to catch them in one fell swoop.

Don’t tell me that the people in this barbeque shop are from the diabolic creed?

He stared at the two vice creed leaders for a long time as they grilled the skewers. Finally, he concluded that his speculation was probably wrong.

The elders of the Dao-Seeking Sect had already made the relevant arrangements with everyone, informing them not to panic when they see Lu Yang in places he shouldn’t be and to pretend not to recognize him.

When Vice Creed Leader Liu saw that Lu Yang was back, he was overjoyed. “Little Lu, you’re back! Just in time! Go maintain order and get everyone to line up properly.”

Lu Yang, “...”

Do you still remember what you are here for?

Lu Yang’s original plan was to find a few customers to stall them, but he hadn’t expected the barbeque shop to become so popular. When he noticed a sincere smile on Man Gu’s countenance as he worked and the nostalgic expression on Meng Jingzhou’s visage as he reminisced about Yanjiang Commandery, he didn’t even know how to let out the pent-up expletives.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy nodded in satisfaction. “As expected of my followers. Their self-reliance skills are acceptable. It’s just that their barbecue skills could use some improvement.”

“Lu Yang, let me control you. I’ll demonstrate to you what an immortal-tier barbeque skewers look like. Remember to take notes.”

She was in high spirits and couldn’t be bothered about how ‘techniques could not be passed on lightly’ as she eagerly insisted on showing off her skills.

Hearing what she just said, Lu Yang was so frightened that he hastily stopped the Everlasting Immortal Fairy. “Please don’t make things worse!”

1. Weila is a common term to ask for just a bit of spiciness in China. ☜

Chapter 173: This Thing Seems to Be More Profitable Than Working in the Everlasting Creed

As night fell, the cultivators began yearning for a pleasant and relaxing meal.

Just a street away from the Martial Plaza was a seemingly inconspicuous small shop, but the fragrant aroma that wafted into people’s nostrils alone was sufficient to draw people of all backgrounds there—One More Time Barbeque Shop.

Just like the name suggested, customers who had eaten there once wanted to come here one more time to satisfy their stomachs that could never be filled.

Most of the customers patronized the shop for their Barbarian Tribe’s special lamb, a timeless barbeque recipe that had been passed down in the tribe for hundreds of thousands of years.

The barbeque recipe had to be prepared fresh each day. The ancestors of the Barbarian Tribe had their own insights into roasting and seasoning beef and lamb. This was precisely the reason for the subtle differences in taste across the dozens of barbeque shops in the Dao-Seeking Sect.

However, Chef Liu, who also served as the vice creed leader of the Everlasting Creed, held a different opinion. He believed that the best ingredient should be cooked with the simplest methods. When it came to barbecuing skewers, the key was still heat control and the heart behind it.

Every time Chef Liu grilled the skewers, he would view it as a battle, giving his utmost effort and never slacking off. Even when the orders piled up like mountains, Chef Liu maintained his composure and meticulously controlled the fire, immersed in his own world.

Eating was like war; this was an unchanging truth since ancient times. For a barbeque shop to perform well, it naturally required the cooperation of its support staff.

Although the support staff of One More Time Barbeque Shop were temporary workers who had never worked with something like this before, they seemed to be born for this job. When serving the customers, they worked seamlessly as if their hearts were connected. One would do the accounting, while the other would work on cleaning the dishes. Their coordination was so impeccable that they resembled biological siblings.

However, there was no perfect shop in the world. No matter how well they collaborated, there would always be someone distracted and lost in daydreaming.

“Little Lu, what’s wrong with you? Can you be more focused on your work?!” Chef and Vice Creed Leader Liu reprimanded Lu Yang.

Lu Yang, “...”

Was I too rash in becoming the creed founder? The Everlasting Creed doesn’t look like it has a future. I should just obediently stay as a disciple of the Dao-Seeking Sect.

“You want to leave the creed?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy shot Lu Yang an unfriendly glare. You sure have guts to be speaking of leaving the creed in front of me.

“Immortal Fairy, do you need anything? If not, you can just go back to sleep.”

“Of course, I need something. Go tell Little Gao that his method of grilling the skewers is wrong. The meat is too soft. They need a stronger flame to obtain that charred aroma.

“Quick, go tell him. This is an order from an immortal,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy urged.

In ancient times, people would regard whatever she said seriously. They treated it as an immortal revelation and would analyze her words from all kinds of angles.

However, she received no such treatment now. Lu Yang acted as if didn’t even hear her words at all.

Man Gu secretly approached Lu Yang, his face plagued with worry. “Brother Lu, things can’t go on like this.”

Lu Yang was elated. Has someone finally realized the problem?

“We didn’t prepare enough skewers. If things go on like this, they will sell out very quickly!”

Lu Yang didn’t know what to say, and he began to reflect. To think I expected anything from Man Gu... Does the problem lie with my head or Man Gu’s head?

“What? There are hardly any skewers left?!” A higher-up of the Everlasting Creed looked grim. This is no small matter. Jiang Yitian was responsible for handling the accounts. “Quickly go buy some more from outside then!”

Man Gu shook his head. “The skewers are marinated in advance. If we buy meat now, not only is the quality not guaranteed, but there is also not enough time to marinate them.” As a member of the Ancient Barbarian Tribe, Man Gu was adamant about not tarnishing their reputation.

“He has strong principles!” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy praised. In ancient times, she had also eaten the barbeque from the Barbarian Tribe. The taste was indeed top-notch, but the issue is that they didn’t pay attention to nutritional balance.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy always placed emphasis on nutritional balance in her cooking, so she offered some constructive suggestions to the Barbarian Tribe. However, they refused to listen and remained firm in their stance.

By the time the contest at the Martial Plaza neared the end of the Nascent Soul category, the skewers were all sold out.

Everyone began reflecting on what they had gained today.

“Damn it! Aren’t we here to cause trouble for the Dao-Seeking Sect? What are you all doing? Playing house?!” Vice Creed Leader Liu displayed his authority first. Despite realizing that he had been engrossed in barbecuing and delayed their official matters, he couldn’t admit to his mistake in front of everyone.

As expected of the vice creed leader of a diabolic creed, he was born for evil deeds and had wielded mastery over the art of “the thief crying thief first.”

Vice Creed Leader Gao also chastised everyone, “Where are your opinions? With how inattentive you are with your mission, are you living up to the Everlasting Immortal’s expectations?!”

Everyone thought to themselves, Weren't you two the most caught up in the excitement just now?

Jiang Yitian, who had been managing the accounts for the whole day, pondered for a moment and asked in a serious tone, “Is it too late for us to switch to opening a barbeque shop now?”

Another higher-up raised his eyebrow. “What do you mean? Open a barbeque shop? Are you going to abandon your faith in the Everlasting Immortal?!”

“But opening a barbeque shop in the Dao-Seeking Sect is really lucrative.”

The higher-up was disdainful. “How lucrative could it be?”

“It’s worth one month of offerings.”

The higher-up now lowered his head in contemplation. “We could worship the Everlasting Immortal’s statue while running a barbeque shop on the side. It doesn’t seem to contradict the creed’s precepts.”

Vice Creed Leader Liu berated him for lacking conviction. “This is simply nonsense! As loyal followers of the Everlasting Immortal, how could we have someone like you...”

“It’s worth one month of everyone’s offerings summed up.”

“Someone like you is a blessing for the Everlasting Creed!” Vice Creed Leader Liu immediately changed what he was originally going to say and began planning for the future. “We can open chain stores across the entire continent. Not only can it solve the creed’s employment problem, it can also rake in money for us. Eventually, we will be a rich taxpayer in the Great Xia Dynasty!”

Vice Creed Leader Liu was furious. “Have you not thought about whether the prices elsewhere will be as outrageous as those in the Dao-Seeking Sect? How can one’s spending level during a holiday be the same as on normal days? You are only looking at the immediate profits and not thinking about the long run! Most importantly, if we open chain stores, who can guarantee that the skills of every follower will be as good as ours?!

“Prepare to set off. We are heading to the Martial Plaza!”

Lu Yang sighed inwardly. The original plan was to have the customers stall them and give them another chance. Unfortunately, the skewers sold out too quickly and couldn’t last until the event ended.

“Specific positioning is required for the Yellow Millet Dream Pillow to unleash its full potential. Little Lu, you three take us to the Martial Plaza for reconnaissance. When the time is ripe, we will activate the immortal treasure. You will be great contributors then!”

Lu Yang bowed slightly with a solemn expression, adopting the stance of a hero’s selfless self-sacrifice. “We seek no accolades. Dedicating ourselves to the Everlasting Creed is our duty!”

“Good, I knew I wasn’t wrong about you!” Vice Creed Leader Liu was very pleased with Lu Yang. No wonder the creed leader highly values him. He definitely has his merits.

The creed founder of the Everlasting Creed led his subordinates to the Martial Plaza and spread out into their positions.

When Vice Creed Leader Liu saw the battle on the stage, he nodded slightly. As expected of disciples from the Five Great Immortal Sects. Although their cultivation isn’t high, their combat methods are worthy of praise. I can’t really pick anything to critique.

He told the great creed founder, “Little Lu, observe these battles closely. They will be very helpful for you.”

Chapter 174: Take Action!

The fifth match of the Nascent Soul category was nearing its end, and the representative from the Dao-Seeking Sect was Ma Tianyang, also someone the Everlasting Immortal Fairy had challenged.

Vice Creed Leader Liu provided his appraisal. “This person called Ma Tianyang is at the Advanced Nascent Soul Stage, whereas his opponent from the Dao-Seeking Sect is at the Apex Nascent Soul Stage. Both are disciples of immortal sects with similar resources. External factors don’t matter now. It’s a contest of their cultivation. A subtle difference in cultivation is the determining factor of the outcome. Ma Tianyang is not far from losing.”

Just as Vice Creed Leader Liu had predicted, Ma Tianyang gradually fell into a disadvantageous position, while his opponent became increasingly bold, and resolved to defeat Ma Tianyang in one final blow.

Ma Tianyang was a talisman cultivator, and the myriad talismans he crafted were considered the finest and most premium products in the outside world. If a small clan purchased them, they could even enshrine it as an ancestral treasure which can deliver a fatal blow in critical moments and secure the clan’s survival.

Unfortunately, Ma Tianyang’s opponent was a cultivator who wielded lightning and thunder. The deafening booms of thunder moved at peak speed, and every bolt of lightning precisely disrupted Ma Tianyang’s attempts to draw the talismans, preventing him from leveraging the strengths of a talisman cultivator.

Just when his opponent assumed that victory was assured and followed up with an attack, he saw Ma Tianyang suddenly slamming his palms down on the ground. Countless runes flickered, forming a towering mountain that suppressed him.

Pinned beneath the mountain, his opponent could not mobilize any spirit energy. He couldn’t figure out why he had lost. “Crushing-Weight Mountain Talisman! This talisman cannot be stored on paper and must be drawn on-site. Even you would need five minutes to draw it. How did you get the time to do that?”

Ma Tianyang snorted. “I have been drawing it all this time. You simply didn’t see it.”

“How is that possible?! Where did you draw it?”

Ma Tianyang pointed at himself. “Blood vessels.

“While I was fighting with you, I was constantly adjusting the position of my blood vessels.”

“I @#¥%...”

The arrays at the Martial Plaza were comprehensive and considerate in their designs. It even had an array that could automatically censor profanities. To outsiders, all they could hear was a series of beeping sounds.

His opponent thought that after observing the Dao-Seeking Sect for so long, he was about to grasp their line of thought, but he now realized that he was actually far from it.

Vice Creed Leader Liu’s eyelids twitched. I didn’t expect Ma Tianyang to have such a trump card hidden up his sleeves. I was too careless.

The blood contained spirit energy, so adjusting the blood vessels into the shape of a talisman was certainly feasible. In fact, it could also be said to be even more ingenious than drawing talismans outside, for it didn’t incur any loss of spirit energy.

But the problem is, would a normal person ever think of using their blood vessels to draw talismans?!

Vice Creed Leader Liu educated Lu Yang dispassionately, “Don’t learn from this type of fighting style. Blood vessels can easily form blood clots when tied up.”

Lu Yang felt that Vice Creed Leader Liu was overthinking things. He had heard that Ma Tianyang could undo even the most complex knots.

After the Nascent Soul category ended, the Divine Transfiguration category was the final one left.

This was the category with the highest stakes in the exchange event. Watching a battle between Divine Transfiguration cultivators would undoubtedly offer tremendous benefits!

Representing the Dao-Seeking Sect was Lu Wang[1] from the Pill Cauldron Peak, someone Lu Yang had not met before.

Others whispered, “It’s Senior Brother Lu! I haven’t seen him in a long time.”

“I heard that Senior Brother Lu discarded his three Golden Cores from his three attempts because he was very dissatisfied with his first-grade golden core.”

“Why is that?”

“He insisted that a golden core is also a type of pill.[2] If the golden core doesn’t have pill marks or pill fragrance, it’s considered a useless golden core. Hence, he repeatedly formed his golden core, trying to create one with pill fragrance.”

“Did he succeed?”

“He succeeded. Senior Brother Lu really formed a golden core with pill fragrance.”

“What kind of miraculous effects does this kind of golden core have?”

“It’s amazingly fragrant.”

Lu Yang didn’t know how he should react.

He asked his subordinate, “Little Liu, who do you think would win?”

“Huh?” Vice Creed Leader Liu thought he had misheard. What did this kid just call me?

Lu Yang explained calmly, “Your identity here is a temporary staff I have hired, so I am your boss. If we are going to act, we need to see it through. If I’m too respectful toward you, it’ll seem very fake. Our plan is about to be implemented soon. We mustn't slip up now!”

Vice Creed Leader Liu nodded, agreeing with Lu Yang’s point.

“Lu Wang is famous among Divine Transfiguration cultivators. Few are willing to have him as their opponent. He is both a pill and poison cultivator, and his poison skills are stronger than his pill abilities. However, Lu Wang is unlucky to meet an opponent who counters him.

“I have heard about his opponent before. He grew up in the Five Poisons Pit[3] and has long cultivated a body immune to poison. Against him, Lu Wang cannot showcase his full potential.”

As Lu Wang and his opponent from the Five-Elements Sect faced off, he first released a bone-corroding poison mist as a test. However, just like Vice Creed Leader Liu had mentioned, his opponent was not in the least bit afraid. The poison mist had no effect on him.

“This will be a tough one.” Lu Wang felt that the situation was getting tricky.

His opponent snickered, “Lu Wang, just give up. You might win against anyone else, but you will definitely lose to me!”

In a battle among Divine Transfiguration cultivators, they were no longer limited to the ground. Both parties would sometimes fly into the sky and burrow into the ground. Although each side had their strengths and weaknesses, Lu Wang’s opponent possessed more strength, putting Lu Wang at a disadvantage.

Lu Wang whipped out a pill for boosting one’s strength from the front of his robe; this was allowed in the competition.

Just as Lu Wang was about to consume it, his opponent snatched it away and swallowed it instead.

His opponent sneered. “You wanted to ingest a pill? You’ll need the chance to do so first!”

As soon as the pill entered the opponent’s stomach, however, he felt that his strength was plummeting at an alarming rate. “What’s going on?!” He was shocked. This shouldn’t be!

Lu Wang sent him flying with a punch. “It’s the Ten-Elephant Strength Pill. It grants the strength of ten elephants to the user.

“However, this is only for the Foundation Establishment Stage. In other words, you now only have the strength of ten Foundation Establishment elephants.”

“You &%*#...”

“Be glad I didn’t give you the Ten-Elephant Strength Pill Aphrodisiac Version. I have saved your face.” Lu Wang tossed his opponent out of the ring.

Of the four subsequent matches in the Divine Transfiguration category, Vice Creed Leader Liu failed to predict any of the outcomes correctly. It wasn’t because he lacked foresight—the Divine Transfiguration cultivators of the Dao-Seeking Sect had too many ideas beyond one’s imagination.

Vice Creed Leader Liu inhaled two deep breaths and steadied his emotions. The time to take action is drawing near. I can’t let such trivial matters affect my mood.

He noticed that the others had already taken their respective positions, forming the Yellow Millet Dream Array which would maximize the effects of the Yellow Millet Dream Pillow.

According to the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, this was her go-to array for sleeping, and it worked wonderfully.

Vice Creed Leader Liu heard the members of the Dao-Seeking Sect begin their closing remarks. “The friendly exchange event between the Dao-Seeking Sect and the Five-Elements Sect has concluded here. It has been a pleasure spending this wonderful time with everyone...”

Everyone’s attention was on the stage. This is the perfect moment to take action!

Vice Creed Leader Liu raised his hand and hollered, “Take action!”

The disciples from the Dao-Seeking Sect had been lying in ambush around the area. As soon as they heard the code “take action,” they immediately sprang into action and pounced toward the higher-ups of the Everlasting Creed.

They remembered Lu Yang telling them that someone would shout “take action,” and that would be the cue for them to act.

Prior to this, they had been speculating who would issue the command. Some guessed it would be Lu Yang, some guessed it would be Meng Jingzhou, while some guessed it would be Man Gu.

Now, the mystery was finally unraveled.

The Dao-Seeking Sect’s disciples even respectfully nodded in salute to the stunned Vice Creed Leader Liu. What a true hero!

It turns out that Vice Creed Leader Liu has been a spy from our side all along, and he even managed to climb to the position of vice creed leader.

1. The surname “Lu” here is a different one from Lu Yang’s surname. ☜

2. It may not be obvious in the English translation, but golden core is jindan in Chinese, while pills are danyao, and the “dan” in both terms is the same. ☜

3. The Five Poisons or Five Noxious Creatures refer to centipedes, snakes, scorpions, lizards, and toads. ☜

Chapter 175: Tofu Heavenly Sovereign

The higher-ups of the Everlasting Creed were all dumbfounded. They had just chanted their grand phrase in the ancient language when a group of people suddenly burst forth from the crowd and threw burlap sacks over their heads.

We admit we’re unlucky to get bagged and tied up, but why does the Dao-Seeking Sect seem so practiced?

Aren’t you supposed to be a righteous sect?

What they had just recited was in an ancient language that was associated with the immortal treasure, the Yellow Millet Dream Pillow. The words were profound and the content incomprehensible to ordinary people. Even until today, they remain undeciphered. The Everlasting Creed speculated that this was an ancient immortal technique used to activate the immortal treasure, though some theorized that it was an ancient language meant for awakening the immortal treasure.

No matter what the truth was, one thing was certain—pairing the ancient words with the Yellow Millet Dream Pillow would culminate in an unstoppable lethal weapon against those of the same level.

The Everlasting Creed deduced that the Everlasting Immortal was proficient in the laws of Immortal Dao related to dreamscapes. Ancient cultivators who dabbled in poetry ascribed the Everlasting Immortal with the phrase “A grand dream spans thousands of autumns, but what year is it on this night?”

Upon further verification, they discovered that the Qilin Immortal had once said that he wished the Everlasting Immortal would remain in eternal slumber.

The creed leader of the Everlasting Creed had claimed, “This implies that although no clear winner could be determined among the five ancient immortals, the Qilin Immortal must have feared the Everlasting Immortal. That’s why he hoped that the Everlasting Immortal would never awaken!”

Vice Creed Leader Liu shook his head, cutting off his thoughts. It dawned upon him that the Dao-Seeking Sect had come prepared. We have been ensnared in a trap like turtles in a jar.

Who is the traitor?!

Vice Creed Leader Liu suddenly realized that Lu Yang had disappeared from his side without a trace. When he looked up, he saw Lu Yang standing on the stage as he addressed the crowd.

Lu Yang seemed to have noticed Vice Creed Leader Liu’s gaze and met his eyes, flashing a breezy smile before continuing his speech. “Through this exchange, everyone should...”

“It’s you!” Vice Creed Leader Liu’s eyes widened in rage, his pupils almost popping. I never expected Lu Yang to be a traitor.

Did the Dao-Seeking Sect win Lu Yang over to their side?

Wait, that can’t be right. If he can stand on the podium, it means that he has always been part of the Dao-Seeking Sect and perhaps even one of their higher-ups?!

“Heh, Lu Yang, you despicable thief! Did you think that victory is already in your grasp?” Vice Creed Leader Liu’s expression cracked into one of derangement as he planned to burn his boat and cut off all means of retreat.

He took out the immortal treasure, the Yellow Millet Dream Pillow, from his storage ring. “I’ll show you what an immortal treasure truly is! Even if I’m alone, I can activate it!”

Vice Creed Lear Liu spat a mouthful of essence blood onto the Yellow Millet Dream Pillow. It emitted a sinister green light that rippled outward like waves. Wherever the green ripples touched, friend and foe alike fell into a deep sleep. Regardless of whether they were a disciple from the Dao-Seeking Sect, disciples of the Five-Elements Sect, or even the higher-ups of the Everlasting Creed who had been captured, they all swayed under the indiscriminate green ripples, collapsing to the ground with a loud thud. Soon, a cacophony of snores reverberated through the air.

Snore, snore...

The Martial Plaza was supposed to be the central hub of the Dao-Seeking Sect, bustling with activity. However, only the rhythmic snores remained, adding an eerie tinge to the atmosphere.

Even the higher-ups of the Dao-Seeking Sect at the spectator stand succumbed to the power of the Yellow Millet Dream Pillow and were dragged into the dreamscape.

Vice Creed Leader Liu’s breathing had visibly weakened, but he paid no mind to it, laughing maniacally. “Hahaha! Dao-Seeking Sect? Five-Elements Sect? So what! Serves you right for belittling the Everlasting Creed!”

Murderous intent was overflowing from him. He wanted to seize this opportunity to wipe out the disciples of the Dao-Seeking Sect. “I must make haste! If the Transcendent Tribulation cultivators from the Dao-Seeking Sect sense the commotion here, they will surely rush over. Even if I offer my essence blood to the immortal treasure as sacrifice, I won’t be able to withstand the might of a Transcendent Tribulation expert,” Vice Creed Leader Liu mumbled to himself.

Transcendent Tribulation cultivators typically hid themselves in the deepest parts of their sects, guarded secrets, pursued the Immortal Dao, or isolated themselves from the mundane world. Rarely did they intervene and make a move. To his knowledge, among the Five Great Immortal Sects, only the abbot of the Hanging Monastery was at the Transcendent Tribulation Stage. The other four sect leaders were only at the Fusion Stage. The abbot of the Hanging Monastery belonged to the previous generation, while no one in their current generation had achieved the Transcendent Tribulation Stage.

Without any Transcendent Tribulation cultivators around, I am the most powerful with the immortal treasure in my possession!

“What’s this? Trying to kill people in front of this esteemed one?” A derisive voice laced with coldness interrupted Vice Creed Leader Liu’s musings.

The voice sounded familiar. He abruptly looked up and was shocked to see that Lu Yang was still awake!

“How is this possible?!”

Soon, his shock escalated to shocking horror. If Lu Yang wasn’t affected and didn’t fall into slumber, that means he’s a Transcendent Tribulation expert!

Everything makes sense now! That explains why Lu Yang appeared to be at the Foundation Establishment Stage before me but can still hold a position among the higher-ups of the Dao-Seeking Sect.

It must be because Lu Yang’s cultivation far surpasses mine!

“Who on earth are you?!” Vice Creed Leader Liu sternly barked. He has to be a renowned expert to have reached the Transcendent Tribulation Stage. But I can’t seem to match Lu Yang with any such figure.

Lu Yang stood at the spectator stand with his hands behind his back, his white robes billowing in the wind like a sword immortal exiled from the heavens.

With a strong flick of his hem, he leaped down.

“This esteemed one is the Tofu Heavenly Sovereign!”

It was already late at night. Under the moonlight, a figure stood out starkly against the darkness, as if he was heaven and earth’s favored child, the focus of all gazes.

As Lu Yang bathed under the moonlight, he released aura waves that far exceeded that of a Fusion cultivator, forcing Vice Creed Leader Liu to prostrate himself in worship.

“Kismet rises, sword falls.”

A sword ray pierced through the black clouds. A cyan immortal sword descended from the heavens, imbued with the wrath of gods and the indifference of immortals, as if punishing all evil.

Faced with this unparalleled strike from the sword, Vice Creed Leader Liu couldn’t muster even a shred of resistance. It was as though his body had been frozen in place, rendering him unable to budge.

All he could do was raise his head with his eyes wide open, watching helplessly as the cyan immortal sword fell.

The immortal sword pierced through Vice Creed Leader Liu’s head.

“A sword is an inauspicious item. This esteemed one doesn’t wish to kill.”

The Tofu Heavenly Sovereign’s expression was aloof as he turned to leave, leaving the silhouette of his departing figure forever etched in people’s memory.

~~~

In reality, everyone had gathered around to watch Vice Creed Leader Liu sleeping on the ground, where he would occasionally twitch. They were very curious about what kind of dream Lu Yang had woven for him.

All this time, Lu Yang had actually been standing beside Vice Creed Leader Liu, while the person delivering the speech on stage was First Elder.

From the moment Vice Creed Leader Liu noticed that Lu Yang wasn’t by his side, he had already entered the dreamscape.

The Yellow Millet Dream Pillow belonged to the Everlasting Immortal Fairy. After Yun Zhi learned to use it, she activated it remotely through her storage ring and pulled Vice Creed Leader Liu into a deep slumber before getting Lu Yang to weave a dream for him.

As for the other higher-ups, they had genuinely been captured and stuffed into burlap sacks.

“It’s clearly my pillow! Why don’t you let me use it?!” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy wanted to have some fun, but Lu Yang stopped her.

“I’m just testing it for you. It’s been more than three hundred thousand years. It might have spoiled.” Lu Yang claimed the first round of dream-weaving rights, confident that reason stood with him.

“Speaking of which, did you get someone to sing to you when you were using the Yellow Millet Dream Pillow?” Lu Yang recalled the higher-ups of the Everlasting Creed chanting some grand ancient words, as if they were offering sacrifices to some great being. “What were they even singing?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy sieved through her memories for a bit. “It’s the lullaby my toy used to play while I slept. The lyrics go, ‘Sleep, sleep, my dear little baby...’”

The Everlasting Creed’s chanting was of such imposing grandeur that it completely didn’t fit with the mood of a lullaby. It took her a while to connect the dots and figure out what they had been singing.

Lu Yang, “...”

Chapter 176: Shangguan Yu

“Eh, so this is the high-ranking Everlasting Creed member you caught?” A sudden voice from behind Lu Yang startled him. He turned around sharply and saw that it was Shangguan Yu.

“Say, he’s doing great with the barbeque shop, so why did he have to go down the path of joining the diabolic creed?” Shangguan Yu shook her head, relishing the taste of the barbeque skewers that lingered in her memory. She felt sorry for these people.

“In any case, you did a good job. It has been years since someone caught a big shot like this. I wish you the best in extracting useful intelligence from him.” Shangguan Yu patted Lu Yang’s shoulder. “I can tell that you were born to be part of the Dao-Seeking Sect. Keep working hard, I’ve got high hopes for you. Maybe you’ll even surpass the Taciturn Daoist Priest in the future!”

Yun Zhi commented by the side, “Of course, he’ll surpass Shifu.”

Shangguan Yu scratched her head. What I actually meant was that Lu Yang’s wild imagination can surpass the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s. Did Little Yun misunderstand?

Forget it. Explaining will be a hassle.

Lu Yang was about to say something when Shangguan Yu vanished into thin air, leaving him clueless about how she had done it.

~~~

At the spectator stand, First Elder was maintaining order. “Everyone, please do not panic. It’s just a few Fusion cultivators from a diabolic creed ambushing us with an immortal treasure. There’s nothing to worry about.”

He wore an expression that read, “This is a very common occurrence in the Dao-Seeking Sect. You folks from the Five-Elements Sect haven’t seen something like this before, right? These kinds of people don’t get to stir up any waves here.”

Qiu Jin’an could swear that First Elder was showing off to him.

If a similar incident happened in the Five-Elements Sect, we would certainly go into full security mode. How could we be like the Dao-Seeking Sect and still be in the mood to tease others?

You guys really have nerves of steel, huh.

“From the Everlasting Creed?” Qiu Jin’an recalled that Yun Zhi knew some secrets about the Everlasting Creed.

Fusion Stage? That has to be minimally at the vice creed leader level. The Dao-Seeking Sect has caught a big fish this time.

Qiu Jin’an couldn’t help but be envious. If they dig deep into this big fish, they’re bound to uncover plenty of good things.

Why does the Dao-Seeking Sect always encounter good stuff like this?!

“Verily, it is so,” First Elder replied in an archaic and genteel manner.

Qiu Jin’an suppressed the urge to give First Elder a beating as he tried to suggest, “The Five Great Immortal Sects should unite against a common adversary. Whatever intel you acquire, do share it with us too.”

First Elder was unruffled. “That’s easy. All you need to do is admit that the Five-Elements Sect is inferior to the Dao-Seeking Sect and that you are our little brother. As the big brother, we’ll naturally be happy to share any intel with you.”

“Qin Jiunian, you’re going too far! Among the Dao-Seeking Nine, the only one I can’t beat is the Taciturn Daoist Priest!” Qiu Jin’an slammed the table and stretched with the sounds of his joints popping.

First Elder scoffed and snapped his fingers. From Second Elder to Eighth Elder, all the elders appeared behind him, fanning out like a peacock spreading its tail.

A horrifying aura suffocated Qiu Jin’an.

Sixth Elder is here.

First Elder flashed a smug smile. Just as he was about to speak, he realized that he couldn’t utter a single word.

He transmitted an auditory message to Sixth Elder helplessly. “Sixth Junior Sister, when will you finally be able to control your celestial physique?”

Sixth Elder rolled her eyes. “Be content. Of all those with an Immaculate Celestial Physique in history, my control over it is the best. The last recorded person with an Immaculate Celestial Physique was Chi Qianqian. After she reached the Fusion Stage, her body began automatically repelling the surrounding spirit qi, causing her to give up on cultivation entirely.”

Evidently, celestial physiques were not without downsides.

With the interlude from Sixth Elder, First Elder lost interest in mocking QIu Jin’an.

Sixth Elder tactfully left. The closing ceremony was still ongoing. If she stayed any longer, First Elder and Qiu Jin’an wouldn’t even be able to deliver their closing speeches.

In this competition between the Five-Elements Sect and the Dao-Seeking Sect, the former suffered a disastrous defeat.

The disciples of the Five-Elements Sect were no fragile flowers sheltered in a greenhouse. They had exterminated their fair share of demons and devils and also mingled with the common folk for the sake of their missions. Both their combat and life experiences were extensive.

However, they had truly never encountered fighting styles similar to the Dao-Seeking Sect. It was so unpredictable that all their experience was useless.

Even for the few matches they won against them, it was because the disciples of the Dao-Seeking Sect had indirectly gone mad.

For instance, during one of the Golden Core matches, the disciple of the Dao-Seeking Sect started out ferociously, completely different from his usual self. Just when his opponent from the Five-Elements Sect was about to crumble under the pressure, the Dao-Seeking Sect disciple suddenly collapsed in exhaustion.

In his last moments, he told the referee, “This is a do-or-die battle... Before the match, I ingested a poisonous pill... It takes effect in five minutes... I’ll only take the antidote after I get off the stage... If I can’t defeat my opponent in five minutes...only death awaits...I...I can’t hold on any longer... How I wish I could win...”

The referee saw that the person was on the brink of death, but he didn’t have any antidote on him, so he quickly took out two of the same poison pills, extending his life by ten minutes. He then rushed offstage to find the antidote and eventually managed to save him.

After both First Elder and Qiu Jin’an hypocritically recited their closing speeches and bid farewell with reluctance, others could see that the Five Great Immortal Sects had a steadfast bond, a far cry from the rumors in the outside world that the Dao-Seeking Sect isolated the other four sects.
