“Of course, of course. If the opportunity arises, I’ll definitely come to visit the Dao-Seeking Sect again to enrich my learning.”

At the same time, both of them inwardly cursed, Finally, I don’t have to see this old codger anymore.

However, Second Elder was genuine when he spoke to Shangguan Yu. “Come look for me if you get bullied in the Five-Elements Sect. I have seen Qiu Jin’an grow up. He may look proper, but he’s actually a bad egg. Don’t get fooled by him!”

Shangguan Yu tittered and said that Qiu Jin’an wouldn’t dare to deceive her.

Second Elder’s heart was aching, telling her that it was because she was too innocent that Qiu Jin’an could deceive her.

Qiu Jin’an stepped in between the two, his face stormy enough that it could almost produce rain. “Old Two Ba, I’ve told you before to stay away from her!”

Second Elder shrugged nonchalantly. “Don’t try to scare me. The outside world has been spreading that Shangguan Yu is your younger half-sister. I have already asked around. You are the only son, which means you have no sisters.

“We’ve all grown up together, we know each other well enough. You also don’t have a fiancée. Shangguan Yu has nothing to do with you. Who are you to stop me?!”

Qiu Jin’an exploded in anger. “She’s my mother!”

Second Elder was not one to back down. “Even if she is your mother... Huh? What did you say?” He had retorted out of instinct, but halfway through, he realized something was wrong.

How did courting a girlfriend turn into a conversation about a mother?

First Elder and the others took a few steps back. Perhaps it was because they had been beaten too often as children that they had an instinctive reverence toward those from the previous generation and an impulsive desire to distance themselves.

The disciples of the Five-Elements Sect reacted even more strongly—one of the Five Great Mysteries of the Five-Elements Sect had finally been solved.

“No wonder the cultivation world always says that you can’t judge one’s age by their appearance. It’s indeed true!”

“I remember someone came knocking to propose marriage, and the sect leader kicked him out with an expression that could kill. Back then, I thought he simply had a sister-complex. I didn’t expect the real reason to be this instead!”

Qiu Jin’an turned to Shangguan Yu, who was watching the spectacle unfold. His voice was filled with helpless frustration. “Mom, you too! You can’t hide your identity just so you can pretend to be young and naive. Do you know how much misunderstanding this has caused?”

Shangguan Yu felt that her son was being unfilial. “What do you mean I’m pretending to be young? Am I not only eighteen? Besides, what’s wrong with me pretending to be your younger sister? Your father agreed to it!”

“The grass at my dad’s grave is even taller than I am! Did he visit your dream and send you a message?!”

Chapter 177: Yellow Millet Dream Pillow

“The grass at my dad’s grave is taller than me!”

“You’re not that short,” Shangguan Yu mumbled to herself.

After learning of Shangguan Yu’s true identity, Grandpa Ba’s eyes lit up as he patted Qiu Jin’an’s shoulder. “You can call me Old Ba from now on.”

“Get lost!” Qiu Jin’an shook off Grandpa Ba’s hand. As I thought, we can’t dwell in the Dao-Seeking Sect for long. This place has depleted almost all my lifetime of anger.

“Little Qiu, I find it quite fun here. It’s rare for us to come to the Dao-Seeking Sect, so why don’t we stay a few more days,” Shangguan Yu proposed.

Qiu Jin’an dragged Shangguan Yu away without looking back and boarded the flying vessel to depart.

Shangguan Yu was still jabbering on, “Since you were young, I have been teaching you, solve problems without anger, handle matters with composure, carry yourself with steadiness. Look at yourself, you’re all grown up and the sect leader, yet you get angry all the time. That’s not good...”

Qiu Jin’an’s face darkened, though he didn’t answer her.

Shangguan Yu wiped away a tear. “My child has grown up and doesn’t listen to me anymore.”

Qiu Jin’an responded helplessly, “Mom, can you stop acting like a child?”

“What’s wrong with acting like a child? That’s what your dad liked about me.”

“I...” Qiu Jin’an was at a loss for words. He had no idea how his father had taken a liking to his mother back then.

On the flying vessel, Qiu Jin’an assigned everyone their task. “Everyone must write a 2000-word reflection on this visit to the Dao-Seeking Sect. It must incorporate your insights, retrospection, and actionable next steps. Hand it in to me tomorrow!”

Groans instantly filled the air.

~~~

At the entrance of the Dao-Seeking Sect, Grandpa Ba waved goodbye to the flying vessel, his zest waning. “Say, do you think I still have a chance with Shangguan Yu?”

First Elder sized up Grandpa Ba with disdain. “You’re not even as handsome as I am, and you have the nerve to court her?”

Third Elder shared his heartfelt words, “Second Brother, I won’t stop you from changing your seniority to the previous generation, but I’m just afraid that Shifu won’t approve. Shifu oversees the Incarceration Peak, so he probably wouldn’t mind having one more person there.”

The elders adhered to the tradition of “when a brother has fallen down a well, hurl stones at him instead.” All of them were not about to help out their brother in times of trouble and instead advised Grandpa Ba not to give up on his life.

“Get lost, all of you!” Grandpa Ba shouted angrily. What kind of brothers do I have? None of them can say anything nice.

“Come on, let’s go and see the Everlasting Creed’s higher-ups we have caught,” First Elder reminded everyone what the priority was.

~~~

At the Martial Plaza, the disciples of the Dao-Seeking Sect had congregated around the higher-ups from the Everlasting Creed, pointing and whispering as if they were viewing a menagerie of rare animals.

However, they actually hadn’t captured all of them—two branch leaders and the creed founder were still at large, disguised as disciples of the Dao-Seeking Sect.

Lu Yang inspected the Yellow Millet Dream Pillow in his hand with much curiosity. It was his first time seeing an immortal treasure.

The Yellow Millet Dream Pillow was made of bluish-green porcelain. A blooming cyan lotus was painted on it with a colorful glaze.

“This is the immortal treasure, the Yellow Millet Dream Pillow, Little Lu had mentioned?” First Elder and the others arrived, equally intrigued with the immortal treasure.

“Let me examine it.” First Elder took the pillow. He was an expert in dreamscapes, so he was particularly excited about such treasures that could forcefully induce sleep in people.

He tried infusing a wisp of spirit energy to activate the Yellow Millet Dream Pillow. However, the spirit energy was like a stone sinking into the deep sea, and there was no response from the pillow.

“Interesting.” First Elder was even more curious about how the pillow could be activated.

Yun Zhi parted her lips, wanting to tell First Elder how to use it, but seeing how elated he was, she closed her mouth again. Maybe it’s better to let First Elder figure it out on his own.

First Elder exhausted every method he could think of, but they all ended in failure, and he became somewhat frustrated. “How on earth do you use this thing?”

Vice Creed Leader Liu, also currently a prisoner, laughed derisively. “Fools! This is an immortal item from my creed. How could mere plebeians like you be qualified to use it?”

As First Elder continued to analyze the pillow, Vice Creed Leader Liu ridiculed him, while the other five higher-ups would occasionally snicker sarcastically.

Finally, First Elder couldn’t take it anymore. He grabbed the porcelain pillow and hit Vice Creed Leader Gao, putting him into a peaceful sleep.

“So that’s how you use this immortal treasure,” First Elder murmured pensively. I finally know how to use the Yellow Millet Dream Pillow.

Yun Zhi also couldn’t take it anymore. She reminded him, “First Elder, use your spirit energy thread to create a cyan lotus on the back of the pillow, just like the one at the front. That will activate it.”

“I see, so that’s how it works.”

First Elder followed her instructions and drew the exact cyan lotus on the back of the pillow, then hit another higher-up from the Everlasting Creed with the pillow, putting that person into a peaceful sleep.

“It’s pretty useful.”

First Elder returned the pillow to Lu Yang. The latter followed the same instructions, but nothing happened.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy mocked, “With your mere Foundation Establishment cultivation, you think you can activate my immortal treasure?”

Out of options, Lu Yang could only pass the pillow to Yun Zhi.

Yun Zhi formed a seal with just one hand, and the sigil gradually sank into the Yellow Millet Dream Pillow. Once the sigil disappeared, she handed the pillow back to First Elder.

“First Elder, you are the most adept at dreamscapes in our sect. This item can reach its full potential in your hands. I have left an imprint on the pillow so that I can chase it back even if someone else steals it.”

First Elder was stunned and delighted. He thanked Yun Zhi earnestly. This is an incredibly precious immortal treasure. With this item, my combat power can be elevated to a whole new level.

I’m already the most powerful among the Fusion Stage. Now that I have this immortal treasure, I will be invincible at the Fusion Stage. Even the Taciturn Daoist Priest will have to be careful!

Yun Zhi also told First Elder to remember an ancient phrase he should recite when using the Yellow Millet Dream Pillow, claiming that it could enhance its power.

First Elder was curious and asked Yun Zhi if she knew the meaning of this ancient phrase.

Yun Zhi’s expression morphed into a strange one as she told First Elder that he was better off not knowing what it meant.

Lu Yang asked the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, “Speaking of which, why is your pillow called the Yellow Millet Dream Pillow? Is it because you fell asleep on this pillow while making millet porridge and lived through your entire life in your dream, only to realize that the millet porridge still wasn’t cooked when you woke up?” Lu Yang remembered a certain legend.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy nodded. “You’re pretty close.

“When the pillow was first crafted, I invited the Heaven Mandate Immortal and the others over for a meal, and the main dish was millet porridge. As my mind was occupied by something else, the millet porridge bubbled and almost boiled over.

“At that moment, I suddenly remembered the Nine-Layers Immortal once saying to throw porcelain shards into boiling liquid to prevent it from bubbling. I didn’t have porcelain shards on hand, but I did have this porcelain pillow, so I tossed it into the millet porridge. When I fished it out, the pillow was covered in millet porridge, and that’s why it is named the Yellow Millet Dream Pillow.”

Lu Yang, “...”

How does that have anything to do with what I guessed?

“Then after you threw it in, did it still spill over?” Lu Yang was intrigued about how the whole thing played out.

“It stopped.”

Just as Lu Yang was about to comment that the method seemed really reliable, he heard the Everlasting Immortal Fairy continue. “But I used too much strength and smashed the pot.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy still looked shaken from the trauma. “Fortunately, the Heaven Mandate Immortal and others stood me up. Otherwise, we would have no main course, and it would have been very embarrassing.”

It’s said that immortals possess the ability to focus on the benefits and avoid the negatives. The rumors are indeed not groundless.

Chapter 178: This Immortal’s Name Is Huang Doudou

“Let’s go to Incarceration Peak and interrogate them to find out where the Everlasting Creed’s headquarters are.” Yun Zhi curled her finger, and those from the Everlasting Creed lost control of their bodies, floating in the air as they trailed behind Yun Zhi.

After some thought, she also called Lu Yang over. “You come along too. You might come in useful.”

In just a few days, Lu Yang found himself at Incarceration Peak once again.

The atmosphere at Incarceration Peak was as heavy and oppressive as usual.

In one of the prison cells, Lu Yang saw the Blood Devil Venerable Lord, the ancient Transcendent Tribulation cultivator from the Three-Tenets Cave Domain. All that remained of him was his soul, completely stripped of the defiance he once had. When he heard Yun Zhi’s footsteps, he cowered in the corner of his cell, trembling non-stop.

On the other hand, Yun Zhi didn’t even spare him a glance when she walked past.

The white-haired child feigned an elderly demeanor as he welcomed Yun Zhi and Lu Yang. “Little Yun, you’re here again. Who did you bring this time?”

By now, Lu Yang knew that the white-haired child was the previous sect leader, Tang Shengyi.

“Two vice creed leaders and five higher-ups from the Everlasting Creed.”

“Dang, those are all big shots. Did you wipe out their lair or something?” Tang Shengyi was stunned. This grand-disciple of mine is truly built different.

“They all walked into the trap themselves.”

Right then, Vice Creed Leaders Liu and Gao woke up and began cursing out when they heard Yun Zhi’s words.

“Despicable Dao-Seeking Sect! It was clearly you who tricked me into coming here.”

“What an elaborate scheme! You sent a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator, Tofu Heavenly Sovereign, to go undercover in the Everlasting Creed and gain our trust!”

Evidently, Vice Creed Leader Liu was still not fully awake.

Vice Creed Leader Gao whispered, “Wake up. What’s this Tofu Heavenly Sovereign?”

Vice Creed Leader Liu was a bit dazed. “Isn’t that Lu Yang?”

Yun Zhi stared at Lu Yang silently. She was now curious about what kind of dream Lu Yang had weaved for the vice creed leader.

Lu Yang cleared his throat, embarrassed to say the contents of the dream out loud. Instead, he changed the subject. “Let’s quickly question them. What tools do you need? Chili water, a tiger bench, or a whip soaked in water?”[1]

The two vice creed leaders had been in the diabolic creed for several centuries, if not millennia, and were all ruthless individuals. Ordinary interrogation and torture methods wouldn’t cause them to bat even an eyelid.

“Heh, young man, did you think that using such methods would make us disclose our creed’s secrets? Impossible!”

“The righteous path are ignorant fools to stop us from reviving the Everlasting Immortal. With the impending return of the Ancient Great Era, who will protect us if we don’t resurrect the Everlasting Immortal?!”

“Exterminating demons and devils, you say? You make it sound so noble! Yet you fail to realize that it is precisely such actions that will doom humanity’s future!”

The vice creed leaders took turns mocking the righteous path.

“No need for all that hassle just yet.” Yun Zhi held Lu Yang back. She asked the white-haired child to leave, then turned to Lu Yang. “Immortal Fairy, come out and meet your followers.”

An ethereal fairy-like maiden appeared from Lu Yang, her bare dainty feet hovering over the ground and the hem of her dress fluttering in the air. Her eyes were bright and her teeth pearly white. Her entire being exuded the graceful demeanor of an otherworldly immortal.

“Are the two of you my followers?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s expression was cold, her gaze as placid as an ancient well. The way she looked at the two vice creed leaders was no different from observing mere insects.

On the Central Continent, Fusion cultivators were considered puissant figures. Within sects, they were revered as ancestors; within the court, they held high offices; and in the jianghu, they were mysterious legends. Yet, before an immortal, none of that mattered.

“Who are you?!” the two vice creed leaders shouted, trying to mask their panic with their volume.

For some reason, the moment they saw this celestial-like maiden, the impulse to prostrate in worship would surge through them.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy chuckled nonchalantly. “This esteemed one is the Everlasting Immortal Fairy.”

“Everlasting Immortal Fairy?” Hearing how she referred to herself, their hearts rattled with unease.

Why does the title sound so similar to the Everlasting Immortal? Is it a coincidence?

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy continued, “You have been deceived. There has never been an Everlasting Immortal. It has always been only this esteemed one, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy. Someone feared my resurrection and attempted to use this laughable title of “Everlasting Immortal” to bury my existence. ”

“How benighted and risible. The world lacks no fools who believe the rumors spread by the mastermind behind the scenes. Fortunately, the Dao-Seeking Sect bears the will of heaven, and someone with great fortune bore the karma of resurrecting me. They called forth my true name and brought me back to life.”

The two vice creed leaders felt a chill running down their spines. What they had just heard was an alarming amount of information. What did she mean by “there has never been an Everlasting Immortal?” Feared the Everlasting Immortal Fairy? And what does she mean by “the Dao-Seeking Sect bears the will of heaven” and “someone with great fortune?”

The more they ruminated on the details, the more terrifying it became.

“So, are you saying that who we have been worshiping all this time is not the Everlasting Immortal but you?” Vice Creed Leader Liu looked up at the divine-looking Everlasting Immortal Fairy, his heart filled with trepidation and unease.

“That’s right, you have been deceived. I am not a bloodthirsty killer. The rumor about me taking pleasure in slaughter is baseless nonsense.” She tried to guide them, “Correcting one’s mistakes is a great virtue. If you tell this cultivator Yun Zhi the location of the Everlasting Creed’s headquarters now, there is still a chance to redeem yourselves.”

Vice Creed Leader Gao suddenly asked, “Immortal Fairy, can you tell us your real immortal name?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy nodded, stating her name in a measured manner, “This immortal’s name is Huang Doudou.”

The two vice creed leaders immediately grew agitated.

“I knew it! You’re a liar sent by the Dao-Seeking Sect! How could a dignified immortal have a name like that? It’s obvious that you made it up on the spot!”

“We got you, didn’t we?! Huang Doudou? Does your family make tofu[2] or something?”

A spine-tingling aura emanated from the Everlasting Immortal Fairy.

If a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator were present, they would immediately recognize that the aura was beyond that of a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator, revealing her identity right away.

Unfortunately, the two vice creed leaders were only at the Fusion Stage. Mount Tai was in front of them, but they failed to recognize it; they only knew that the aura surpassed that of a Fusion cultivator, unaware that it was unique to immortals.

Yun Zhi softly conciliated the Everlasting Immortal Fairy. “Senior Immortal Fairy, there’s no need to get angry. Having you appear was just a last-ditch effort. Since they don’t recognize you, I’ll just have to use a few of my own methods to make them reveal the location of their headquarters.”

Only then did the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s expression look better as she returned to Lu Yang’s body.

Yun Zhi then told Lu Yang, “My methods will be a bit harsher this time. You are still young, so it’s better not to watch.”

Heeding Yun Zhi’s advice, Lu Yang shuddered as he obediently left Incarceration Peak.

~~~

On the way back, Lu Yang kindly tried to placate the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, complimenting that her name actually sounded very nice and cute.

“Really?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s spirits were lifted. It was rare for someone to compliment her name.

“Yes, really!” Lu Yang nodded repeatedly.

He looked up at the moon in the sky and suddenly remembered something. “By the way, I wonder what time it is now. Is it already the next day?”

Just then, they heard the sound of laughter from nearby.

“Junior Brother Lu, you have asked a good question. What a coincidence! The time of the rat has just passed, and it is already the next day!”

In other words, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy was no longer the acting sect leader.

Ma Tianyang grinned sinisterly. “Junior Brother Lu, did you enjoy your three days as acting sect leader? I heard that you possess the aura of a celestial being and have the ability to battle opponents beyond your level. I’d like to consult you and see for myself.”

Ma Tianyang grabbed Lu Yang like he was carrying a little chick and took him to the arena.

Word spread that Lu Yang was here, and more and more senior disciples rushed over. The sight of the crowd made Lu Yang’s knees almost buckle.

He glowered at the Everlasting Immortal Fairy in the mental space. “Immortal Fairy, you have to take responsibility for this!”

To think I was consoling the Everlasting Immortal Fairy just a while ago. What a joke! She should be the one consoling me!

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy turned her head away with a guilty conscience.

“This...this is also a part of the trial.”

1. As you would have deduced, these are all used for torture. ☜

2. The “dou” in doufu uses the same “dou“ in Huang Doudou. ☜

Chapter 179: Ancient Mighty Ability: Scatter Dou-Beans For Soldiers

As the pinnacle of the cultivation system, immortals were often associated with terms like unbeatable, apex, and unparalleled.

An immortal’s legacy was considered an even more priceless treasure by the Central Continent. Countless people sought out the legacies of immortals, scouring every trace in hopes of acquiring even the smallest fragments of information about them.

The journey to obtaining an immortal’s legacy was fraught with challenges. One had to grow stronger in the face of strong opponents and become braver with each battle. Being unparalleled at their cultivation stage was the most basic requirement.

In addition, one must also pass the immortal’s trial and satisfy their requests no matter how unreasonable they might be.

This was also something Lu Yang could deeply relate to due to his firsthand experience.

~~~

At the Martial Plaza, the senior disciples took turns battling with Lu Yang. Meanwhile, in the mental space, Lu Yang was chasing the Everlasting Immortal Fairy relentlessly, demanding that she take responsibility.

“Huang Doudou, stop right there! You're the one they’re looking for, so why am I the one getting beaten?!”

“I have already told you, this is an immortal’s trial. I guarantee that if you can safely survive the night, I will teach you the mighty abilities!”

“I would rather learn from Big Senior Sister instead. Stop right there! I’ll let you know what a trial from a mortal is like!”

“You are being disrespectful to an immortal!” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy took to her heels, resolved not to let Lu Yang catch up with her.

In reality, the various experts placed Lu Yang in high regard, the prodigy capable of challenging opponents beyond his level. One after another, they repeatedly crushed him.

Lu Yang tried his best to explain calmly, “Dear senior brothers and sisters, I think there may be some misunderstanding between us. Actually, there is another powerful soul residing within me. All the actions I took during my time as the acting sect leader were done by her while occupying my body.”

The senior disciples sneered, not believing Lu Yang’s nonsense. You’re pretending to have a split personality disorder now? Too late!

Although they were here for revenge, they didn’t swarm up to him all at once. That was what boorish people would do. As civilized folks, they should line up.

Below the stage, everyone tacitly formed a long queue.

“Those at the front, hurry up! There are so many people waiting behind!”

As the strongest sect among the Five Great Immortal Sects, the Dao-Seeking Sect’s strength was unquestionable. Every disciple they recruited was talented. When these disciples reached the Golden Core Stage and beyond, they would formulate their unique insights into their combat styles, methods of spirit energy circulation, and spell-casting sequences.

Fighting against these people would be beneficial for rapidly boosting one’s combat experience, allowing one to handle future battles with ease, no matter the combat style.

This was corroborated by the disciples of the Five-Elements Sect. Engaging in battle with the disciples of the Dao-Seeking had been a tremendous boon to them.

In the external world, countless people wished for a chance to exchange experiences with the disciples of the Dao-Seeking Sect and would envy Lu Yang for having the opportunity to do so.

On the other hand, Lu Yang expressed that he had no desire to become the target of envy.

The devastating battles prompted Meng Jingzhou to clap and cheer as he watched from the sidelines.

However, Lu Yang couldn’t help but acknowledge one thing—the battles with his senior brothers and sisters were immensely helpful for both his combat experience and cultivation realm.

After the senior disciples unleashed their unique arts to crush Lu Yang, they would pinch his mouth open and feed him precious pills like the Golden Vitality Stabilizing Pill and Spring Breeze Restoration Pill, as if they didn’t cost any money.

These pills aided him in a speedy recovery and solidified his foundation, allowing him to face the next battle in better shape.

Through this process of repeated battles and pill consumption, Lu Yang’s cultivation steadily rose, which was a cause for celebration. He felt that he was just a thought away from breaking through the Intermediate Foundation Establishment Stage.

Furthermore, during his duels with the senior disciples, he became more proficient in his abilities, such as the Three Flavored True Fire, Shrinking Earth, To Inches, and Tree-Planting Mantra, as he found their loopholes and figured out their corresponding solutions.

Perhaps this was what they meant by “great fortuitous opportunities lie between life and death.” Lu Yang’s potential was further squeezed out in a cruel manner.

For example, Lu Yang could now spit out the Three Flavored True Fire and only burn the opponent’s insides without harming them on the surface. He also gained enhanced control over his fire—he could freely adjust the spiciness level, including mild, medium, special, and explosive spiciness, and the saltiness, with options for light, normal, more salty, and extra salty. However, it was still far from the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s level of saltiness.

For example, during his battles, Lu Yang realized he could combine Shrinking Earth, To Inches, and the Tree-Planting Mantra. First, he would use Shrinking Earth, then To Inches, and finally the Tree-Planting Mantra. That way, the tree could grow three Lu Yangs instead.

However, as Lu Yang’s mental power was currently on the weaker side, he was unable to control three of himself simultaneously.

“Hmm, Ginseng Fruit?” Yi Jing was Lu Yang’s current opponent. She looked at the little bald Lu Yang swaying on the Bodhi tree in surprise and found him very adorable.

A male disciple exclaimed, “Could this be the origin of the legendary ginseng fruit?” Ginseng Fruits had only existed in the legends and were never seen.

Another male disciple found him too imaginative. “Junior Brother Lu is the only person in history to have learned spells like this. No matter how rare Ginseng Fruits are, they can’t be rarer than him.

One other male disciple chimed in, “I also think that Ginseng Fruits don’t appear in this way. I once read in a wild unofficial history book that described the origin of the Ginseng Fruit. In ancient times, ginseng was rare, so a fraudster claimed that he had ginseng. When people asked him where he found it, he said that it grew on trees. That’s how the name ‘Ginseng Fruit’ came about.”

“...This wild unofficial history is indeed very wild.”

“Did the book write who the fraudster was?”

“It was someone called the Heaven Mandate Immortal.”

Inside the mental space, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy had run so fast that she lapped Lu Yang by a full circle, and Lu Yang finally caught hold of her wrist.

“I’ve finally caught you!” Lu Yang smiled gently like a refined scoundrel.

In reality, Lu Yang had shouted, “Wait!” and stopped the Divine Transfiguration male disciple who was about to attack.

The Divine Transfiguration male disciple paused, curious to see what Lu Yang was up to.

This Divine Transfiguration male disciple, Senior Brother Wu, was one of the people the Everlasting Immortal Fairy had challenged, and he was here to take his revenge. After lining up for half a day, it was finally his turn.

Lu Yang heaved in a deep breath of air and said slowly, “Senior Brother Wu, I advise you not to go too far. If you go overboard and corner me, I’m capable of doing anything!”

Senior Brother Wu was not intimidated and laughed. “So what if I go too far? Don’t tell me you still have a fourth Sect Leader Experience voucher?” He didn’t think Lu Yang had any more. If he did, he would have used it long ago.

“I don’t have a Sect-Leader Experience voucher, but I have an ancient mighty ability capable of slaying all enemies. As we are fellow disciples of the Dao-Seeking Sect, I do not wish to unleash carnage within the sect!”

Senior Brother Wu didn’t buy it. Not wasting his breath further, he launched his attack.

When Lu Yang saw that his persuasion tactic had failed, he had no choice but to use the spell he just learned.

“Behold my ancient mighty ability—Scatter Dou-Beans For Soldiers!” [1]

Inside his mental space, Lu Yang forcefully handed over control of his body to Huang Doudou.

Scatter Dou-Beans For Soldiers means letting the Everlasting Immortal Fairy fight in my stead!

This is no small feat! Just imagine how invincible one can become with an immortal possessing their body. This move would have been mind-blowing in ancient times and even considered taboo!

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s heart was filled with despair as she watched Senior Brother Wu approaching. This is a Divine Transfiguration cultivator. How am I supposed to fight him?

“Lu Yang, you have no reverence for immortals!”

Lu Yang scoffed. Reverence? That’s something I’ll think about only after I survive the night!

1. This is based on a classical story where someone scattered beans which turned into soldiers. There is a wordplay on “bean” as the meaning of “dou” in Huang Doudou is bean. ☜

Chapter 180: Junior Brother Lu, Do You Have Any Other Unfulfilled Wishes?

To have survived the cruelty and savagery that was the ancient era and successfully ascended to one of the five immortals, her exceptional luck was not the only factor at play. Part of the credit was also the myriad hidden abilities she had hidden up her sleeve.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s eyes gleamed coldly. Her opponent’s cultivation was too high for ordinary methods to work. If that’s the case, don’t blame me for holding back.

She directly employed the forbidden temporal spell—Play-Dead Technique!

With a thud, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy collapsed to the ground, lying motionlessly and devoid of any vital signs.

Senior Brother Wu was startled. I haven’t even made a move yet, and he’s already dead?

Someone from the audience suggested, “Why don’t we bury him?”

“We should give him a proper burial,” Senior Brother Wu nodded. Everyone had borne witness to the contributions Lu Yang had made during his time as the sect leader.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was so appalled by their words and hurriedly got up. This caused Senior Brother Wu to be on edge, as if a formidable enemy stood before him. He whipped out a yellow talisman and pasted it on Lu Yang’s forehead.

“I didn’t expect Junior Brother Lu to turn into an animated corpse.[1] Does he have some unfulfilled wishes?” Senior Brother Wu softly recited a Rebirth Requiem, “Dust to dust, earth to earth, all has passed. Junior Brother Lu, speak your wish, and I will help you fulfill it.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy said in a faint voice, “My wish is to defeat Yun Zhi.”

Senior Brother Wu’s expression shifted slightly as he placed another yellow talisman over Lu Yang’s mouth. “Junior Brother Lu, do you have any other unfulfilled wishes?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy couldn’t utter a single word.

Senior Brother Wu heaved a sigh of relief. “Looks like there’s no more.”

Agonizing wails erupted from the crowd. They lifted Lu Yang’s still-warm body and buried him in the small grove on Heaven’s Gate Peak, leaving only his head exposed.

Afterward, they left for the Great Mission Hall, eager to complete missions, accumulate contribution points, and redeem the Sect Leader Experience voucher to also indulge in the thrill of being the acting sect leader.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy had three lively days as the acting sect leader, tempting people to also satisfy the gnawing feeling in their hearts.

“Being the sect leader seems like a lot of fun.”

“I have some ideas that can only be realized by becoming the sect leader.”

Everyone was so fired up in taking on missions at the Great Mission Hall that even Dai Bufan got a fright. He had never seen everyone so pumped up as if they were buying items on sale.

In the end, the mission wall was completely empty—all the missions were taken. Dai Bufan was left with his eyelids twitching non-stop.

After asking for the reason, he breathed a sigh of relief. Good to know that they’re not doing this in the heat of the moment.

Completing just one or two missions is not going to get them their Sect Leader Experience voucher.

That was unless someone slayed a Fusion diabolic cultivator like the Everlasting Immortal Fairy did.

“That's not a bad thing. There has been an increase in the number of missions the past few days, just right for satisfying their appetite,” he murmured to himself.

Since yesterday, they observed a rise in the number of mortals from the Great Xia Dynasty seeking help from the Dao-Seeking Sect. Upon further investigation, Dai Bufan realized that all these people originated from the same place. They had heard a wandering storyteller narrate Saga of the Dao-Seeking Sect and learned of the existence of a place that championed virtue and punished evil like the Dao-Seeking Sect.

Dai Bufan pondered for a bit and discovered the root cause. “Big Senior Sister asked the sect leader to travel around telling stories to promote the Dao-Seeking Sect, and it looks like it’s starting to show results.”

However, Dai Bufan also heard about some strange things. For example, some mortals that came to the Dao-Seeking Sect for help said that they wanted to meet the Taciturn Daoist Priest from the Saga of the Dao-Seeking Sect, the legend who went against the tide to save the Dao-Seeking Sect from decline and propelled the sect to its rank as the leader of the Five Great Immortal Sects.

Aside from them having the same name, Dai Bufan could find no other connections between this legendary Taciturn Daoist Priest and the sect leader.

It was hard to distinguish the Five Great Immortal Sects based on their power. After all, the sects could be harboring a few crazy old overlords, so comparing their combat strength on the surface was pointless.

The Dao-Seeking Sect did go through a period of decline, but that was something numerous generations ago. It had nothing to do with the current or previous generation. By the time the Taciturn Daoist Priest took over, the Dao-Seeking Sect had long emerged from its slump.

It was Yun Zhi’s appearance, however, that broke the stalemate among the Five Great Immortal Sects.

No sect’s crazy old overlords were as capable as Yun Zhi in combat. Even the Great Xia Dynasty’s ancestor hidden in the forbidden grounds of the imperial palace knew that he was not Yun Zhi’s match in a one-on-one fight, let alone those old colossi from the Five Great Immortal Sects.

These crazy old colossi were renowned experts in their active years, shaping the course of those eras and stirring up storms. Now, they were retired, and their reputations were no longer as resounding. It would be embarrassing if word got out that they couldn’t defeat a young girl, so they didn’t reveal the specifics of Yun Zhi’s true strength. They simply urged the current generation of leaders to be shrewd enough not to provoke Yun Zhi.

Although the current generation was not cognizant of Yun Zhi’s exact strength, they took the old colossi’s teachings to heart.

Among them, the Great Xia Dynasty had to take the crown for adhering to their admonition.

Dai Bufan was a bit distressed as he thought about another issue. “Junior Brother Lu tricked the higher-ups of the Everlasting Creed into coming in to capture them in one fell swoop. How many contribution points should I give him? Although Big Senior Sister played the most critical role, Lu Yang and the other two also contributed significantly.

“Forget it, I won’t think about it anymore. I’ll just let Big Senior Sister make the decision.” Dai Bufan decided to toss this matter to the back of his mind.

~~~

In the small grove of Heaven’s Gate Peak, Lu Yang’s head peaked out of the ground. Turning his head, Lu Yang regained control of his body.

“Shrinking Earth.” Lu Yang burrowed out of the soil with a whoosh.

The senior disciples had shown Lu Yang mercy, letting him off the hook because they knew he could use the Earth Escape Technique. Otherwise, a move like “Earth to Steel With a Finger” would have been enough to give him a potful of a nightmare.

“Congratulations, you have passed this immortal’s trial!” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy clapped her hands in applause.

She analyzed in a serious manner, “This has been a fruitful experience for you. Not only did you gain valuable combat experience, but you also witnessed visible improvement in your various spells and techniques, and even your cultivation is almost at the Advanced Foundation Establishment Stage. I dare guarantee that you’re the strongest among the peers of your age!”

Lu Yang remained silent, his eyes staring at her like a specter.

“Ahem, don’t look at me like that.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy coughed awkwardly. “I have said before that if you can pass this trial, I will pass down part of my legacy to you.

“I know you’re celebrating on the inside. In ancient times, how could anyone have learned my immortal techniques without becoming my disciple?”

Lu Yang eyed the Everlasting Immortal Fairy with suspicion. “You had disciples back then?”

“No.”

Lu Yang, “...”

Thankfully, you didn’t. Otherwise, just imagine how much you would have harmed them.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy didn’t know what Lu Yang was thinking and simply continued, “The spell I’m about to teach you has quite the origin. The Epoch Immortal was begging me to learn it. It involves time and the future. Although I am not as talented as the Epoch Immortal in temporal spells and only grasped the gist of it, it’s more than enough to teach you!”

“What spell is it?”

“Clairvoyance!”

Lu Yang inhaled a cold breath of air sharply. I never thought I’d have the chance to learn this famous spell. This can’t even be considered a spell anymore. Calling it an immortal technique is not an exaggeration.

Is the Immortal Fairy finally becoming my golden finger cheat?

This beating was not in vain.

Chapter 181: Only Family Share the Same Roof

The only thing Lu Yang knew about the Epoch Immortal was his honorific title, but he could still infer some information. Just like how “Everlasting” characterized the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, he could deduce that the Epoch Immortal was related to “epoch” or time itself.

Since this was a technique the Epoch Immortal taught to the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, now that she is passing it on to me, it is equivalent to receiving the blessings of two immortals. This goes to prove how powerful this spell is!

Besides, temporal spells are the rarest of all, even rarer than spatial and karmic spells.

“Why did the Epoch Immortal teach you this spell?” Lu Yang wondered, Immortal Fairy, did you poison the Epoch Immortal until he was in a stupor and finagle the spell out of him?

The more Lu Yang thought about it, the more plausible it seemed.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy feigned anger. “What are you talking about? With my charisma, isn’t it very normal for the Epoch Immortal to have begged me to learn his spells?!”

As I thought, you poisoned him silly.

“So what actually happened?”

“Once, I complained to the Epoch Immortal that I had worked hard in preparing so much nutritious food and invited them, yet none of them turned up, wasting all that food. I asked him whether he could teach me a spell that lets me predict whether they would be coming. That way, I could prepare the food portion accordingly.

“The Epoch Immortal appeared very reluctant. I could guess the reason easily. He must have thought that if I learned this spell, he would become unemployed. That I could understand. Seeing how troubled he was, I didn’t press him further.”

“What happened next?”

“You should know that I am a gentle, considerate, generous, and poised immortal fairy,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy listed a few adjectives that were completely unrelated to her.

“At that time, I was very considerate and told them that I could understand that they didn’t have time to come over to my place for a meal because of how busy they were managing so many stars.

“Since that was the case, I could reluctantly roll out a delivery service and bring the food straight to their tables. That way, not only would my food not go to waste, but they would also save time.

“The Epoch Immortal probably felt that my time was also precious and shouldn’t be spent on such trivial matters. He immediately offered to teach me ‘Clairvoyance,’ so that I could previse who would come.

“I expressed that the spell sounded quite difficult and I should just continue with the food delivery idea, but the Epoch Immortal very enthusiastically said that this was an extremely simple spell to master.

“Looking at how zealous he was, I decided to acquiesce.”

“Then did you master it?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy proudly nodded. “Who do you think I am? I’m the dignified Everlasting Immortal Fairy! How could there be anything I can’t master?! I can forecast things that will happen three days in advance without any errors!”

Lu Yang was immediately filled with reverence for her. She can even foretell events three days in advance. As expected of one of the five ancient immortals.

“I’ll give you a demonstration!” As the words left her mouth, so did her soul leave her body. A mysterious wind from somewhere blew at the hem of her light cyan dress, making her appeal like a maiden who had just stepped out of a painting.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy raised her hand, chanting an obscure ancient language. As she did so, countless golden runes appeared and scattered in all directions before fading into the void. When her recitation reached a climax, the golden runes returned and converged in her eyes.

Her eyes now glittered with a dazzlingly golden light.

“I saw...”

“What did you see, Immortal Fairy?”

“I saw that from tonight until tomorrow morning, moderate rain will transition into clear weather, with temperatures ranging from fifteen to nineteen degrees, accompanied by southeast winds...”

Question marks were popping out of Lu Yang’s head.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy continued, “I could even see that the day after tomorrow, the clear skies will turn cloudy, with temperatures ranging from seventeen to twenty-four degrees...”

Seeing how she was about to continue reporting the weather forecast, Lu Yang quickly interrupted her. “Wait, Immortal Fairy, this is the ‘Clairvoyance’ you learned?”

The Epoch Immortal dared to let you graduate with this level of skill? Is he not afraid of tarnishing his reputation?

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy advised Lu Yang sincerely, “You are too narrow-sighted. Did you think that only predictions about what you and I have done are considered clairvoyance?

“I used to have the same doubts as you. However, the Epoch Immortal patiently explained this to me. Isn’t the weather forecast also a part of clairvoyance? In fact, forecasting the weather is even harder than predicting other people’s actions.

“What does the weather represent? It represents the continuous changes of heaven and earth. The world is constructed by heaven, earth, and humans; heaven and earth come before humans. Predicting the changes in heaven and earth is far more difficult than predicting human behavior. It is precisely my ability to forecast the weather that attests to my major success with this spell! Ordinary people couldn’t achieve what I have even if they wanted to!” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy had repeated whatever the Epoch Immortal had relayed to her, feeling smug and elated.

Lecturing students, no, I mean, being a teacher feels amazing.

Lu Yang couldn’t help but suspect that the Everlasting Immortal Fairy had been duped by the Epoch Immortal. However, since he couldn’t beat the Epoch Immortal, he didn’t dare to question it.

“Can you predict anything else?”

“I can only predict the weather.”

Lu Yang was now convinced that the Everlasting Immortal Fairy had been duped by the Epoch Immortal. However, he couldn’t beat the Epoch Immortal.

The ancient era is so cruel. Immortals lack basic decency, deceiving even fools. How incorrigible!

“Is your weather forecast reliable? It is spring in the Dao-Seeking Sect all year round. Rarely do we have rain.” Lu Yang eyed the Everlasting Immortal Fairy suspiciously, skeptical of her accuracy.

“My weather forecasts have never been wrong!”

“So you were planning to teach me weather forecasting?” Lu Yang’s eyes twitched as he retracted his initial hopes.

This golden finger is truly not useful at all.

“What I learned was the highest realm of ‘Clairvoyance,’ which is weather forecasting. Although your talent in spells is sublime, it is still beneath mine. Besides, you’re only at the Foundation Establishment Stage. How could you possibly emulate me?”

Lu Yang didn’t really understand where the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s hubris stemmed from.

“So what you’re actually teaching me is the normal ‘Clairvoyance,’ just that it became weather forecasting when you learned it?”

“That’s right.”

Lu Yang felt that this was probably what they meant by “only family share the same roof.” Birds of a feather truly flock together.

Since the Everlasting Immortal Fairy is my nascent soul, it’s not unusual for her to share some similarities with me.

“Are you learning it or not?”

“Yes, I am!”

“If you want to learn it, we have to start with the most basic ancient language. The ancient language is vastly different from our modern language, so you will take some time to learn it. To witness results in the short term, you can just focus on chanting the phrases used in casting ‘Clairvoyance.’”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy paused before repeating the ancient phrase.

“What does it mean?” Lu Yang was curious.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy translated, “What I just said was ‘Heavenly spirits, earthly spirits,[1] Epoch Immortal, you grandson of a turtle, show yourself!”

Lu Yang instinctively took two steps back, afraid that the Epoch Immortal would descend and crush him with a finger. He felt that learning spells from the Everlasting Immortal Fairy did not offer even the most fundamental semblance of safety.

Big Senior Sister is still the most reliable.

“Repeat after me.

“Mmm, but just in case, let me ask first. Must I recite ‘you grandson of a turtle?’”

“That’s up to you. It’s just a modal particle to infuse your emotions.”

1. Up until here, it still sounds like a typical spell. ☜

Chapter 182: Clairvoyance

Lu Yang felt that a major reason for the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s inability to master Clairvoyance was the Epoch Immortal’s lack of seriousness in teaching her.

Under the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s guidance, Lu Yang learned the ancient language, terms foreign to his tongue jumbling out of his mouth. After repeating it a few times, however, he could recite the sentence fluently.

Suddenly, Lu Yang recalled that he had used modern language to revive the Everlasting Immortal Fairy. “By the way, to resurrect you, it doesn’t matter whether your name is called out in the ancient or modern language, right?”

“Hehe, I’ve already told you that my Dao Fruit is ‘Everlasting.’ What it means is that it is imperishable and lasts for an eternity. How could it be restricted by mere language? But, of course, the Heaven Mandate Immortal and the others didn’t know about this.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy grinned slyly, willing to share this little secret with Lu Yang.

She warned, “You mustn’t tell anyone about this! I’m only telling you because you resurrected me and let me reside in your body for such a long time!”

“Of course!” Lu Yang promised as he patted his chest.

He began industriously learning the art of clairvoyance. Sitting cross-legged, he carefully comprehended this mighty ability whose reputation resounded through the ages.

Lu Yang rarely asked the Everlasting Immortal Fairy for pointers, afraid that she might lead him astray. However, when he encountered something he truly couldn’t figure out, he could only turn to her for help.

At the side, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy watched as Lu Yang gradually grasped the quintessence of Clairvoyance and was secretly alarmed. This means that Lu Yang is not far away from mastering it.

Although she often claimed that Lu Yang’s talent in spells was inferior to hers, it was only because she was embarrassed to admit that the truth was the opposite. She couldn’t learn any temporal spells when she was at the Foundation Establishment Stage.

Despite being at the Intermediate Foundation Establishment Stage, Lu Yang has already mastered a complex spatial spell like Close Horizon From Cliff and now a temporal spell. Calling him an abomination wouldn’t be an exaggeration.

She soon cast this matter aside. After all, my forte isn’t in spells, so why should I compare my weakness with Lu Yang’s strength?

As Lu Yang recited the ancient phrase solemnly, he pressed his middle and index fingers together, then yelled, “Clairvoyance!”

“Did it work?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was astonished. That was so quick!

Golden runes appeared around Lu Yang and dissipated into the void. About three minutes later, the golden runes broke free from the void and returned to Lu Yang. His eyes shone brightly like gold.

He had successfully seen the future!

“I saw...myself from two minutes ago?!”

Lu Yang stared at himself from two minutes ago who had his arms raised, waiting for the golden runes to respond in a daze. He looked somewhat silly.

The corner of his eye twitched. Theoretically, he had mastered Clairvoyance and should have predicted events a minute into the future. But in practice, it took him three minutes to receive the results.

“How is this useful at all?!” Lu Yang grumbled. He reckoned that it was probably because he hadn’t fully grasped the spell.

“Let me practice a bit more.”

He reflected on his previous attempt, tried to identify the possible mistakes, rectify them, and cast the spell again.

This time, he waited for three minutes again, and he foresaw events one and a half minutes after him casting the spell.

“...I guess that’s an improvement,” Lu Yang consoled himself and kept himself motivated.

“Jiayou, you can do it!” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy cheered him on from the side.

“Again!”

After the Five-Elements Sect left, the senior disciples had taken turns fighting with Lu Yang until dawn before burying him in the small grove on Heaven’s Gate Peak. Having passed the test of an immortal, Lu Yang had started cultivating since dawn.

As time passed, dawn turned to evening, and the sun gave way to the moon, which light sprinkled over the Dao-Seeking Sect like water, cloaking it in a veil of mystery.

Heaven never let down those who persevere. Through persistent practice and determining, analyzing, and solving problems, he could see into the future for a longer duration, edging closer and closer to the three-minute mark.

Suddenly, Lu Yang felt a thunderous boom inside his head, as if something had been broken through. He immediately surmounted the three-minute obstacle and wielded clairvoyance.

His eyes shone brilliantly like two lanterns in the night.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy asked excitedly, “What did you see?”

Lu Yang’s expression was odd. “I saw this snippet: Big Senior Sister left Incarceration Peak, and I ran up to her, saying, ‘I must learn from Shifu and become as indolent as him, spending all day eating and playing, neither cultivating nor doing proper work.’ Then, Big Senior Sister revealed a faint smile as she hugged me and patted my back, telling me that she’d take care of me from now on.”

“For real?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was shocked. What kind of weird future is that?

“It feels real!” Lu Yang also couldn’t make sense of it.

“Why do I feel like something is not quite right?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s eyes twinkled as she prodded. “The Epoch Immortal said that the future cannot be changed. Since you saw it, it must be something that will happen.

“The only way to verify its veracity is to test it out!”

Lu Yang agreed with the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s reasoning, so he hurried to Incarceration Peak.

~~~

Yun Zhi had just emerged from Incarceration Peak, her fists stained with blood. Although her face remained impassive, those familiar with her could discern that she was in a good mood.

She had successfully obtained an enormous amount of information from the two vice creed leaders, including the location of the Everlasting Creed’s headquarters.

When she saw Lu Yang rushing toward her in high spirits, she asked, “Junior Brother, what’s the matter?”

Lu Yang flashed a scintillating smile. “I must learn from Shifu and become as indolent as him, spending all day eating and playing, neither cultivating nor doing proper work.”

Boom—crack—

The sky that was clear just a moment ago suddenly darkened as ominous clouds gathered. Lightning flashed and thunder roared as rain began to pelt down.

“Huh, it’s raining? I told you that there’d be moderate rain tonight!” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was pleased with herself, smug that her weather forecast was accurate.

Lu Yang noticed that after he uttered those words, Yun Zhi’s deadpan expression slowly shifted into a faint smile. Although she wore a smile, its combination with the lightning and thunder in the backdrop weighed down on Lu Yang suffocatingly.

It’s a life-and-death crisis!

Lu Yang swallowed his saliva, his consciousness rapidly returning to his mental space as he secretly asked, “Immortal Fairy, when one’s cultivation reaches a certain realm, will changes in their mood affect the weather?”

“Yes.”

Lu Yang finally understood why it had rained today despite the Dao-Seeking Sect not raining all year round.

It’s because I angered Big Senior Sister!

“Immortal Fairy, your weather forecast is truly accurate!” Lu Yang said through gritted teeth.

In reality, Yun Zhi gently patted Lu Yang on the shoulder and crooned, “Little Junior Brother, have you been too nervous from overworking yourself in your cultivation that you began speaking nonsense?”

Lu Yang shuddered and instinctively shook his head. Immediately, he realized that he had given the wrong response, and he hastily nodded like a chick pecking at grains, unable to mouth a single word.

He finally knew what spell he had actually learned.

Clairvoyance—predicting what would never come to pass.

Chapter 183: Strongest Tiger-Henchman Ghosts

Lu Yang candidly recounted everything that had transpired and even got the Everlasting Immortal Fairy to testify. Only then was Yun Zhi finally convinced that Lu Yang was just conducting an experiment.

The sound of thunder faded, the moderate rain abruptly ceased, and moonlight pierced through the dark clouds. The Dao-Seeking Sect regained its clear skies.

The disciples of the Dao-Seeking Sect were baffled to see the rain stop right after it had just started.

Whenever it rained in the Dao-Seeking Sect, it was usually because an elder was casting spells. They would infuse the spirit energy in the rain such that when it poured, the concentration of spirit qi in the sect would increase.

“What did I say? Cloudy skies turning clear from tonight until tomorrow morning. Look how accurate I was,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy bragged about her weather forecast ability.

“...” Lu Yang was in no mood to talk.

Just then, he noticed a few familiar figures trailing behind Yun Zhi—the seven higher-ups from the Everlasting Creed. The seven of them looked like they had lost their souls, their eyes tinged with fear as they gazed at Yun Zhi.

“Eh, they are all in a soul state.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was surprised.

“Big Senior Sister, you are planning to...” Lu Yang was very puzzled.

Yun Zhi explained insipidly, “I saw that they are quite the masters at barbecuing and are popular among the junior brothers and sisters. Rather than keeping them locked up at Incarceration Peak, it would be better to have them return to the barbeque shop and put their talents to use.

“So I refined the seven of them into tiger-henchman ghosts.”

Naturally, the seven of them would not get to pocket a single coin they had earned; everything had to be handed over to Yun Zhi.

As Incarceration Peak housed a number of ancient Fusion souls, there was no shortage of materials for crafting magical treasures for the time being.

Lu Yang’s eyes widened, his mouth agape. Why does this tactic seem so familiar? Besides, Fusion tiger-henchman ghosts? That has to be the pinnacle of tiger-henchman ghosts, right?

Refining the seven of them into tiger-henchman ghosts could reduce the risk of them rebelling and causing trouble in the sect. If they harbored malicious intentions, they would die on the spot.

Yun Zhi took the Everlasting Creed crew to One More Time Barbeque Shop, instructing them to run the place peacefully.

Vice Creed Leader Liu and the rest immediately nodded, promising to promote the spirit of barbeque. They would not cut corners and overcharge customers, guaranteeing that they would serve every customer with the highest level of professionalism and attentiveness.

Only then was Yun Zhi satisfied. Before leaving, she told Lu Yang to follow her back to Heaven’s Gate Peak.

And thus, One More Time Barbeque Shop opened successfully, and many merchants came forward to congratulate them on the inauguration of their new business.

At the start, the Everlasting Creed crew was full of contempt. Although they had become tiger-henchman ghosts, they were still Fusion experts, big shots who could easily command the clouds in the outside world. They were unwilling to converse with the merchants, whom they felt were beneath them.

However, they soon discarded that notion. A casual scan with their spiritual consciousness left them drenched in cold sweat. Just a cursory sweep was already enough to reveal several cultivators whose cultivation they couldn’t determine.

The beautiful owner of Hundred Fragrance Restaurant was one, and the teahouse proprietor was another. They concluded that these people were also at the Fusion Stage!

It’s one thing for cultivation experts to hide among the common folk, but for the Dao-Seeking Sect to do something like this?

Vice Creed Leader Liu also noticed several Void Refinement cultivators who exhibited erratic fluctuations in their cultivation. At their peak, they could even unleash the combat strength of a Fusion cultivator. Unless they made a move, no one could ascertain their true combat prowess at that particular point in time, instilling fear in others.

“Scary, the water really runs deep in the Dao-Seeking Sect...” they communicated secretly.

If that’s how the calculations work, just imagine how many Fusion cultivators there are in the Dao-Seeking Sect?

“It’s not just the Dao-Seeking Sect. The Five Great Immortal Sects are neck and neck, and I’m afraid the other four immortal sects may even be stronger than the Dao-Seeking Sect.” Even though they were using their spiritual consciousness for communication, Vice Creed Leader Gao still lowered his voice, as if he was afraid of being discovered by someone.

“This is only the tip of the iceberg in the Dao-Seeking Sect.”

That was when it dawned upon them just how humongous the chasm between the Four Great Diabolic Sects and the Five Great Immortal Sects was. The Five Great Immortal Sects stood in a league of their own. It was no surprise that they would always choose to hide or flee whenever they met someone from the Five Great Immortal Sects.

If they failed to hide or escape, they would end up as either tiger-henchman ghosts or materials for refining magical treasures.

Vice Creed Leader Liu couldn’t help but feel an odd sense of familiarity.

“Why does this tactic seem so uncannily similar to ours?”

~~~

Back at Heaven’s Gate Peak, Yun Zhi’s physical body remained in the cave abode while her soul left her body.

“Big Senior Sister, you...” Before Lu Yang could finish, he saw Yun Zhi’s soul entering his mental space, giving both him and the Everlasting Immortal Fairy a fright.

“You...you...you scared me to death!” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy had been lounging lazily on a soft couch with her feet crossed when she was jolted out of her reverie. Yun Zhi’s sudden appearance sent her springing up from her seat right away.

Yun Zhi paid no heed to the Everlasting Immortal Fairy and turned to Lu Yang. “I’ve already obtained the location of the Everlasting Creed’s headquarters, but if I go there just like this, I might alarm them again like the last time, leaving us empty-handed.

“The plan is for me to hide in your mental space first. By following my instructions, you’ll be able to enter their headquarters. This will ensure that we can capture them in one fell swoop without any fish escaping the net.”

Lu Yang felt that his mental space had the potential to become a ground for playing cards.

Nonetheless, he could understand Yun Zhi’s concerns. This is indeed a good idea.

“What should I do?”

“First, go find Meng Jingzhou and Man Gu.”

~~~

Inside the creed leader’s secret chamber in the Everlasting Creed Headquarters, two rows of bookshelves lined both sides, laden with precious pills, secret spells, and cultivation techniques. Most of the pill bottles lay empty, their contents long consumed by the creed leader to heal his wounds. At the end of the shelves stood a life-sized statue of an androgynous Everlasting Immortal.

In the darkness, the creed leader of the Everlasting Creed slowly opened his eyes, emerging from his seclusion. Stretching his limbs, he sensed the still-sluggish spirit energy within him and couldn’t help but force a bitter laughter.

During the creed’s entrance trials, Yun Zhi had appeared from nowhere, and he still hadn’t fully recovered from the blow she delivered. He was slightly worried about the future. “At this rate, will I really need a century of secluded cultivation?”

If I can only regain my strength in a hundred years, who would lead the Everlasting Creed during this period of time? The three vice creed leaders, including Vice Creed Leaders Liu and Gao, coveted his position with the eyes of a tiger, while only the examiner of the entrance trials, Vice Creed Leader Jin, showed no ambition toward his position for now.

The creed leader shifted his gaze to the Everlasting Immortal statue, a look of yearning swirling in his eyes. He vaguely sensed that the Everlasting Immortal was awakening. Lighting three incense sticks for offerings, he inserted them into the incense burner. Then, he knelt and pressed his palms together, bowing to the statue three times.

“Great Everlasting Immortal Brazen-Faced Bu Yaolian[1], please save your devoted follower and this world!”

“Who calls upon this immortal?” A benevolent and aged voice reverberated throughout the secret chamber.

The creed leader looked up, his eyes tinged with fervor and joy, his whole body shaking uncontrollably.

The statue’s eyes emitted an eerie red light. The wisps of incense smoke shrouded the statue, forming a veil of mist.

The mist gradually morphed into a benign-looking elderly man.

1. The name here is a homophone for being thick-skinned and having no sense of shame. If you translate the name literally, it’s “cloth wants face.” ☜

Chapter 184: Everlasting Immortal

The creed leader was not counting on the Everlasting Immortal to really appear. Although he had indeed sensed the Everlasting Immortal awakening, he had not expected it to be so quick. It was a pleasant surprise for him.

Excitement pumped through the creed leader as he introduced himself, “Venerable Immortal, congratulations on awakening from the river of history. I am Xie Bingzhi, the creed leader of the Everlasting Creed. It has been three hundred thousand years since your era. Oh, you may not know about the Everlasting Creed. We are one of the Four Great Diabolic Creeds, and our mission is to awaken you from your slumber...”

The Everlasting Immortal listened quietly to the creed leader’s voluble introduction. Finally, when the creed leader ended his speech, he chuckled and said in a measured tone, “Child, stay calm. One is already aware of all that you have just spoken.”

The creed leader regained his composure, realizing that he had overstepped his boundaries and probably made a spectacle of himself. “You are omniscient, Immortal.”

The Everlasting Immortal shook his head. “Not quite. Who would dare claim to be omniscient? Even the other immortals including Heaven Mandate and Qilin couldn’t be considered all-knowing, much less this immortal. After all, I have been detached from the world for three hundred thousand years. Seas may now be fields, and stars may have shifted from their positions; the world has metamorphosed drastically. Who could have foreseen today’s events back then?”

A golden droplet appeared out of nowhere in his hand. With a casual flick, the Everlasting Immortal shot it into the creed leader’s hand.

The creed leader could feel the terrifying vital energy it encompassed.

“You have been gravely injured by a formidable opponent, and you will need at least a century’s worth of time to fully recover. This drop of Everlasting Liquid can help to accelerate your healing process.”

“This...is this the legendary ‘Everlasting’ Dao Fruit?” The creed leader’s hands were quivering. It was his first time experiencing the grand power of an immortal.

The Everlasting Immortal smiled benevolently, “The Immortal Dao Fruit must not be revealed easily. This is just a dewdrop from the Everlasting Dao Fruit.”

The creed leader immediately consumed it. As soon as the golden liquid entered his mouth, it transformed into a strange energy that flooded his limbs, bones, and every fiber of his being. He could distinctly feel his injuries healing much more rapidly.

From what he had heard, the Dao Fruit of an immortal was their foundation and would never be lightly shown to others. The Everlasting Immortal truly lives up to his reputation as the messiah of humans. He is generous and selfless, even bestowing me the opportunity to have a glimpse of the Dao Fruit’s might.

The Everlasting Immortal had both his hands behind his back. “I know why you have awakened me. Since time immemorial, the struggles between prodigies and ascending to an immortal have been unchanging topics...” His clouded eyes were slightly closed, as if he was reminiscing about the ancient era. Eventually, it all culminated in a deep sigh. He shook his head, not making further comments about the past.

He muttered, “Does the human race need my salvation again?”

The creed leader hurriedly replied, “Immortal, the reemergence of the Ancient Great Era is imminent, and there are cultivators reviving everywhere. When war breaks out, only you can save humanity!”

“Never mind, perhaps saving the human race is my calling. What harm is there in saving them once again?”

The creed leader was about to say something when the Everlasting Immortal raised his hand to stop him. “However, all that remains of me is my soul. As my Dao Fruit is incomplete, I am confined to this statue temporarily, so I am unable to protect you as I did toward the end of the ancient era. To return to my peak, I still need a body to inhabit.”

“Can I offer mine?” the creed leader volunteered eagerly.

The Everlasting Immortal shook his head. “Your body is already set in stone, and you have strayed many times in your cultivation journey. The chances of condensing a Dao Fruit are slim.

“I heard that Yun Zhi from the Dao-Seeking Sect is known as the strongest among the Five Great Immortal Sects. Would her body be suitable?” the creed leader suggested.

The Everlasting Immortal shook his head again. “Hmph, the strongest among the Five Great Immortal Sects? From what I know, the Five Great Immortal Sects are just five sects with some resources and remnants of heritage. Even if we put aside the four regions in the north, south, east, and west, the collective strength of the Five Great Immortal Sects may not even match up to the Great Xia Dynasty which currently governs the Central Continent.

“Given these circumstances, how powerful can their strongest member really be? Are you sure they can let me become an immortal once more?”

The creed leader lowered his head and apologized for his mistake.

The Everlasting Immortal continued, “There is still some time until the Battle of the Great Era erupts, but that is enough for me to cultivate back to my peak. I just need someone who has started cultivating to take over their body so that I can return to the realm of immortals. If I am lucky, I may even surpass the Heaven Mandate Immortal and Qilin Immortal as the leader of the five ancient immortals. At that time, even if I protect the human race, the risk of me perishing will be reduced significantly.”

“You are wise, Immortal.”

“Go summon all the followers at the Foundation Establishment and Qi Training stages. I shall personally select who is worthy to serve as my vessel.”

“Understood. Immortal, I have a question.”

“Ask, child.”

“Who exactly refined the countless stars into a continent back then?”

In the legends, the Everlasting Immortal had personally witnessed this major event that marked the end of the ancient era.

The Everlasting Immortal shut his eyes and shook his head. “Your cultivation is too low. This is not something you should know.”

The creed leader was slightly dejected, but he also acknowledged that a huge gulf lay between them. Before leaving, he hesitantly asked, “Your name...doesn’t seem to be ordinary?”

What he really wanted to say was that he had randomly made up the name “Brazen-Faced Bu Yaolian” simply because he had run out of ideas. Why would the Immortal come up with such a strange name?

A dark face from the Everlasting Immortal said it all.

The creed leader realized that he had misspoken and quickly excused himself.

~~~

After leaving the secret chamber, the creed leader hurriedly summoned the vice creed leaders and elders. However, only Vice Creed Leader Jin turned up. Upon further inquiry, he learned that the two other vice creed leaders and the elders had headed to the Dao-Seeking Sect with the immortal treasure on a suicide mission.

“They’re so obsessed with power that they don’t even want their lives anymore?!” The creed leader gritted his teeth. I can guess what those two fools were thinking. They simply want to make a name for themselves at the Dao-Seeking Sect to have a better shot at fighting for the position of creed leader.

But why did you have to choose the Dao-Seeking Sect of all places?!

You may make it in alive, but can you make it out alive?

“How long has it been since the end of the Five-Elements Sect’s visit to the Dao-Seeking Sect?”

“Just half a day. There has been no word yet.”

The creed leader inhaled a deep breath of air. “No need to wait for news. They must have been captured. The Dao-Seeking Sect might have even learned of our headquarters’ location!

“There’s only one option left.”

“Surrender?”

The creed leader flew into a rage. “Surrender my ass! Have you ever seen diabolic creeds surrendering to the righteous path?”

“Then does this count as us making history?”

The creed leader suppressed the urge to strangle him. “Move our base right now to our fifth backup site!”

“Oh.”

To prevent the higher-ups from revealing the locations of the Everlasting Creed’s headquarters and backup bases, the creed leader only allowed every vice creed leader to know of one backup site’s location. For instance, Vice Creed Leader Liu only knew about the third backup base, while Vice Creed Leader Gao only knew of the fourth.

In just two months, they already had to relocate from the second base to the third base—all because of the Dao-Seeking Sect.

The Everlasting Creed acted swiftly as they packed up, ready to head to their fifth backup base.

The creed leader peeked into the secret chamber. “Immortal, shall I carry you, or will you leave by yourself?”

The Everlasting Immortal, “...”

Why does it feel like I could lose my life at any moment?

Chapter 185: Big Senior Sister’s Plan

“Big Senior Sister, this is your plan?”

“Of course.

“Vice Creed Leaders Liu and Gao only know about the third and fourth backup bases, so the Everlasting Creed will definitely move to the fifth backup site, but its location is still unknown to us. This is why I need the three of you to use the reason I have provided you to gain Tang Yunsheng’s trust and get him to take you to the original base. The Everlasting Creed would have evacuated in a hurry, so there’d definitely be many spies staying behind in the vicinity to inform the others how to head to the new backup base.

“When the three of you and Tang Yunsheng show up nearby, it will attract the attention of the Everlasting Creed’s followers. From the creed’s perspective, it is likely that the three of you have been captured by the Dao-Seeking Sect and converted into double agents, so you mustn’t be trusted.

“But Tang Yunsheng is different. The Everlasting Creed is aware that he has been lurking outside the Dao-Seeking Sect, so he wouldn’t have been captured. He is someone they can trust. Only with him guiding you to the original base will the Everlasting Creed accept you and tell you the real location of the base.

“The ultimate objective of this plan is for you to earn the Everlasting Creed’s trust.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy repeatedly nodded at the side, finding it a terrific idea.

~~~

Tang Yunsheng had been hiding around the meeting spot near the Dao-Seeking Sect, waiting anxiously for updates from the vice creed leaders. He had watched the Dao-Seeking Sect seeing the Five-Elements Sect off, but there was still no sign of the vice creed leaders and the other higher-ups.

A sense of foreboding grew in his heart. It’s over! They must have been captured by that damn Dao-Seeking Sect!

After waiting the whole day, Tang Yunsheng finally noticed Lu Yang and the other two scampering toward him in a sorry plight.

“Why are there only the three of you? Where are the rest?!” Tang Yunsheng shook Lu Yang by the shoulders.

Upon hearing Tang Yunsheng questioning him, Lu Yang’s vacant eyes welled with tears, and his lips quivered, finally bursting into sobs.

“Vice Creed Leader Liu...all of them...they failed! When Vice Creed Leader Liu took out the immortal treasure to unleash his divine abilities, an expert hiding in the Dao-Seeking Sect suddenly resisted the power of the immortal treasure and engaged in an all-out battle with the whole group!”

Meng Jingzhou also began wailing as the tragic scenes played out in his mind. “Vice Creed Leader Liu and the others refused to surrender, and that damn Dao-Seeking Sect beat them to death!”

Man Gu only wept, not uttering a single word—he had forgotten his lines.

The trio cried their hearts out, their heartfelt grief evident.

“What?!” Tang Yunsheng was in disbelief as his knees buckled under him. Two vice creed leaders and five higher-ups have all fallen into the hands of the Dao-Seeking Sect? How will I explain this when I go back?!

“Wait a minute, why are the three of you fine?” Tang Yunsheng suddenly thought of a problem. The vice creed leaders and the higher-ups only managed to enter the Dao-Seeking Sect through their barbeque shop, so the Dao-Seeking Sect would definitely suspect these three.

Lu Yang calmed himself. “Vice Creed Leader Liu left a sigil in our minds to disguise us as puppets controlled by his formidable mental power. That’s why the Dao-Seeking Sect let us go.”

“Then you three should have continued staying undercover in the Dao-Seeking Sect.”

The three of them are spies that are hard to come by.

Lu Yang shook his head. “Even if it wasn’t our fault, no one else would tolerate us after something like that happened. Our business is ruined, and people will be pointing fingers behind our backs. There’s no longer a place for us in the Dao-Seeking Sect.”

Tang Yunsheng patted Lu Yang on the shoulder. “It has been tough on you guys.”

Lu Yang’s eyes gleamed with visceral hatred as he declared, “Sacrificing ourselves for the Everlasting Creed is nothing at all. But I will never let the traitor get away!”

“Traitor?”

Meng Jingzhou nodded vigorously, his eyes also smoldering with resentment and malice. “Vice Creed Leader Liu and the others had such an impeccable plan, and they even had our support from the inside. If there hadn’t been a traitor, how could they have failed?

“Before Vice Creed Leader Liu passed away, he secretly transmitted an auditory message to us and revealed the traitor’s identity. He told us to return to the Everlasting Creed in one piece and expose the traitor!”

Tang Yunsheng’s expression turned grim. “Who is the traitor?”

This is no small matter. The raid on the Dao-Seeking Sect was a secret operation only known to a few people within the creed, and all of them are high-ranking and influential members. Suspecting anyone could lead to huge complications!

Lu Yang stated the identity of the traitor, “It’s the third vice creed leader, Vice Creed Leader Jin!”

“It’s him?!” Tang Yunsheng’s voice rose in pitch. As the idea sank in, he felt that it did make sense. There are altogether three vice creed leaders. With two vice creed leaders dying, the position of creed leader will eventually fall upon the person who remains standing.

Everything adds up now.

“Let’s go! We must quickly report this to the creed leader!” Tang Yunsheng realized the gravity of the situation, and they set off posthaste.

Now, the trio were no longer spies but witnesses.

Tang Yunsheng took the trio to head south on a flying vessel. When they arrived at a large city, they alighted and traveled another three hundred li into the mountains and wilderness.

“Inspecting Officer Tang, is the headquarters here?” Lu Yang looked around for traces of an ancient cave ruin.

Tang Yunsheng’s face twisted into a cruel smile. “You three reckless fools still want to go to the headquarters? We might not even make it there before getting slaughtered by assassins sent by Vice Creed Leader Jin!

“Besides, who can guarantee that the creed leader isn’t involved? It’s also possible that the creed leader has accepted Vice Creed Leader Jin’s plan for the stability of the Everlasting Creed and decided to get rid of us.
