“If we go to the headquarters, it’s no different from walking straight into a trap! Whoever gets embroiled in this kind of power struggle between the higher-ups will only die. I’m not interested in being a part of it.

“The safest option right now is to kill you three little brats and escape to a place with no one else!”

Tang Yunsheng was very rational. Ferreting out the traitor? What does that have to do with me? As a diabolic cultivator, survival is the top priority!

I’ll just find a random place in the wilderness and kill these three until nothing but ash remains of them. The Everlasting Creed will be none of my concern then!

With my Nascent Soul cultivation, killing these three Foundation Establishment brats will be as effortless as flipping my palm!

Lu Yang, “...”

Meng Jingzhou, “...”

Man Gu, “...”

This was quite a deviation from Yun Zhi’s plan. Things had already gone wrong at the second step. They had indeed obtained Tang Yunsheng’s trust, but that didn’t mean that he was willing to take them to the Everlasting Creed.

Lu Yang asked Yun Zhi in his mental space, “Big Senior Sister, what do we do?” What other brilliant tricks do you have up your sleeve?

Yun Zhi was as indifferent as ever, but when faced with Lu Yang’s question, her gaze suddenly faltered for a moment before she stared at Lu Yang and said in an unruffled manner, “No need to worry, everything is going according to plan.”

The change in Yun Zhi’s gaze was very subtle, but it didn’t go unnoticed by Lu Yang, who had spent a long time with her.

She’s clearly feeling guilty.

Lu Yang suddenly recalled some past events, such as when Yun Zhi had prepared him a boiling water bath to temper his body and how she had misinterpreted the Moon Laurel Celestial Palace’s request as a marriage proposal.

Big Senior Sister is unfamiliar with the ways of the world.

She may seem calm and perfect in whatever she does, as if she has everything under control, but in reality, it’s because her expression never changes that gives people this false impression.

Chapter 186: Everything Is According to Plan

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was fuming with rage. Tang Yunsheng doesn’t have the basic loyalty a follower of mine should have!

Back in ancient times, I was a hegemon reigning over a planet where everyone was honored to be a pious devotee of mine and treated my words as precepts.

Lu Yang commented to himself, Yeah, right, keep telling that to yourself. This was only because they conceived of their immortal as a perfect being. If the Everlasting Creed learns what the true Everlasting Immortal Fairy was like, forget loyalty, I can even believe they’ll be disbanding the next day.

At least, I wish I could resign from being the creed founder every day.

If the creed founder already held such opinions, one shouldn’t hope for more from the ordinary followers.

Hold on, why don’t I flip the script and have the Everlasting Immortal Fairy resign instead? The whole Everlasting Creed can change their faith!

The more Lu Yang thought about it, the more convinced he was about his idea. He was not at all flustered as he let his thoughts run wild. With Yun Zhi around, he was confident that they wouldn’t get hurt.

The problem now was how to deal with Tang Yunsheng. If we kill him, it’ll complicate our follow-up plans, but if we don’t kill him, the three of us are doomed. This is really a dilemma.

Meng Jingzhou and Man Gu were also not afraid. Before coming, Lu Yang had already assured them that everything was part of Yun Zhi’s plan and that nothing would go wrong.

There was nothing more reassuring than the words “Big Senior Sister.”

Tang Yunsheng raised his hand and drew out a blood-red wide saber wrapped with malevolent ghosts and grievous souls. When he saw that the trio hadn’t moved at all, he thought they had lost the will to resist.

That makes sense. This is a normal response in the face of an absolute gulf in cultivation stage.

Tang Yunsheng had witnessed numerous cultivators who resigned to their fate like Lu Yang.

Die!

A bone-chilling aura emanated from Tang Yunsheng, speaking of the countless lives he had taken. He flashed a sinister smile as he leaped high into the air with ceaseless murderous intent, ready to slash the three to death in a single strike and leave not even their bones behind.

Suddenly, the space beside a boulder distorted. The creed leader of the Everlasting Creed stretched lazily and stepped out from the fifth backup base. He had instructed the others to tidy up the place first while he would come out for a break.

Then, he saw Tang Yunsheng with his bloody blade raised, preparing to slice the trio who stood rooted to the ground as if they were petrified with fear.

The creed leader, “...”

Tang Yunsheng, “...”

Question marks were surfacing from the creed leader’s head. What on earth is going on?

“Tang Yunsheng, what are you doing?!” The creed leader realized that it was not the time for sitting around with question marks. He roared and grabbed Tang Yunsheng, his bones cracking under the grip.

“Wait! Creed Leader, I can explain...” Tang Yunsheng panicked. Can someone tell me what’s going on? I had randomly picked an isolated place in the wilderness, and now, the creed leader has appeared out of nowhere?

The creed leader didn’t bother listening to Tang Yunsheng’s nonsense. Without caring about the consequences, he used his spiritual consciousness to scan Tang Yunsheng’s mental space, destroying his mental capacity while uncovering his memories. He naturally was no saint to have become the creed leader of a diabolic creed. Killing people to plunder from them and scanning others’ mental spaces brutally were common things for him.

The creed leader finally learned the full picture: Lu Yang’s group had successfully infiltrated the Dao-Seeking Sect with much effort, but it was all because of the two vice creed leaders that their plan had failed. That was not all. After Liu and Gao failed, they revealed that Vice Creed Leader Jin was a traitor. Being the staunch followers they were, Lu Yang’s group was determined to inform the headquarters of the news, but Tang Yunsheng wanted to silence them out of his selfish motives.

“Bastard!” The creed leader crushed Tang Yunsheng to death. If it weren’t for me appearing here by chance, this faithful trio of diabolic spawns would have died!

In fact, after Tang Yunsheng’s mind was probed, he had already become an idiot, no different from a dead man.

“You three have suffered,” the creed leader consoled the trio. This was also his first time meeting Lu Yang, Meng Jingzhou, and Man Gu in person.

These are promising talents, the pillars of the diabolic creed, and future trusted aides.

Lu Yang, “...”

He had heard Tang Yunsheng cry out “creed leader” in his last moments. So this middle-aged man is the creed leader of the Everlasting Creed?

Did he just come out from the fifth backup base?

And the three of us even earned his trust?

A series of questions popped into Lu Yang’s mind.

Did we miss out on a step somewhere? We achieved our goal just like that?

Inside Lu Yang’s mental space, Yun Zhi remained expressionless, appearing detached from the mundane world. “Everything is according to plan.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy looked at Yun Zhi with admiration. This young lady is so impressive and so shrewd! I could never do that.

Meng Jingzhou and Man Gu also thought that this was part of Yun Zhi’s plan. As expected of Big Senior Sister! Nothing can escape her calculations! We have the trusty Big Senior Sister around, after all.

Only Lu Yang wore a peculiar expression; he suspected that all of this was merely a series of coincidences.

However, considering Yun Zhi’s power, he reckoned that even coincidences were a part of the plan.

Yes, Big Senior Sister’s plan is perfect.

Initially, the creed leader had felt that Lu Yang and the other two were talents with great potential, ideal to have their body taken over by the Everlasting Immortal. However, he was worried that the trio had died at the Dao-Seeking Sect. If they did make it out alive, it likely signified that they had been won over by the Dao-Seeking Sect, and he couldn’t ask them to participate in the test.

With Tang Yunsheng’s memory and the scene before him, all of the creed leader’s doubts had been dispelled. “You must keep the matter about Vice Creed Leader Jin a secret. I hope this is something only the four of us know.” He surmised that the accusation against Vice Creed Leader Jin was just a desperate slander by the two other vice creed leaders before they died.

The Everlasting Fairy nodded.

Yun Zhi nodded.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy had nodded halfway when she knitted her brow. “This person is so strange. Why do I sense a familiar aura from him?” The aura was too faint and required her concentration. “It seems like the Everlasting Dao Fruit but not quite the same. Strange.”

Hearing what the Everlasting Immortal Fairy had just muttered under her breath, Yun Zhi raised an eyebrow. She felt that the truth behind the Everlasting Creed was quite different from what she had imagined.

Then, the creed leader personally led Lu Yang and the other two into the fifth backup base, As the trio finally arrived at the Everlasting Creed’s headquarters, they realized that expectations could differ significantly from reality.

In their imagination, even if the Everlasting Creed’s headquarters did not evoke the imagery of mountains of corpses and seas of blood, there should minimally be an old devil hiding in the dark to intensify the horror atmosphere.

In reality, followers at the real headquarters were scuttling about, carrying bricks and sawing trees to build huts and altars for a massive construction project.

The creed leader casually explained, “To be on the safe side and avoid being tracked down by the Dao-Seeking Sect, our creed has just relocated. Although everything has been moved here, we still need to organize and rebuild them.

“You three came at the right time. Our creed is just about to begin an internal selection. A group of Foundation Establishment and Qi Training followers will be coming soon. All of you will compete, and the best will earn the favor of the Everlasting Immortal.

“Alright, I'll leave it at that. You three will be staying here for the time being. Someone will notify you when the selection starts. I still have matters to attend to.” The creed leader then left in a hurry.

The Everlasting Creed has no more usable backup bases. I'll need to choose three more backup sites as further backup.

He had been able to become the creed leader not just because of his cultivation, but also his cautiousness.

Chapter 187: The Thorough Creed Leader

Inside the mental space, two peerless women sat side by side, each displaying a unique charm that was a feast for the eyes. Yun Zhi held a scroll in her hand as she sat quietly with a scholarly aura, appearing aloof from the world, while the Everlasting Immortal Fairy lounged lazily with her limbs sprawled and yawned out of boredom, appearing isolated from the world.

“Little lass, do you still need to read the book page by page at our cultivation level? Can’t you just scan it with your spiritual consciousness and know everything instantly? The Everlasting Immortal yawned, not caring the slightest bit about her appearance.

Lu Yang kept shaking his head by the side. What a beautiful immortal fairy. It’s a pity that she talks.

Yun Zhi smiled as she shook her head. “Senior, you might not have known this, but the greatest joy in reading books is turning each and every page. You never know what surprise the next page holds. If you scan it with your spiritual consciousness, wouldn’t you miss out on this wonderful experience?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy mused over what Yun Zhi said and found it a good idea. “So what book are you reading?”

“How to Be a Good Big Senior Sister﻿.”

“That’s quite the interesting title.”

“Exactly. I wrote it.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy, “...”

Lu Yang casually asked, without any intention of fanning the flames. “Big Senior Sister, do you not mind that the Everlasting Immortal Fairy is calling you ‘little lass?’”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy glared at Lu Yang. Is this something the creed founder should be asking?

Yun Zhi nodded almost imperceptibly. “What Senior said isn’t wrong. Even if we disregard the fact that the era she lived in was three hundred thousand years in the past, judging just by her actual age, it’s not wrong for her to call me a little lass.”

Perhaps emboldened by her foolishness, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy stood her ground as she retorted, “Hey hey hey! I can’t pretend I didn’t hear that. I’m clearly only sixteen years old!”

Lu Yang joined the fray, “Immortal Fairy, are you referring to your intelligence or brain?

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy flew into a rage, clamoring about challenging Lu Yang to a duel. However, Lu Yang was not to be outdone and hid behind Yun Zhi.

“I dare you to come out!”

“I dare you to come out!”

Neither of them backed down.

While both of them made a racket, Yun Zhi quietly read her book by the side.

Halfway through their argument, Lu Yang suddenly remembered something. “Big Senior Sister, don’t you need to let your soul and consciousness drift outside to investigate the layout of this headquarters?”

Lu Yang and the other two were too low in cultivation to wander around, but it was different for Yun Zhi. She could let her soul and consciousness leave her body, and no one would notice.

In the real world, Lu Yang and the other two were cultivating diligently and did not venture anywhere.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy rolled her eyes. “You mean her? She has projected her soul outside a long time ago. What you see here is a clone of her soul that she left behind.”

If it weren’t just a soul clone, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy wouldn’t have dared talk to Yun Zhi like that.

Lu Yang remarked, “...Indeed, no one noticed.”

Including myself.

~~~

The Everlasting Creed didn’t lack stunning experts and outstanding talents, yet no one noticed a soul moving through the headquarters, silently observing something.

With Yun Zhi’s inexplicably deep cultivation, she could enter the headquarters of the Everlasting Creed as if it were a no-man’s land.

She discovered that the layout of the headquarters was very meticulously designed. There were altogether twenty-five exits. In the event of an emergency, the creed followers would escape from these exits, making it very difficult to capture them all.

However, Yun Zhi had already located all twenty-five exits and locked onto them with her soul. As long as she decided to take action, she could guarantee that no one would be able to leave the place, trapping them like turtles in a jar.

She also noted that the cave was somewhat desolate. It was probably a relic from the Great Yu Dynasty that the Everlasting Creed accidentally uncovered.

As Yun Zhi continued flying deeper into the headquarters, she noticed a secret chamber right at the end. There were a multitude of arrays around the secret chamber to prevent anyone from sneaking inside.

Except for Yun Zhi.

Yun Zhi entered the secret chamber and saw the creed leader worshipping the Everlasting Immortal. A wisp of smoke slowly wafted from within the Everlasting Immortal’s statue and morphed into the figure of an old man.

“Hmm?” Yun Zhi frowned.

Neither the creed leader nor the Everlasting Immortal noticed Yun Zhi’s presence, as she had perfectly concealed her breathing.

“Immortal, there is something I don’t understand. Please show me the answer.”

“Ask, child.”

“The ancient texts mention that you are bloodthirsty and fond of killing. To please you, we have slaughtered countless lives.”

“Dead beings are one of the sources of this immortal’s power.”

The creed leader furrowed his brow. “We don’t mind killing to restore you to your peak, Immortal, but times have been tough recently. The righteous path has been cracking down on us more vigorously. Our members are all struggling.

“A few days ago, I even organized a question-and-answer event on criminal law and a lecture on the exclusionary rule of illegally obtained evidence. I was trying to improve our followers’ education level and grasp of criminal law so that they can leave behind less evidence when committing crimes. If they do get caught, they can still defend themselves with their knowledge of criminal law.”

The Everlasting Immortal scratched his chin. “Are you asking me to organize a criminal law lecture too?”

“No, I noticed that our members’ learning abilities are worrying and that they dislike studying criminal law. In order to motivate them, I changed the design of your statue to hold a law book and spread the word that you also studied criminal law avidly.”

The Everlasting Immortal replied, “...Is there anything else?”

“Yes, I wanted to ask if your strength strictly stems from killing people. Does killing other beings work? Truth be told, my family used to run a slaughterhouse. Although we don’t do that anymore, I’m still familiar with the process inside out. What do you think about transforming the Everlasting Creed into the ‘Everlasting Slaughterhouse?’ We could wash off our tarnished reputation and climb ashore. That way, our members will be safe.

“We also have three talents adept at barbecuing. We could have them open a barbeque chain store and link it up with the slaughterhouse, building an entire industry value chain—we are killing many birds with one stone!”

Seeing that the Everlasting Immortal wanted to say something, the creed leader continued, “Are you concerned about the tax issues? Don’t worry about that! I was wanted because of massive tax evasion, so I had no choice but to join the diabolic path instead. When it comes to taxes, I’m a professional!” The creed leader’s voice was full of confidence, his eyes shining bright.

The Everlasting Immortal said, “...If there’s nothing else, can I go back now?”

“There’s one more minor thing.” The creed leader respectfully took out a few sheets of paper.

“What is this?”

“Evacuation drill plan. After all, we have relocated our headquarters and are still unfamiliar with the escape passages. In a while, we plan to carry out a large-scale evacuation drill by simulating an attack from the righteous path. Would you like to participate, Immortal?”

The Everlasting Immortal fell silent for a long time, contemplating if he should step down and let the creed leader take over as the creed’s faith instead.

“That’s not necessary. I can appear anywhere through my statues. The righteous path won’t be able to catch me. Also, hurry up with the trials. The sooner I take over a body, the sooner I can cultivate and return to my peak.”

“Oh.”

~~~

“Hmm? She’s back,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy suddenly said in the mental space, though Lu Yang couldn’t sense anything.

From the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s perspective, a golden light had flown in from the outside and merged with the Yun Zhi here.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was an immortal after all and did have some skill to show for it.

Yun Zhi put down her literary work; her expression was now different. Her delicate eyebrows were slightly knitted, as if she had discovered something. She looked toward the Everlasting Immortal Fairy and said hesitantly, “Senior... you’ve become fake.”

“Huh?!”

Chapter 188: Drill

Hearing Yun Zhi describe everything she had witnessed in the secret chamber, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy was infuriated.

“Which son of a turtle dares to impersonate me? Do they not know that I was undefeated across the land in ancient times? Anyone who saw me had to take a detour!”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy had reasons to be proud. After all, the cultivator who mastered Law Follows Words and was considered unmatched among their ranks had died by her hand.

“I sense a familiar aura from the creed leader. Could it have come from the one impersonating me?” The more the Everlasting Immortal Fairy thought about it, the more furious she became. She made a fuss, insisting that she wanted to confront the so-called Everlasting Immortal and expose his true colors.

Yun Zhi stopped the Everlasting Immortal. “Senior, please calm down. That self-proclaimed Everlasting Immortal can manifest at will within the Everlasting Immortal statues scattered across the continent. If he manages to escape, capturing him will be an uphill battle.”

“So, you are proposing that...”

“During the conversation between the creed leader and the Everlasting Immortal, there was mention of a selection trial. On the surface, its purpose is to pick out talents, but in reality, it is for the Everlasting Immortal to choose a suitable host for taking over their body. As long as we have Lu Yang become the target, the Everlasting Immortal will walk right into our trap. They wouldn’t be able to escape then.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy snapped out of her wrath. “Little lass, you’re really clever!”

“Hmm?” Yun Zhi raised an eyebrow.

Seeing the clueless Everlasting Immortal Fairy about to tick Yun Zhi off, he hurriedly slipped away. Big Senior Sister didn’t care about titles when her soul was away, but now that her soul is back, there’s no saying for sure.

Immortal Fairy, good luck.

“But what’s the deal with the Everlasting Immortal?” Lu Yang didn’t expect an Everlasting Immortal to appear. Was the fifth ancient immortal the Everlasting Immortal or the Everlasting Immortal Fairy?

From an emotional standpoint, he leaned toward the latter, but from a prestige standpoint, he leaned toward the former.

“Or could there have been a sixth immortal?”

Lu Yang opened his eyes, breaking away from his cultivation state. He sensed his current cultivation realm. “I should be at the Great Perfection Apex Intermediate Foundation Establishment Stage, only a half-step away from the Advanced Foundation Establishment Stage.”

“What are you going on about?” Meng Jingzhou grumbled as he dissociated from his cultivation state.

Man Gu mused, “Is such minute classification of cultivation realms one of the reasons Brother Lu is so strong?”

Meng Jingzhou quickly interrupted Man Gu. “Don’t think too much. It’s just another one of Lu Yang’s crazy antics again. Don’t join him.”

“The three of you, get ready for the drill!” A creed member at the entrance reminded the three.

Meng Jingzhou and Man Gu were flummoxed. Drill? What drill?

Sound amplification arrays everywhere blared, “Attention everyone! The righteous path is about to attack! Attention everyone! The righteous path is about to attack!”

Outside, there were even creed members screaming to heighten the atmosphere. “The righteous path is coming! We’re doomed!”

“Run for your lives!”

“We’d rather die than surrender.”

“Fight to the death with the righteous path!”

“Hahaha, those dogs from the righteous path, don’t think you can catch me!”

“Everlasting Immortal, please protect us!”

Then came the frenzied sounds of people running away.

Lu Yang remarked to himself, You guys are really getting into character.

Lu Yang briefly explained the matter of the drill to Meng Jingzhou and Man Gu, and they finally understood what was happening.

The trio hastily dashed out of the room, shouting as they ran, “Oh no, the Great Xia Dynasty and the Five Great Immortal Sects are attacking!”

The people in front glared at them. “Stop yelling nonsense. If the Great Xia Dynasty and the Five Great Immortal Sects really came, it would not be an evacuation drill but a capitulation drill!”

It was evident that the Everlasting Creed had outlined very detailed categories for their drills.

On the way out, Lu Yang saw creed followers swiftly packing their belongings into their storage rings, their practiced efficiency almost heartbreaking.

Some were wailing, vowing to stick with the headquarters no matter life or death, while others took advantage of the chaos to steal and made off with plenty of loot.

“Hey! What do you think you are doing?!” One of the members had caught a thief.

The other person took to their heels without turning back. “It’s a drill, right? The more realistic, the better. These are all possible scenarios!”

“Catch the thief!”

The Everlasting Creed was thrown into a frenzy; the drill felt almost too real.

Lu Yang and the other two followed the other members toward an exit.

After exiting, they didn’t know how much distance they covered until they arrived at a completely unfamiliar place.

The person bringing up the rear was Vice Creed Leader Jin. He destroyed the exit, severing all karma to prevent the righteous path from tracking them down. His smooth execution was evidence of his frequent training.

The followers applauded, celebrating the successful completion of the drill.

Only Man Gu had a question. “How are we going back?”

Silence fell across the crowd.

That’s right, we never sealed off the passageways in previous drills. Why did we cut it off this time?

With the passage disconnected and karma severed, there’s no way to get back!

Vice Creed Leader Jin felt a bit embarrassed. He had gotten too immersed in the drill, acting as if the righteous path was truly coming. However, he quickly came up with a solution.

“Don’t worry, everyone. I have a flying vessel in my storage ring that can carry all of you. We will fly back.”

With the plethora of experts in the headquarters, everyone else apart from Lu Yang’s group could fly. However, a large group of cultivators flying in the sky would easily attract the attention of the Great Xia Dynasty. If a few constables came over to investigate and ordered them to stop and present their identification documents, they would quickly realize that the whole bunch of them were high-profile fugitives, with the lightest punishment being life imprisonment.

Oh man, that would be quite the joke.

We might as well take the flying vessel and disguise ourselves as low-level cultivators renting a vessel for traveling, something common enough not to draw attention to ourselves.

Vice Creed Leader Jin pulled out a rather old-looking flying vessel from his storage ring. He had chosen this on purpose as the outdated design wouldn’t attract scrutiny from the officials.

Everyone was an old youtiao, a slick veteran who understood Vice Creed Leader Jin’s intention. They boarded the flying vessel and lowered their cultivation to display themselves as Qi Training cultivators. Suddenly, Lu Yang and his companions became the ones with the strongest cultivation.

On the flying vessel, Vice Creed Leader Jin reassured everyone, “It’s really no big deal. Judging by the speed of the flying vessel, by the time we get back, the other Foundation Establishment and Qi Training talents from the branches would have mostly arrived. The timing is just right.”

~~~

As the flying vessel cruised steadily, unbeknownst to the passengers onboard, danger was already at their doorstep.

Not far from the flying vessel, three mysterious figures in gray robes hovered in the air.

“What do you think about this flying vessel?”

“It’s not from the Luodi Merchant Guild or other major merchant guilds. It also looks pretty old. It’s probably rented.

“There are quite a few people on board, but their cultivation is nothing impressive—only three at the Foundation Establishment stage, just enough to be eliminated in one strike. Who knows, we might find them hiding some good stuff.”

“Shall we go in for the kill?”

“Let’s do it!”

The three figures turned into streaks of light, rapidly closing in on the flying vessel as they formed an array to trap it.

“Don’t move! This is a robbery!” One of them growled menacingly. Two scars ran across his face, a clear sign that he was an outlaw who disregarded lives.

“I believe you’ve also heard of the infamous Three Hu Brothers! As long as you hand over your valuables obediently, we guarantee that we won’t kill you!” Another person stuck out his tongue and licked the tip of his blade in a disturbingly perverted manner.

“If you refuse, don’t blame us for being ruthless!” The third person emitted a series of strange and ghost-like wails, sending chills down people’s spines.

“Don’t think we don’t dare to kill you. We have slain more people than you’ve ever seen!” They unleashed a frightening aura to intimidate everyone.

These three are actually at the Nascent Soul Stage!

Usually, as long as they released their aura waves, the other party would give up on the struggle, handing over their valuables as they beseeched them for mercy.

Whether or not they spared these people’s lives, however, depended entirely on their mood.

Then, the Three Hu Brothers noticed that the passengers on the flying vessel did not display any signs of fear. Instead, all of them were wearing an eerie smile.

One by one, the passengers let out their aura waves: Nascent Soul Stage, Divine Transfiguration Stage, Void Refinement Stage...

As the Three Hu Brothers experienced the aura waves that were beyond their realm of experience, they swallowed hard.

Oh no, we’re done for. Things seem to have gone wrong.

Vice Creed Leader Jin stood up, asking in an unruffled manner, “I heard that you have slain more people than I’ve ever seen?”

Chapter 189: Resounding Figure

“What are you trying to do?” The Three Hu Brothers trembled like leaves.

Vice Creed Leader Jin flashed a signature smirk. “Do you know who we are?”

“No...we don’t.”

“You don’t even know who we are? You deserve to die!”

The Three Hu Brothers hurriedly said, “No no no, we know who you are.”

“Since you know who we are, we can’t let you live anymore!”

The Three Hu Brothers were on the verge of tears. So should we or should we not know who you are?!

Vice Creed Leader Jin stopped toying with the three brothers, directly killing them with ease. The Three Hu Brothers were ultimately nothing more than a minor episode on their return journey.

The flying vessel continued traveling for some time before it was shrouded by several aura waves ranging from the Half-Step Divine Transfiguration to the Basic Divine Transfiguration stages.

“The Three Hu Brothers were supposed to have gotten in contact with us at a designated location, but they didn’t do so this time around. You were the only ones who passed by during that period. Did you kill my subordinates?” The eldest brother of the Three Hu Brothers wanted to take revenge.

Lu Yang mused, “Is this what they mean by ‘beat the young one and the old one comes?’”

He had heard of such tales where young chivalric heroes upheld justice. After beating the local bully, their father would appear. After beating the father, their grandfather would appear. After beating the grandfather, their great-grandfather would appear. There was no end to the revenge spanning the generations.

Lu Yang was extremely moved by their spirit of perseverance, just like how the foolish old man had attempted to move the mountains over multiple generations in the tale.

It went without saying that the big brother of the Three Hu Brothers was similarly squashed to death by Vice Creed Leader Jin.

The flying vessel continued on its course for some time. Suddenly, an even stronger surge of aura waves engulfed it.

“Were you the ones who killed...?”

Vice Creed Leader Jin was exasperated. “...Are you people never done?” As a Fusion expert, he was fed up with the repeated provocations. He decided to attack the source of the problem, storming their stronghold and wiping them out.

~~~

By the time the flying vessel returned to the headquarters, Vice Creed Leader Jin was holding a commendation silk banner with a look of utter defeat, as if he had lost all will to live.

The commendation banner was issued by the authorities, so no one suspected Vice Creed Leader Jin of belonging to a diabolic creed. After all, which diabolic creed would eradicate evil for the people?

When the creed followers heard about this, they whispered among themselves, filled with immense respect for Vice Creed Leader Jin.

“As expected of a vice creed leader! He could make the righteous path award him with a commendation banner and effectively play both sides, a testament to his incredible influence!”

“Exactly! I heard that before Vice Creed leader Jin joined the diabolic creed, he was a resounding figure of the righteous path!”

Lu Yang was quite surprised to hear that. I didn’t know that Vice Creed Leader Jin was so renowned in the righteous path. He hurriedly asked, “Vice Creed Leader Jin had such a background? What did he do in the righteous path?”

“He was a night watchman.”

Lu Yang, “...”

“Vice Creed Leader Jin could also control time when he was with the righteous path, right?” Lu Yang finally came up with a response.

The creed follower gave Lu Yang a look of surprise. “This is something I haven't uncovered!”

The creed follower ran to Vice Creed Leader Jin and relayed Lu Yang's idea. Vice Creed Leader Jin was very delighted and personally approached Lu Yang to praise him for his out-of-the-box thinking.

“What a great idea! From now on, I'll tell others that I was once a resounding figure in the righteous path who could even control the time of a city!”

For those in the diabolic path, the most important thing was to speak the truth while also embellishing their reputation as much as possible.

Although Lu Yang had caused trouble in the entry examinations Vice Creed Leader Jin had designed, these were all in the past. Now, the more Vice Creed Leader Jin looked at Lu Yang, the more he liked him.

As the flying vessel had met with some delays on its journey, Lu Yang and his two companions were the last to arrive. The Foundation Establishment and Qi Training talents from the various regions had already gathered.

Lu Yang scanned the Qi Training cultivators and concluded that they posed no threat, so he placed his attention on the Foundation Establishment cultivators. He had learned of a few famous Foundation Establishment geniuses based on what he had heard from passers-by.

“Do you see that monk over there with the robes and beard, holding a golden alms bowl? He's called the Fleshly Monk. I heard that he originally had a chance to enter the Hanging Monastery, one of the Five Great Immortal Sects, but he suddenly gave it up and made a grand vow to find the way to achieving enlightenment on his own!

“And the one holding a blade next to him, could he be the legendary Saber Devil, Ancient Piercer? Legends have it that his devil saber is very sinister. The moment the forging process was completed, the devil saber floated into the air and killed the blacksmith. Every subsequent owner of the saber, including Divine Transfiguration cultivators suffered from its backlash. Only the Ancient Piercer has wielded the saber up until now!

“The most powerful is Flying Swallow. Everyone says that he is a prodigy the creed leader has personally groomed. He is well-versed in drawing talismans and has even used talismans to trap several Golden Core cultivators, toying with them before killing them with utterly cruel methods!

Needless to say, all three were at the Advanced Foundation Establishment Stage.

Lu Yang transmitted auditory messages to the other two. “Let’s not get close to them yet. The three of us will pretend we don’t know one another. The contents of the examination are still unknown. Depending on the situation, we’ll decide whether we team up.”

The only ones who know about the ingrained diabolic nature of Lu Yang’s trio were the creed leader and a few higher-ups. These Foundation Establishment cultivators had never even heard of Lu Yang’s name.

Just then, the creed leader appeared in the air with his hands behind his back. He wore a cold expression as he announced the rules of the competition.

Everyone noticed a mark with the number “one” on their hands, though they didn't know when it had appeared.

“In this trial, you can kill as you please. When you kill someone, you will gain the number of points they had, as indicated by the mark.

“The person with the most points will be the final victor and receive the blessings of the Everlasting Immortal.”

Everyone except the fake followers, Lu Yang and friends, revealed fervent expressions. To obtain the blessings of the Everlasting Immortal was the highest honor in the Everlasting Creed.

“Foundation Establishment cultivators will be in one category, and Qi Training cultivators will be in another category. Each category will have one winner. The duration of the trial will be two days.”

Lu Yang thought to himself, As expected of a diabolic creed to have trials about killing people. Aren't they afraid that everyone will be killed off and there will be no successors?

As the creed leader flung his sleeves, everyone suddenly appeared in a secret forest with no chance of resistance.

“This is a forest from the Great Yu Dynasty. There are all kinds of natural treasures hidden here. You can not only slaughter but also find fortuitous opportunities to break through.

“Remember, the Everlasting Immortal is watching you.” The creed leader gave everyone a hint, but only Lu Yang understood what it truly meant.

“Let the competition begin.”

After announcing the commencement of the competition, the creed leader asked the Everlasting Immortal with deference, “Why do you use such a method to choose a vessel to take over? Wouldn't it be more efficient to select someone directly based on their aptitude?”

The Everlasting Immortal replied with a benevolent smile. “Child, what do you think is key to becoming the strongest? Single Spirit Root? Celestial Physique? None of these matter. Even if you have a trash physique, as long as I am willing, I can still take over your body and cultivate until the Transcendent Tribulation Stage or even become an immortal.

“The most important thing is the vessel’s compatibility with me.

“A life-and-death trial is best for displaying one's potential. What I need is for them to showcase their abilities as much as possible. Through my observation, I'll be able to choose the lucky one who has the highest compatibility with me.”

The creed leader asked further, “Do those with high compatibility exhibit any special characteristics?”

“Whoever I find pleasing to the eye.”

“Then do you find me pleasing to the eye?”

“You are the least pleasing to the eye.”

“But I am your most devout follower!” the creed leader protested with much grievance.

Chapter 190: Great Fortuitous Opportunities!

An all-out massacre unfolded in the secret forest, each and every battle so intense that it sent chills creeping down people's backs.

The diabolic path was vicious and full of crafty schemes. Everyone poured in all they had, unleashing their innate talents and true nature.

The Fleshly Monk, Saber Devil Ancient Piercer, and Flying Swallow needed no further elaboration; they were the favorites. Apart from the three of them, there were many people who usually kept a low profile but stunned everyone with their performances in this trial.

Meng Jingzhou and Man Gu were especially outstanding. Several people had either fallen at their hands, gotten pierced through by iron fists, or pulverized to a clump by iron hammers.

Their reputation gradually spread, and contestants who were aware of their ruthlessness hoped to avoid confrontation with them.

Meng Jingzhou and Man Gu’s fists and hammers were stained with blood. They had bloodshot eyes, and their whole body radiated with a murderous energy. It was clear at a glance that they were merciless people who killed without blinking an eye, likely having gone mad from the slaughter.

The Ancient Barbarian Tribe’s blood in Man Gu was stimulated further. In ancient times, wars raged ceaselessly. As one of the strongest tribes, the Ancient Barbarian Tribe had no shortage of wars. The blood coursing through Man Gu’s veins encompassed bloody battles and an indomitable spirit...as well as Huang Doudou’s Tame Head Curse. [1]

“I've never heard of these two people before. Where did they come from? Their strength seems to match up to the Fleshly Monk. Look, even the Fleshly Monk isn't willing to bump into them and keeps his activities confined to other areas!”

“They probably obtained some legacy somewhere, or maybe they're spawns groomed by the elders in secret!”

“I can't help but wonder who edges out between the two of them.”

Avid discussions about Meng Jingzhou and Man Gu broke out.

Meng Jingzhou was invincible with his iron fists. With just one punch, he crushed a rather well-known Intermediate Foundation Establishment cultivator.

As Meng Jingzhou was currently at the Intermediate Foundation Establishment Stage, a disciple of the Dao-Seeking Sect, and a descendant of the Meng Family’s main branch, he could be considered invincible among his peers outside the Dao-Seeking Sect.

Recitations from Words of Sages echoed around Man Gu, who didn’t even blink with every strike of his hammer. The uncanny sense of incongruity made him appear like a madman.

Finally, the two met, their eyes ablaze with an intractable spirit; neither was willing to bow down to the other person.

Man Gu raised his massive hammer as he hollered, “State your name!”

“I’m Meng Jingzhou! Who are you?”

“Man Gu.”

Both were men of few words, immediately beginning to fight.

As they were the cream of the crop among the Foundation Establishment cultivators, once they clashed, the earth shattered, and trees snapped in half or were crushed to smithereens from the shockwaves of the battle.

Other competitors observed from a distance, hoping the two sides would go down together. That way, these people would be at an advantage when facing either of the two later, just like how the fisherman would benefit from the fight between the snipe and the clam. Meng Jingzhou and Man Gu possessed incredibly high points as indicated by the marks on their hands, a sum that tempted everyone. Whoever managed to kill them would be able to gain all those points!

~~~

As the Fleshly Monk and Saber Devil Ancient Piercer watched from the shadows, their hearts were secretly racing.

“These two people are no less dangerous than Flying Swallow!”

“They’re so powerful but still inferior to me. While I still have trump cards yet to be revealed, I’ve already seen through them.”

“I didn’t expect to meet such formidable opponents apart from Flying Swallow and Fleshly Monk this time. This place is truly full of hidden dragons and crouching tigers!”

“Perfect timing! My devil saber is thirsty. The blood of those trash weaklings wasn’t enough to satiate it, but the blood of these two peerless talents will be its favorite!”

~~~

Meng Jingzhou laughed heartily. “Hahaha, what a thrilling battle! It’s been a long time since I’ve encountered a worthy opponent!”

Man Gu was equally exhilarated, the Ancient Barbarian Tribe’s blood boiling as it surged through his veins.

Another old tree fell during their battle. After it gave way, a Bodhi tree appeared before the two. On the tree were three little dolls swaying in the wind, while the Bodhi tree exuded a calming presence, depicting a sacred image.

Meng Jingzhou was astounded. “It’s a Bodhi Ginseng Fruit Tree?!”

“Ginseng Fruit?” Man Gu was similarly shocked.

Both people tacitly chose to cease fire in front of a sacred entity.

Man Gu was half in disbelief. “Is this the legendary Ginseng Fruit Tree?”

Meng Jingzhou nodded. “It can’t be wrong. Look at the three plump little dolls growing on the tree. Aren’t they exactly the Ginseng Fruits in the legend?”

Man Gu continued to ask, “But why would Ginseng Fruits grow on a Bodhi Tree?”

Meng Jingzhou gave him a side-eye. “That’s because you don’t know how rare Ginseng Fruits are! You can’t find a single Ginseng Fruit Tree in the world. That’s because there’s no such thing as a Ginseng Fruit Tree!

“Ginseng Fruits are born from the cadence of the union between heaven and earth. It will only appear on other trees. When a tree has amassed sufficient essence from heaven and earth, it will grow Ginseng Fruits naturally.

“Among all the trees, the Bodhi tree is the most mystical and surrounded by many legends. It’s the ideal tree for Ginseng Fruits to grow on!”

Man Gu felt like he had seen the light. This is something I’ve never considered.

It was a great fortuitous opportunity to have the Ginseng Fruits before them. There was no need to continue fighting. Even if each of them took one, they would still have an additional one left.

Initially, everyone else didn’t recognize the Ginseng Fruits. However, they were convinced after listening to Meng Jingzhou’s logical and rational explanation. They were also reminded of what the creed leader had mentioned about great fortuitous opportunities in this secret forest.

Could they be these three Ginseng Fruits?

“Charge!”

The spectators originally hidden in the dark swarmed toward the tree in a frenzy, determined to snatch at least one Ginseng Fruit!

The Saber Devil Ancient Piercer tossed out his projectile of cow-hair needles. Sensing the covert weapons, Meng Jingzhou and Man Gu leaped backward, dodging the attack.

As the two were now a distance from the Ginseng Fruits, it created an opening for the others. Even if the competition included tough opponents such as Meng Jingzhou and the Fleshly Monk, everyone was willing to risk it all. As long as they could secure a Ginseng Fruit, their cultivation journey from now onward would be a smooth-sailing one.

It was worth putting everything on the line!

The Saber Devil Ancient Piercer was the first to grab one of the Ginseng Fruits. Wasting no time, he bolted right away. “So this is a Ginseng Fruit? Its texture feels like flesh. No wonder it’s called a Ginseng Fruit!”

The rest were seized with regret as they pursued him relentlessly. However, the Saber Devil Ancient Piercer was faster at navigating the dense forest, successfully shaking them off in no time.

It is mine only when it is refined. Living by this principle, the Saber Devil Ancient Piercer took a bite.

He couldn’t bite into it.

“Could it be that although the Ginseng Fruit has a flesh-like texture, it becomes extremely hard once you try to eat it?”

Just as he was mulling over how he could consume the Ginseng Fruit, his expression changed drastically.

“Damn, there’s poison!” A look of incredulity spread across his face. The surface of the Ginseng Fruit was laced with poison!

Who could’ve done this? On a Ginseng Fruit, no less! Poisoning something as precious as this is sacrilegious!

Suddenly, the Ginseng Fruit spoke, “Has no one ever told you not to eat random fruits by the roadside?”

As regret nearly suffocated the Saber Devil Ancient Piercer, the Ginseng Fruit, the Ginseng Fruit moved.

The three-inch-tall Lu Yang stretched lazily. After pretending to be a Ginseng Fruit for so long, I can finally move again.

This was a new technique he had comprehended while being tormented by his senior brothers and sisters in the Dao-Seeking Sect. He would first use To Inches, then Shrinking Earth, and finally the Tree-Planting Mantra. This combination allowed three miniature Lu Yangs to grow from the Bodhi Tree. With Meng Jingzhou and Man Gu as his shills, his status elevated to that of a Ginseng Fruit.

In passing, he also coated himself in a layer of lethal poison. Anyone capable of laying their hands on the Ginseng Fruits will undoubtedly have a high cultivation. I’ll make sure to poison them all.

“That’s all you got for someone from the diabolic path? So gullible.” Lu Yang shook his head in disdain as he finished off the Ancient Piercer.

This cohort of diabolic cultivators is truly not up to standard. It only took the three of us from the righteous path to have them wrapped around our fingers.

1. Jiangtou or “Tame Head” is a type of witchcraft and curse. There seem to be three types of Jiangtou, herb, flying and ghost. ☜

Chapter 191: Devil Saber

The mark on Lu Yang’s palm displayed the number “one,” while it read “eighty-seven” for the Ancient Piercer. After Lu Yang killed the Ancient Piercer, his mark changed to “eighty-eight.”

“So this is that infamous devil saber? It killed all its previous owners with the Ancient Piercer being the temporary exception?”

From how the Ancient Piercer casually tossed his things around, it was evident that he hardly bore any sense of morality. Lu Yang even had to pick them up for him.

The devil saber was dark red. Its hilt appeared to be crafted from the horn of some colossal demon beast. A ruby red gemstone resembling an eye was inlaid where the hilt joined the blade. Apart from its strange design, Lu Yang found nothing else of note.

“Hmm, this saber is quite interesting,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy suddenly remarked. “The hilt is forged from the horn of a jiao dragon, while the blade is made from refined steel. As for the crimson gemstone, it’s actually the eye of the demon beast called the ‘fei ox.’”

The fei ox[1] was a powerful large demon beast that roamed the wilderness. It had the body of an ox, a white head, a snake’s tail, and only one eye.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy finally played her role as a golden finger cheat, explaining the intriguing traits of the saber to Lu Yang.

“The materials used are stellar. If forged properly, this saber can develop a spiritual nature. However, the blacksmith’s skills were inadequate, crafting a mere shell. That said, even if it is an empty shell, it is still a rare treasure. This saber instinctively craves a spiritual nature, which is why it lusts for blood and slaughter. The more it kills, the more likely it can develop a spiritual nature.”

Lu Yang asked, “How does it acknowledge a new master?”

“You just have to drip your blood on it.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy proceeded to advise, “But I wouldn’t recommend you to claim it. This saber is extremely greedy and insatiable. If you become its master, the more blood you feed it, the more it desires to consume its master. Even if you don’t feed it blood, it will still turn on you.”

In ancient times, there were also magical treasures with similar characteristics. The Everlasting Immortal Fairy had witnessed numerous self-assured geniuses who believed they were special and capable of taming such magical treasures. From the results though, only a handful ever succeeded.

“So that’s how it is.” Lu Yang finally understood why the devil saber’s previous wielders were all killed by it. The blade had never intended to let its master live. “It’s an interesting saber.”

“The only reason the Ancient Piercer hasn’t suffered from the backlash is that he had wielded the saber for too short a time.”

Lu Yang asked another question, “If this devil saber develops a spiritual nature, how powerful would it be?”

“In any case, it’s not even worthy enough to be my stepping stone,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy replied in contempt.

Lu Yang let out an “oh.” Looks like this devil saber’s quality isn’t anything impressive.

All this while, Yun Zhi had been quietly reading her book. She was confident that Lu Yang’s trio would have no trouble winning the competition

During their conversation, the mark on Lu Yang’s palm had changed twice, jumping from “88” to “131.”

As the Fleshly Monk became the center of everyone’s attention, he failed to acquire a Ginseng Fruit. Instead, two somewhat well-known Foundation Establishment cultivators managed to lay their hands on the remaining Ginseng Fruits. Without any exception, both were poisoned to death.

Since the other Ginseng Fruits were too far away, Lu Yang couldn't sense the state of his Ginseng Fruit clones. He deactivated his clone state and reverted to his original height. Storing the devil saber in his storage ring, he began searching for his next target.

The storage ring was something he had prepared at the last minute. After all, he couldn’t use the Dao-Seeking Sect’s identity jade tablet as a storage ring; that would be overly brazen.

“Hmm? Whose blood is this?” Lu Yang noticed a few spots of fresh blood on the ground nearby, seemingly left behind by someone injured while fleeing.

“I should follow and take a look.” Since they’re injured, their combat power will undoubtedly be weaker. These are practically free points at my doorstep.

Just as Lu Yang had deduced, the closer he got to the injured person, the more obvious the blood trail became; what had started as a few drops was now a puddle, clearly indicating that the person was gravely injured.

Finally, Lu Yang caught up to the injured individual—it was the Fleshly Monk!

The Fleshly Monk’s large hand was currently choking a person. With a sharp crack, he snapped the person’s neck.

“Yet another one lured into my trap.” The Fleshly Monk revealed a cruel smile.

During the battle for the Ginseng Fruits, he had pretended to be outnumbered and fled while injured, drawing several competitors to chase him. Then, one by one, he killed them all.

“I can’t help that I’m too infamous. If I hadn’t done this, I wouldn’t have been able to find anyone to take out,” the Fleshly Monk explained with a grin. As one of the top three seeded contestants, everyone else ran at the mere sight of him, leaving him no chance to exchange blows with someone.

I might as well deliberately expose a weakness and let the fish take the bait.

The Fleshly Monk mused, “Hmm? You look familiar, but whatever. Regardless of who you are, count yourself unlucky that you’ve run into me!” He had found Lu Yang familiar because the Ginseng Fruit looked like the latter, as if they were father and son. However, the Fleshly Monk didn’t have time to connect the dots yet.

As the Fleshly Monk clenched his fists and stretched his muscles taut, his bleeding wounds healed instantly. Whipping out a golden alms bowl, he was ready to trap Lu Yang.

Lu Yang silently retrieved the devil saber from his storage ring, squatted down, and smeared it with the blood left behind by the Fleshly Monk.

The devil saber immediately acknowledged the Fleshly Monk as its new master.

It hovered in the air before thrusting toward the Fleshly Monk with a whoosh. Perhaps the devil saber had never encountered such a generous master before and wanted to give its new master a warm embrace—with the blade’s edge.

Color drained from the Fleshly Monk’s face. Where did the devil saber come from? Why is it attacking me?

The devil saber pierced through the golden alms bowl that had accompanied the Fleshly Monk for years, while the Fleshly Monk struggled in the battle.

Lu Yang clicked his tongue from the sidelines. “With skills like that, how did he catch the eye of the Hanging Monastery?”

The Hanging Monastery was the smallest of the Five Great Immortal Sects, only accepting exceptionally gifted disciples. Based on the Fleshly Monk’s abilities, he’d be lucky to qualify as a servant in the Hanging Monastery.

The Fleshly Monk refuted as he fought, “The Hanging Monastery claims that everyone has a chance to join. I naturally had the chance to join them. I simply chose not to!”

“...You really know how to flatter yourself.”

The Fleshly Monk was powerless against the devil saber, which pierced his heart in one fluid motion.

The devil saber was once again without a master.

“What a pity. It just accepted a new master, and now he’s gone.”

Lu Yang picked up the devil saber and continued on his journey.

“Blood Deluges the Yellow Springs[2]!” Someone who had their sights set on Lu Yang launched a sneak attack.

A crimson wave reeking of blood gushed toward Lu Yang.

Lu Yang remained calm and unhurried as he fished out the devil saber again. As someone with a Sword Spirit Root, he had a natural affinity with sabers and swords; comprehending saber techniques was not a difficult task for him.

He performed a saber technique he had just invented.

“Master Acknowledgement Saber Technique!”

The devil saber slashed through the blood-red torrent of water, just like a shark that had smelled blood. Gleaming with an eerie red light, it stabbed through Lu Yang’s attacker once more.

“Raging Waves Bloody Palm!”

“Master Acknowledgement Saber Technique!”

“Blood Skeleton!”

“Master Acknowledgement Saber Technique!”

As expected of a diabolic creed, the techniques they practiced were either related to vengeful ghosts and skeletons or blood and souls of the dead. They were perfect candidates for the devil saber’s master.

Relying on just the Master Acknowledgement Saber Technique, Lu Yang became undefeatable. Unfortunately, all the owners of the devil saber were short-lived individuals—not a single person lasted more than three seconds before suffering from the backlash.

Lu Yang shook his head regretfully. All I wanted was to find a master for the devil saber. Why is it so hard?

“Such a fine magical treasure, yet none of you have the fortune of wielding it.”

~~~

More and more people learned of Lu Yang’s existence, with rumors circulating that he had become the new master of the devil saber and killed indiscriminately, a more ruthless individual than the Ancient Piercer.

Some people also noticed Lu Yang’s striking resemblance to the Ginseng Fruits. Associating it with those poisoned to death, they deduced that the Ginseng Fruits had been a ruse all along.

In the dense forest, Lu Yang had bumped into Meng Jingzhou after the devil saber impaled another master as usual.

Meng Jingzhou glared at Lu Yang with gritted teeth. “Well played, huh? You disguised yourself as Ginseng Fruits and fooled everyone!”

1. The Fei is once again from the Shan Hai Jing. It is a fierce beast with one eye and looks like an ox with the tail of a snake. ☜

2. Huangquan or “Yellow Springs” refers to the underworld. ☜

Chapter 192: Six Directions Eight Corners Immortal Art

Lu Yang’s infamy overshadowed even Flying Swallow, who was hailed as the creed leader’s successor, much less the rising stars that had deliberately concealed their strength and hoped to shine in this competition. He had tricked everyone with his disguise as the Ginseng Fruits. Subsequently, when he wielded the devil saber, every slash of the blade struck fear into people’s hearts. No one knew the exact number of points displayed on his palm, but they could be certain of one thing—it was a terrifying number.

On the other hand, Meng Jingzhou was someone with genuine skills and was unfazed by Lu Yang’s fearsome reputation. “Hmph, I’ve heard that death is inevitable once your devil saber draws blood. In that case, I’ll just have to make sure I don’t get hurt.”

Lu Yang raised an eyebrow. “Such big talk! State your name!”

“Meng Jingzhou!”

“So it’s you. I’ve long heard that you’re unbeatable among the Foundation Establishment cultivators and that your exceptional mastery over the body tempering arts has won the admiration of countless physique cultivators!”

Meng Jingzhou snorted coldly. “You’re not bad yourself, Blood Sea Blade Devil Lu Yang. Your ferocious name alone is enough to silence the cries of children. Everyone says that you are stronger than Flying Swallow, but I have my doubts about that!”

“You’ll just have to find out!”

“Then let me find out!”

The clash of the two most prominent seeded contenders attracted the attention of not just the other participants secretly watching from the shadows but also the higher-ups of the Everlasting Creed. They were curious to know who exactly would emerge victorious between the two.

Would it be the crafty and treacherous Lu Yang or the upright and aboveboard Meng Jingzhou?

The creed leader and vice creed leader could feel their eyes twitching as they silently observed the scene unfolding before them. If they hadn’t already known that these two were on the same side, they might have been convinced that they were truly strangers.

Their pretense is really convincing.

Vice Creed Leader Jin finally acknowledged that the creed leader possessed keen judgment. No wonder he had evaluated this duo as “Innate Diabolic Spawn” and “Descended Dao Diabolic.”

I wouldn’t believe it even if someone told me that they were spies from the righteous path.

Oh right, I almost forgot about Man Gu.

~~~

Flying Swallow hid in the bushes as he watched the battle, feeling the immense pressure from his two enemies. These two people are worthy to be my opponent. In fact, they pose an even greater threat than the dead Fleshly Monk and Ancient Piercer.

Lu Yang wielded his saber with his sword technique, every strike of his unstoppable, while Meng Jingzhou had refined his whole body, including his teeth, and showed no weakness. It felt as if the two of them could even fight a Golden Core cultivator.

The other contestants watched in terror, thinking that the duo were absolute monsters.

Finally, Lu Yang proved to be slightly superior and defeated Meng Jingzhou. The latter knew he was no match for Lu Yang and bolted before sustaining any injuries.

The crowd sighed. If Meng Jingzhou had been injured, they could have joined forces to hunt him down.

Having killed the Ancient Piercer, the Fleshly Monk, and defeated Meng Jingzhou, Lu Yang’s reputation soared to an unprecedented peak. Whenever Lu Yang unleashed his saber techniques, countless people would be slain. Even Man Gu, who never knew the definition of fear, avoided direct confrontation with Lu Yang, fleeing at the sight of him.

Just as everyone assumed that Lu Yang would become the strongest contender in the competition, Meng Jingzhou made a fierce comeback. The latter beamed with radiance and spirit, unlike his troubled state from his previous defeat.

“Lu Yang, let’s fight again!”

Lu Yang sneered. “You've suffered defeat at my hands, yet you dare to challenge me again? Die!” He swung the devil saber down heavily, aiming to cleave Meng Jingzhou into two.

The crowd gasped. He’s giving it his all right from the get-go! This was how Meng Jingzhou lost the last time!

Just when everyone thought this strike would decide the outcome of the battle, Meng Jingzhou defied expectations and blocked the saber.

Noticing that Meng Jingzhou was different this time, Lu Yang cast away his haughtiness and fought with all his might.

Compared to their previous battle, Meng Jingzhou’s combat power had surged. Now, he was evenly matched with Lu Yang.

“Huff...huff...you’ve had a fortuitous encounter!” Lu Yang suddenly discovered the source of the problem. That was the only explanation for Meng Jingzhou’s newfound strength.

This battle gave Meng Jingzhou tremendous confidence. “I’ve only learned the basics, yet my combat power has already shot up. As expected of the Six Directions...” Meng Jingzhou realized that he had misspoken and immediately shut his mouth.

Man Gu heard the first few words Meng Jingzhou had uttered and fell into deep thought, muttering to himself, “Six Directions? Could it be the legendary Six Directions Eight Corners Immortal Art?!”

The crowd quickly pressed Man Gu for details about the cultivation technique, but he refused to answer and escaped without a trace.

“Six Directions Eight Corners Immortal Art? Could it be the Everlasting Immortal’s legacy?”

The crowd broke out in soft gasps. The character “immortal” in the technique’s name was bound to engender wild speculation.

The battle between Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou ended in a draw. Both parties understood that continuing to fight would reap no results, so they tacitly parted ways.

After Meng Jingzhou disappeared for a day, he reemerged with a more fiery aura. This time, he directly looked for Lu Yang, who was dressed in a cloak.

To everyone’s astonishment, Meng Jingzhou’s combat power had soared once more, successfully defeating Lu Yang!

The Six Directions Eight Corners Immortal Art is so terrifying!

“Die!” Meng Jingzhou hollered as his palm pierced through Lu Yang’s chest.

Lu Yang coughed up blood uncontrollably, his life force draining away rapidly. Although Lu Yang’s tenacious vitality prevented him from dying immediately, his demise was already an inevitable fate.

“Haha! You, Meng Jingzhou, to think that you were the one to seize the greatest fortuitous opportunity!” Lu Yang’s face was twisted into a grimace, perhaps not resigned to dying just like that.

As he pulled out a tattered old book from his robes, Meng Jingzhou’s pupils constricted.

“Why is the immortal art with you?! You stole it during our fight!” Meng Jingzhou growled.

The crowd was in an uproar. Lu Yang had stolen the immortal art during their battle? What kind of skill was that? Is it the legendary Miracle Empty Hands Thieving?

A burning desire enveloped the crowd. If the immortal art is now in the dying Lu Yang’s hands, doesn’t that mean that anyone can potentially claim it?

Lu Yang smirked as he continued to cough blood. “What a shame. I’m fortunate enough to steal the immortal art but I don’t have the chance to cultivate it. Since that’s the case, I’ll reveal the immortal art publicly and see what advantage you have left, Meng Jingzhou!” He tossed the book out and used his blood as ink to write its entire text in the air.

A gargantuan fortuitous opportunity!

Meng Jingzhou’s eyes widened in rage as he hurriedly dispersed the blood characters to prevent the immortal art from being spread further. However, it was too late. Everyone present was a Foundation Establishment Cultivator. They could memorize all the contents with just a single glance.

Lu Yang laughed out maniacally before drawing his last breath.

Meng Jingzhou was overwhelmed with fury, but there was nothing he could do to salvage the situation.

The crowd scattered, hoping to seek a safe place to cultivate the immortal art.

~~~

“Why am I not becoming stronger after cultivating the immortal art?” someone questioned. Didn’t Meng Jingzhou become very powerful right after he practiced it?

“Am I doing it wrong?”

~~~

In the dense forest, Lu Yang and the other two were gathered together, their eyes shut as they sensed the positions of the others.

There was no immortal art; it was a position-tracking cultivation technique. As long as someone cultivated it, Lu Yang’s trio would be able to detect their location.

What’s the biggest problem with battles in dense forests? It’s the uncertainty of enemies’ locations! Now that all the contestants are scattered and hidden, it’s the perfect opportunity to strike them down one by one!

The trio set out together, starting their offense from those nearest. With every opponent they slaughtered, the number on their palms soared rapidly.

~~~

Flying Swallow was not in a rush to cultivate the new technique. He couldn’t help but feel that something was amiss. When he found Lu Yang’s corpse, he lifted the hood and was flabbergasted to see a bald Lu Yang.

It’s the clone from the Bodhi tree!

Everything was a lie!

He swiftly concluded, “Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou are together! There’s no such thing as the ‘Six Directions Eight Corners Immortal Art!’ Man Gu is also in it with them!”

~~~

In the distance, the creed leader wore an odd expression after witnessing the whole sequence of events.

As a leader of the diabolic path, even he felt that the trio was too devious.

~~~

Inside the mental space, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy noticed that Yun Zhi was still pensive and was quite curious. “What are you thinking about?”

Yun Zhi sighed. “I’m just wondering... will these three really not get beaten to death?”

Yun Zhi was not at all worried that the trio couldn’t win the competition. What she feared more was that they would be beaten to death before they could claim victory.

Chapter 193: Fusion!

To develop his own cultivation techniques, Lu Yang had spent several months studying on the first floor of the scripture library. Apart from the Comprehensive Xiangsheng Comedy Compendium, the books contained numerous cultivation techniques and spells that broadened his horizons.

For instance, a cultivation technique could reveal one’s location to another party when one cultivated it. Records indicated that a pair of married cultivators wrote it to monitor each other's whereabouts. Then, the husband discovered that his wife often went to brothels, and the wife also discovered that her husband often went to brothels.

Other than this cultivation technique, Lu Yang also came across a cultivation technique for sleeping with one’s eyes open, which would be especially useful during lessons.

There was also a cultivation technique that could make oneself very ugly, though Lu Yang still hadn’t figured out what purpose such a technique could serve.

Another cultivation technique for winter hibernation was modeled after animals, allowing one to eat and sleep for an entire season. Lu Yang still couldn’t fathom how it could come in useful.

Later, Lu Yang finally understood. This is how the senior brothers and sisters rack up their contribution points.

By submitting cultivation techniques without a backup to the Great Mission Hall, one could earn contribution points. Yun Zhi used to only take on this mission, forcing the Great Mission Hall to set up a new column for her. She no longer had to submit her cultivation techniques every single time. Once she had finished writing them, she could just place them in the scripture library and use contribution points however she wished.

Other senior disciples lacked Yun Zhi’s level of capability, yet they still desired contribution points. As a result, the scripture library contained numerous techniques that seemed impressive but were ultimately worthless.

Lu Yang suspected that if he were to also write such cultivation techniques, Yun Zhi would likely hang him up and give him a beating.

Oh, she probably doesn’t even need to do it herself. The puppet can do the job.

“Six Directions Eight Corners Immortal Art?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy seemed to have been reminded of something when she heard the name Lu Yang had randomly fabricated.

“The name sounds very similar to the Nine-Layers Immortal’s cultivation technique!”

“Nine-Layers Immortal?” Lu Yang repeated; the Everlasting Immortal Fairy hardly mentioned this immortal. He had only learned from her that the Nine-Layers Immortal possessed a celestial physique and was the first among the five ancient immortals to ascend to an immortal.

Lu Yang was puzzled. “What was his cultivation technique called?”

Yun Zhi was also intrigued, which was a rare occurrence. She put down her book and waited for the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s reply.

“The Nine-Layers Immortal also wrote his own cultivation technique, and he named it Primal Chaos, One Qi, Two Origins,[1] Four Divisions,[2] Six Directions, Eight Corners, Nine Lands, Ten Heavens, Only I Reign Supreme Immortal Art.

“I usually just call his cultivation technique Numbers Immortal Art. Sometimes people also call it the Four Six Immortal Art, Eight Ten Immortal Art, or they’ll just go with whatever sounds pleasant. In any case, the Nine-Layers Immortal himself can’t even remember the full name of his own cultivation technique.

Lu Yang, “...”

Does the Nine-Layers Immortal have some obsession with numbers?

Yun Zhi was also somewhat speechless. Originally, she had hoped to deduce the other party’s strengths and weaknesses based on the name of their cultivation technique. However, it now seemed like she had been overly optimistic.

While Lu Yang was listening to ancient tales inside his mental space and going around killing people with Meng Jingzhou and Man Gu outside, he suddenly heard the Flying Swallow’s shout.

“Lu Yang, Meng Jingzhou, and Man Gu are in cahoots!” The Flying Swallow had done it on purpose. The pressure from Lu Yang and the other two was too much for him. No matter how strong I am, I won’t be able to defeat these powerful and devious bastards. I must rally everyone’s strength to get rid of these three. That’s the only way I have a chance to win!

“We’re exposed this early?” Meng Jingzhou had thought it would take a while more; he didn’t have enough fun yet.

The trio opened their palms to check on their numbers. Even the lowest among them, Man Gu, had 350 points, to say nothing of Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou. They were unrivaled devils killing people like flies.

Man Gu asked, “What do we do now? Fight or run?”

“Let’s just run. Based solely on our scores, we already occupy the top three positions; now all that's left is to wait for the competition to end,” Meng Jingzhou suggested. Despite being a descendant of the Meng Family’s main branch, he felt no shame in saying the word “run.”

This was a result of his father’s training. When Meng Jingzhou was young and mischievous, his father had herded them like ducks.

“They’re here!” Someone left a cave and saw the trio. These three are indeed in cahoots! If Flying Swallow hadn’t grown suspicious, no one would have noticed!

This is such a disgrace! As diabolic cultivators, we have always been the ones deceiving others. Since when has it been our turn to get deceived? And we were even completely duped and wrapped around their fingers! My cultivation journey will not go smoothly if I don’t kill these three to vent my anger!

“Time to run~” Meng Jingzhou chirped happily as he took the lead.

“After them!”

“They’re here!”

“Kill them!”

Diabolic cultivators usually fought alone and rarely acted in groups. This large-scale operation of diabolic cultivators was all the more unprecedented.

But now, they were united—bent on capturing the trio!

~~~

When the higher-ups of the Everlasting Creed saw the scene unfold, they couldn’t help but click their tongues in amazement. Even they didn’t wield such influence in commanding the masses.

The creed leader secretly nodded. These three are naturally suited to go undercover in the Dao-Seeking Sect. However, he then found it regretful that the other two vice creed leaders were incompetent to have let such pivotal pawns leave the Dao-Seeking Sect.

~~~

Lu Yang told Meng Jingzhou, “If they really catch up with us, you’ll be the bait.”

“Why me? You came up with all these layers of schemes. You go!”

“I was the one who came up with ideas, and you added the details. You’re more important than me, so you go!”

“The ideas are more important than the details. You go!”

The two kept modestly declined each other, encouraging the other party to be the bait. All this time, Man Gu watched by the side, finding no chance to interject.

I’m just an actor.

“I’ve caught up with them!” Someone with excellent tracking abilities and light footwork was about to touch the hem of Lu Yang’s clothes.

Right then, an invisible attack struck the person. Unable to dodge in time, they were sent flying, a large dent forming in their chest. Before his eyes closed, he saw that his original spot was empty except for a talisman hovering in the air.

“What’s that?”

The talisman seemed to have a consciousness of its own as it floated around, knocking away all the contestants who tried to approach the trio.

Finally, someone saw what kind of talisman it was. “It’s an Invisibility Talisman! These three have help!”

This Invisibility Talisman was drawn by Lu Yang. Its effect was so great that even those with keen senses couldn’t detect anyone in invisibility mode.

The person who hollered soon realized that something was wrong. Whose Invisibility Talisman only conceals the person but leaves the talisman visible?

Lu Yang yelled at the Invisibility Talisman. “Flying Swallow, quickly beat them to death!”

“Flying Swallow is in this with them too?!” The crowd was astonished. Could Flying Swallow’s discovery of the trio’s scheme be a part of the trap too?

The real Flying Swallow was fuming as he watched in safety by the sidelines. I’m at least eighty zhang away! How can the person with the Invisibility Talisman be me?!

“I know! The one with the Invisibility Talisman is your clone!” Flying Swallow suddenly remembered that Lu Yang could create wooden clones.

An astute person with deft hands swiftly removed the Invisibility Talisman, revealing the true identity of the person behind it.

It was a bald Lu Yang—the Bodhi tree clone!

Lu Yang’s Invisibility Talisman could only conceal the person but not the clothing. Since his wooden clone only used tree leaves as cover, they were considered part of the wooden clone.

In other words, the wooden clone was not wearing clothes—perfect for Lu Yang’s Invisibility Talisman!

The Bodhi tree clone wore a leaf garment, resembling someone from the wild. Lu Yang made the clone explode, releasing poisonous gas.

Having anticipated this, Flying Swallow summoned a north wind to blow away the poisonous gas.

“Kill!”

The trio was surrounded. Countless weapons were thrown at them, determined to pierce them until they became hedgehogs, while some directly tried to kill them. There was no blind spot among the attacks, and there was no way they could defend themselves!

Lu Yang sighed. “Now that things have come to this, fusion is the only way left.”

The trio exchanged glances with one another, resolution settling in their eyes. We’re going to fuse and fight!

“Fusion?” Although Flying Swallow didn’t know how they intended to fuse, that didn’t stop him from having an ominous feeling.

“Don’t let your guard down! They’re going to fuse!” Flying Swallow shouted to warn everyone.

Even the higher-ups of the Everlasting Creed were completely bewildered. We’ve never heard that cultivators can fuse together?

As Man Gu let out a loud roar, his muscles swelled. With his left hand, he grabbed Meng Jingzhou’s ankle, and with his right, he seized Lu Yang’s ankle.

Meng Jingzhou activated the cultivation technique, his body emitting a faint golden glow that grew incredibly tough.

Lu Yang clasped his hands together above his head, and sword qi enveloped him.

The three of them fused together!

Flying Swallow, “...?”

1. It can refer to heaven and earth or yin and yang. ☜

2. It’s referring to Qinglong, Baihu, Zhuque, and Xuanwu. This was also expounded upon below a chapter. ☜

Chapter 194: Child, What Wishes Do You Have?

Flying Swallow was not the only one with question marks floating above his head; even the higher-ups of the Everlasting Creed felt that they had broadened their horizons.

Is this a combat style popular among the younger generation? Are we falling behind the times?

~~~

Man Gu swung Meng Jingzhou and Lu Yang around as he spun on the spot, swatting away the covert weapons and incoming attacks.

“I don’t care what bizarre antics you have! All together, attack!” the Flying Swallow bellowed as he charged forward.

Following his lead, the others quickly swarmed in. Even if we have to overwhelm them with sheer numbers, we will crush them to death!

“Fusion Unique Technique: Great Windmill!” the trio shouted in unison as Man Gu lifted the two people and spun rapidly.

What Man Gu now carried in his hands were the sturdiest blunt weapon and the sharpest weapon, allowing him to be on both the offense and defense. Most importantly, the blunt weapon and sharp weapon could attack independently, the epitome of smart weapons.

Meng Jingzhou activated the Heaven-Shaking Six Forms, brandishing his fists to beat enemies until their faces were bruised, their bones broken, and their flesh mangled.

Lu Yang wielded his hands as swords as he channeled sword qi and unleashed the Single Character Sword Mantra, mercilessly slicing down enemies like a sword capable of propping up the sky.

Their teamwork was simple yet highly effective. Man Gu spun, Meng Jingzhou punched, and Lu Yang slashed. Each of them played their own role without interfering with the others.

Flying Swallow’s soft armor split open after getting struck by Lu Yang’s sword qi. If not for the armor, he would be bleeding now.

This Fusion technique may seem random and chaotic, but it’s astonishingly powerful.
