Man Gu seemed to have transformed into an ancient devil god, wielding the two qi of yin and yang in his hands as he slaughtered his way around in the crowd. The contestants would either get smashed to death by Meng Jingzou’s head or hacked to death by Lu Yang’s sword qi.

After suffering a severe loss, the Flying Swallow no longer dared to engage in close combat. Noticing him retreating, the others also planned to flee. Revenge is sweet, but that only matters if we’re alive to enjoy it!

However, there were two problems with this technique. First, all the kills were credited to Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou. Second, they could get dizzy very easily.

“Urgh—” the three of them retched.

Despite having trained themselves for this, the time was too short. Such high-intensity spinning had exceeded their limits.

Lu Yang consoled the other two while retching, “I-I heard that dizziness is caused by our organs. Once...once we reach the Golden Core Stage and become able to control our organs, we can use this move repeatedly!”

“Urgh—is that true?” Meng Jingzhou had doubts about Lu Yang’s words.

“In theory, yes. We’ll test it out when we reach the Golden Core Stage.”

Seeing the trio in poor condition, the crowd prepared to charge toward them again.

The trio changed their strategy. When they saw someone attacking, Man Gu grabbed Meng Jingzhou’s ankle, while Lu Yang grabbed Meng Jingzhou by the neck. The two would treat Meng Jingzhou as a shield to block the incoming strikes.

Realizing that this tactic worked, Lu Yang and Man Gu followed up with the opportunity, charging forward with Meng Jingzhou as their shield.

“Hey hey hey! You two are too much! Me being a shield was not part of our discussion!” Meng Jingzhou protested. Even with my tough body, taking the brunt of the attacks still hurt dearly.

The two put Meng Jingzhou down.

When a few people launched their attacks from the same direction, Meng Jingzhou and Man Gu each hoisted one of Lu Yang’s legs. Lu Yang pulled out the devil saber and faced the enemies at once. Holding his ground, he struck as swiftly and fiercely as a serpent’s flickering tongue.

Suddenly, Lu Yang’s eyes sharpened. He pushed off with his feet and darted toward Flying Swallow.

You’re the brat who keeps causing us trouble!

“You overestimate yourself!” Flying Swallow was not scared of Lu Yang. When it was the three of you attacking together, I had no choice but to admit that I’m no match, but now that you’re alone, you still want to kill me?

Flying Swallow drew out a jade dizi flute,[1] which was his life-bound magical treasure capable of unleashing sonic attacks.

Whoo— He played the jade dizi flute, ready to kill Lu Yang.

Lu Yang sank into the ground and evaded the attack. The trees behind him were sliced cleanly in half, their smooth cross-sections testament to the devastating wound it would have left on a person.

“Earth Escape Technique!” Flying Swallow was shocked, not expecting Lu Yang to know such a challenging Five-Elements spell.

“Where will he pop up?!” He nimbly spun around, anticipating an attack from behind.

To his surprise, the ground beneath him split open, and a Bodhi tree broke through the soil, bearing two Lu Yangs on its branches.

Lu Yang and his clone leaped off the Bodhi tree at the same time. His clone performed Tiger Fist and transformed into a ferocious striped tiger lunging at the Flying Swallow, while Lu Yang swung his devil saber at him. At such close range, he could control his clone with impeccable precision.

Tiger demon Lu Yang was savage, while Lu Yang’s saber carried an overbearing momentum. In such close quarters, the Flying Swallow had no time to play his jade dizi flute.

“Enlarge!” The jade dizi flute extended to the height of the Flying Swallow’s brow, and he swung it to block the attacks from both Lu Yang and his clone.

The jade staff spun rapidly, creating a whooshing sound.

Lu Yang jerked his head to the side, narrowly evading an invisible sonic attack. This is another way of making the jade dizi flute sound!

“You do have some ideas!” Lu Yang sneered. Unfortunately for Flying Swallow, Lu Yang was now on guard, and this move no longer posed a threat to him. In fact, it was considered child’s play in the Dao-Seeking Sect, something not even worth mentioning.

Only someone as unknowledgeable as Flying Swallow would treat this as a viable attack method. But in the face of an absolute gulf in power, what kind of waves do you think you can still stir?

Outside the Dao-Seeking Sect, Lu Yang was confident that he was unbeatable among the Foundation Establishment cultivators, especially now that there were two of him.

He performed a sword technique with the devil saber. “Slashing Word Mantra!”

The tiger demon roared and uttered human words, “Tiger Descends the Mountain!”

Both launched their attacks from different directions, ripping Flying Swallow into pieces. The devil saber instantly recognized its new master and devoured him, making Flying Swallow its most short-lived master.

~~~

When Vice Creed Leader Jin witnessed the scene, he turned to the creed leader. “Wasn’t Flying Swallow hailed as your successor? Aren’t you going to stop this?”

The creed leader let out a cold laugh. “Successor? That’s just a title Flying Swallow slapped onto himself. Through various manipulations and subtle hints, he fooled people into thinking that he was my successor to reap all kinds of benefits.”

“Aren’t you going to punish him?”

“Why should I punish him? If he truly had the ability, I wouldn’t have minded acknowledging him as my successor. But if he lacks the ability, just like we saw today, he’d just end up dead.” A mere Flying Swallow is not outstanding enough to make me truly value him.

The creed leader proceeded to ask the Everlasting Immortal respectfully, “Have you decided who will have the honor of being your vessel?”

“Lu Yang.” The Everlasting Immortal had already made his choice. “This person is ruthless and scheming. His talents and constitution are also top-notch. He barely qualifies to become my vessel!” That said, the Everlasting Immortal believed that Lu Yang was the best vessel he could ask for.

The creed leader felt a twinge of reluctance. Ever since I assumed the position of creed leader, I have never met anyone more suitable as a diabolic cultivator than Lu Yang. Unfortunately, the Everlasting Immortal has selected him. However, it’s his honor to be chosen by the Everlasting Immortal. Sacrificing one Lu Yang for the Everlasting Immortal to return to his peak is a very worthwhile deal.

“Let him come to the secret chamber.”

“Understood.”

The creed leader stood in the air and released a wave of oppressive pressure. “The competition is over! Lu Yang has the highest number of points and is in first place. He will have the honor of receiving the Everlasting Immortal’s blessings!”

Everyone was a witness to Lu Yang’s stellar performance. However, the other participants couldn’t help but feel regretful for missing out on the Everlasting Immortal’s blessing.

“Lu Yang, come with me.” The creed leader beckoned with a hook of his finger, lifting Lu Yang into the air and taking him to the entrance of the secret chamber.

He reminded Lu Yang, “Blessings from an immortal are a matter of great significance. Enter the secret chamber first. You’ll understand what I mean when the time comes.”

“Yes.” Lu Yang’s face was wreathed in smiles, and it seemed genuine, prompting the creed leader to nod inwardly in approval. As expected from the Everlasting Immortal’s devout follower.

Lu Yang walked into the secret chamber and noticed how impoverished the Everlasting Creed was. The chamber was pitch-black with not even a single lamp.

Suddenly, the incense burner beneath the Everlasting Immortal’s statue lit up with three incense sticks. The smoke swirled upward, coalescing into the figure of a benevolent old man.

“Child, come here.” The benevolent-looking old man waved at Lu Yang.

Lu Yang was extremely excited upon seeing the benevolent elder. “You are...you are...”

The benevolent elder smiled. “That’s right, it’s just as you have guessed.”

“You’re really a Statue Demon Spirit?”

The Everlasting Immortal, “...”

“Child, I am the Everlasting Immortal. If you have any wishes, you can tell me, and I shall help you fulfill them.”

1. There are two types of Chinese flutes: di and xiao. The di flute is horizontal, while the xiao flute is vertical. ☜

Chapter 195: Incipient Everlasting Dao Fruit

“Are...are you really an immortal, the Everlasting Immortal?” Lu Yang's body was trembling, unsure of where to place his hands. He couldn’t stop the corners of his mouth from curving into a smile as he got very excited.

“Child, don’t get too excited. I am right here.” The Everlasting Immortal bore a soft visage. “You have clinched first place in this competition. While the winner in the Qi Training category also had their merits, they can’t compare to you. You are truly the rightful number one.

“As a reward, I will fulfill one of your wishes.”

“A wish? Are there any conditions?”

“Feel free to make any wish. There’s nothing I can’t do.”

“I wish for eternal world peace.”

“Why don’t you change your wish?” the Everlasting Immoral Fairy tested the waters. He couldn’t help but admit that his previous statement was a bit exaggerated.

To take over Lu Yang’s body, he had to obliterate his soul. However, his soul was deeply rooted in his physical body. Even if it was deracinated, there would be vestiges of it. That would make the body takeover incomplete and hinder future cultivation. Hence, the best solution was to fulfill Lu Yang’s wishes so that the root of his soul would fall off, allowing the perfect body takeover.

Since Lu Yang is only at the Foundation Establishment Stage and a rogue cultivator, what kind of wish could he possibly have? At most, he may want an immortal treasure, and I can just give it to him. In any case, I can still get it back after taking over his body.

“I wish everyone can become immortals.”

The Everlasting Immortal, “...”

This is even worse than the previous one.

“I wish for tremendous development in productivity, where people can obtain resources without labor and freely choose what they are passionate about.”

“...Another one.”

Kid, are you here to join a diabolic creed or are you preparing to overthrow the Great Xia Dynasty and establish a new one?

Lu Yang looked at the Everlasting Immortal in disappointment. Is this immortal even reliable? He talks bigger than Huang Doudou, yet he can’t fulfill even a single wish.

The Everlasting Immortal was triggered by Lu Yang’s gaze, but he knew that this matter couldn’t be rushed.

“Child, all your wishes concern the world. Don’t you have any wishes of your own?” The Everlasting Immortal patiently guided him. As long as Lu Yang answers that he wants to become an immortal, I’ll have the best reason to take over his body.

Becoming an immortal with your body also counts as fulfilling your wish!

“I do! I wish to cultivate to a realm where I can open up heaven and earth and reconstruct the universe.”

The Everlasting Immortal, “...”

Can’t you make your wishes smaller? If I could do all those things, would I still be here desperately trying to hoodwink you?

Lu Yang concluded that the Everlasting Immortal was not competent, so he decided to lower his expectations. “I have a Big Senior Sister whose cultivation is unmatched. I wish to defeat her.”

“Hahaha, that’s easy. I can suppress her with just a flip of my hand.” The Everlasting Immortal couldn’t stop laughing.

He finally said a simple wish! Isn’t it just the senior sister of a Foundation Establishment cultivator? How strong could she be? I, the almighty Everlasting Immortal, can easily subdue such a little lass!

“After I take over your body, I’ll naturally help you suppress that little lass!”

“Take over my body?!” Lu Yang’s pupils constricted. He never expected that what was supposed to be receiving blessings from an immortal would become a body takeover by an immortal.

He turned on his heel, planning to escape from this den of devils.

“Give up. If you can escape from me, where would that leave my dignity?!”

Despair gripped Lu Yang’s heart as he sensed the frightening oppressive pressure from the Everlasting Immortal.

If I hadn’t won the competition, would the outcome have been different?

If I hadn’t made a wish, would the outcome have been different?

If I hadn’t joined the Everlasting Creed, would the outcome have been different?

Panic, regret, fear, and many more emotions gushed into his heart. But it was too late.

Taking in Lu Yang’s contorted expression, the Everlasting Immortal involuntarily sneered. He turned back into smoke and flew into Lu Yang’s mental space.

Then, he was slapped.

A crisp sound rang out as the Everlasting Immortal was sent flying.

“So you’re the brat who’s impersonating this immortal fairy?” A certain unruly woman immediately began to punch and kick the Everlasting Immortal.

If an unknowing outsider had chanced upon this scene, it would have looked like a bratty young girl beating up a centenarian.

“Let me tell you, in ancient times, even Heaven Mandate and the others didn’t dare to do this. Which onion do you think you are?! How dare you impersonate me? Did you pay respects at the dock? Did you offer tributes? Did you get my approval?”

“Who are you?!” The Everlasting Immortal was still a little dazed by the turn of events. He hadn’t even registered what was happening when he was suddenly slapped.

Why is there someone else inside this kid’s mental space? Is he so popular that everyone is lining up to take over his body?

“You don’t even know me, and you still have the audacity to be out there?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy had long found him detestable, for he had swindled others out there by using the title of “Everlasting.”

On the other hand, despite being the real thing, she was either scorned by Lu Yang or bullied by Yun Zhi. My life is truly miserable. Now that the Everlasting Immortal has come in, I can finally sort him out!

The Everlasting Immortal was not a familiar face to her.

“Immortal Fairy Fist Technique!” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy randomly made up a name as her pink fists rained down on the Everlasting Immortal.

The fist technique might appear arbitrary, but in fact, it was extremely exquisite; each strike was unpredictable and elusive.

The Everlasting Immortal felt that every strike had hit his vital spots and weaknesses. Even though he was in a soul form, he still had the sensation of wanting to spit blood and kneel on the ground. He felt as if his soul was on the verge of shattering into oblivion.

Where on earth did this demon monster come from?

“You’ve gone too far with your bullying!” The Everlasting Immortal was furious. With the Everlasting Dao Fruit in his hands, ever since he was resurrected, he had been revered as an ancestor by the Everlasting Creed. He would get everything he wanted, be it wind or rain. When have I suffered such humiliation?

“Everlasting Through the Ages!” the Everlasting Immortal roared in anger as a ball of golden light appeared in his palm with ethereal immortal energy. It was so resplendent that one couldn’t open their eyes.

This golden light was neither physical nor spiritual in nature but something beyond both. It possessed a mystical power that felt invincible and immune to all laws. Any attack directed at the Everlasting Immortal would turn to nothingness.

“The incipient form of the Everlasting Dao Fruit?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was astonished. She finally understood where the faintly familiar aura on the creed leader had come from.

This imposter of mine does have some substance to him.

“You’ve got some knowledge, woman. This is the Everlasting Dao Fruit. In its presence, I am everlasting, unaging, undying, and imperishable.[1] I am the one and only throughout the ages. All fates return to nothingness, and all attacks will turn into the void. Your attacks can’t do anything to me!” With the Dao Fruit summoned, the Everlasting Immortal gained much confidence.

Huang Doudou revealed a look of contempt. “You’re just a poor imitation of me. What’s there to be proud of?

“Immortal Fairy Fist Technique!” Huang Doudou brandished her pink fists again, shattering the Everlasting Immortal’s proud barrier with one punch. The pink fists did not decrease in momentum as they landed squarely on his face.

“This Incipient Dao Fruit is quite interesting.” The Everlasting Immortal casually snatched the Incipient Dao Fruit over, studying the golden substance in her hand keenly.

Inside the golden substance, countless runes and rules appeared and disappeared, as if depicting the eternal changes of the universe and illustrating the true meaning of “Everlasting.”

Lu Yang peeked at it curiously, but the Everlasting Immortal Fairy shoved him to the side. “Go go go! Your current cultivation realm is too low to look at this.”

“What...what have you done?!” The Everlasting Immortal was thrown into a frenzy. The Incipient Everlasting Dao Fruit was originally tightly connected to him, even more so than the fusion with his soul. In theory, no force should have been able to separate us.

But now, I can’t feel any connection to it! I have lost complete control!

Who on earth are they? How did they do that?!

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy smirked smugly. “Flaunting the Dao Fruit in front of me is like a novice trying to show off at a master’s door.”

Just then, a celestial-like voice echoed in the Everlasting Immortal’s ears. “I heard you wanted to suppress me?”

Only then did the Everlasting Immortal notice that there was a third person in the mental space.

Exactly how many people are there in your mental space?!

Is taking over someone else’s body something you gotta queue up for these days?!

1. The original Chinese version has all the adjectives starting with the same negation character. Unfortunately, I could only make the first three adjectives end with “-ing.” ☜

Chapter 196: Why Are There So Many People Inside Your Mental Space?!

If there are two people inside one’s mental space—the original owner and a powerful soul—it can be explained as the powerful soul simply waiting for the right time to take over the body.

But three people? Aren’t you going too far? Does a mental space really need to be so lively? With me joining in, there are now altogether four people.

The Everlasting Immortal deemed himself unknowledgeable to have never heard of anyone’s mental space containing four souls.

Yun Zhi closed her book and quietly watched the Everlasting Immortal. In the spirit of showing respect for elders, I had let the Everlasting Immortal Fairy make the first move.

Now, it’s my turn.

“Even without the Dao Fruit, I am still invincible!” The Everlasting Immortal brushed off his defeat and got back on his feet, launching another attack.

“A World of Devils!” Ceaseless black devil energy surged from within the Everlasting Immortal, and countless devil figures writhed and howled. The dark mist flooded the entire mental space and headed straight for Yun Zhi.

Without even glancing at it, Yun Zhi raised her arm, and the golden bell at her wrist chimed lightly. Her voice was cold like an immortal fairy in a silent moon palace. “Falling Cloud Palm.”

A white cloud appeared behind Yun Zhi, undulating like the vast ocean. As it devoured the black devil energy, the cloud transformed into a massive wave that gushed toward the Everlasting Immortal. The latter felt as if he was a mere pebble in front of the unrestrained river, insignificant and helpless.

“Undying Flame of the Netherworld!

“Eighteen Golden Bell Shields!”[1]

Red-black flames flared up from the Everlasting Immortal’s chest, rapidly spreading into a thin membrane over him. Eighteen enormous golden bell shields dropped one after another with a loud bang, covering the Everlasting Immortal to block him from the incoming attack.

The ocean waves crashed relentlessly at the Everlasting Immortal, breaking through his layers of defenses. After the membrane formed by the red-black flames clashed with the waves, it evaporated, leaving him to bear the aftermath of the attack. He was blasted away until he reached the boundary of the mental space.

Yun Zhi rose from her seat and moved gracefully toward the Everlasting Immortal, as if lotus flowers bloomed with every step.

“Stop there, stop there! I’m telling you to stop!” the Everlasting Immortal screamed. The attack had completely pulverized his confidence.

“Gold Crushing Stone Smashing Palm!” A huge hand formed from fog descended from the sky. This strike was capable of shattering mountains, splitting the earth, and destroying treasures; it had been renowned in the cultivation world for a long time.

Yun Zhi waved her hand casually, and the hand-shaped fog vanished into thin air.

“Tribulation Breaking Everlasting Body!” The Everlasting Immortal summoned his dharma body.

If they were in the outside world, the dharma body would have been tens of thousands of zhang tall; reaching the heavens and stars would be no problem. No attack would even tickle the dharma body upon coming into contact, while the dharma body’s offensive power was devastatingly destructive and unstoppable.

However, with the constraints of the mental space, it was hard to demonstrate the full extent of the Tribulation Breaking Everlasting Body, though its power was not at all attenuated.

“Die!” The Everlasting Immortal seethed with ruthlessness, determined to crush Yun Zhi with a single slap.

Without lifting her head, Yun Zhi merely waved her hand twice, and the terrifying dharma body instantly disintegrated.

“Crimson Lotus Descent!”

“Reverse Five-Elements Killing Array!”

“Buddha-Slaying Fist Technique!”

“Dao-Governing Heavenly Talisman!”

The Everlasting Immortal no longer held back, using every method at his disposal—palm techniques, fist techniques, arrays, talismans—unleashing an assortment of moves that demonstrated his mastery, as if he had practiced them for centuries.

Had any ordinary cultivator witnessed such a barrage of attacks, they would have been frightened out of their wits. However, when it came to Yun Zhi, these attacks were utterly inconsequential.

Lu Yang’s mental space seemed to transform into her domain. As if she was swatting away flies, with every simple wave of her hand, all the attacks would evanesce.

“Far beneath an immortal’s level.” That was Yun Zhi’s evaluation of the Everlasting Immortal’s attack. Not only did he lack offensive power, but his ken was also limited. The same attacks, if executed by the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, would yield much better results.

“These are all modern techniques. Do you not have ancient ones?” Yun Zhi realized that the Everlasting Immortal’s moves might have been varied, but none were ancient or lost arts.

That’s very odd.

After the ancient era experienced great destruction, many legacies were lost. Most offensive methods today were what the later generations had derived.

Suppose the Everlasting Immortal is an ancient immortal. In that case, he should be able to use ancient unique techniques like the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, such as the Water-Repelling Mantra that separates all water and the very embarrassing Play-Dead Technique.

Yun Zhi hadn’t struck down the Everlasting Immortal with one palm because she wanted to see what kind of ancient attacks he could execute.

“Who...who on earth are you?!” The Everlasting Immortal’s fear was even more intense than when he lost his Dao Fruit. This power is totally absurd.

What are all these people inside this kid’s mental space? The first one snatched my Dao Fruit with unfathomable methods, while the second person has boundless cultivation and power!

“Didn’t you say that you were going to help Lu Yang suppress me?”

“You are Lu Yang’s Big Senior Sister?!” The Everlasting Immortal’s voice shot up by an octave, his eyes wide in shock. For a moment, he forgot his current situation and began inwardly cursing Lu Yang for his shamelessness.

What kind of monstrous wishes did this kid make? One was more preposterous than the other! I originally thought that defeating Lu Yang’s Big Senior Sister would be a cinch, that’s why I agreed and came in to take over his body.

Now, things are the complete opposite. Lu Yang’s Big Senior Sister is the one suppressing me effortlessly!

The greatest mare’s nest ever.

The Everlasting Immortal finally figured out that Lu Yang was not his follower at all. He had pretended to be bait the whole time just to lure me in.

How risible I was to think that I could take over the perfect vessel.

Could he be an undercover agent from the righteous path? But his performance in the competition didn’t seem like an act.

Realization suddenly dawned upon the Everlasting Immortal. Lu Yang was sent by the other three diabolic creeds! Everything makes sense now!

“Don’t hit me anymore, I surrender! I’ll tell you everything you want to know. Please just spare my life!” the Everlasting Immortal knelt on the ground and groveled for mercy, completely switching his attitude.

“Speak! Who are you really?! Why are you impersonating me?!” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy stopped examining the Incipient Dao Fruit. She hopped over with Lu Yang following behind, while Yun Zhi listened quietly from the side.

All three of them wanted to know the answer to this question.

“I am...” The Everlasting Immortal dragged out his voice in an attempt to attract their attention. His plan was to unleash all the power within him to break through the barrier around the mental space and run for his life. I’m going to escape this cursed place!

Bang!

As expected, he collided with the barrier, unable to move even an inch forward. Yun Zhi had already anticipated his action and reinforced the strength of Lu Yang’s mental space. The Taciturn Daoist Priest had used this tactic on Yun Zhi many times—needless to say, it never worked.

“Don’t hit my face, don’t hit my face! I’ll really tell you everything this time!” The Everlasting Immortal finally faced reality. It’s best to surrender early. They are too experienced. None of my tricks are useful here.

“Speak, what is your name?!” Huang Doudou blustered.

“I’m shameless.”

“Hmm? You have such self-awareness?”

1. The Jinzhongzhao or Golden Bell Shields is one of the four great arts in Shaolin. ☜

Chapter 197: Forthcoming Confession For Leniency

“No, I mean that my name is Bu Yaolian, “Bu” as in fabric, and “Yaolian” from buyaolian (shameless).”[1] The Everlasting Immortal was now obedient after all that beating, willing to answer every question patiently.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy frowned. “Why do you have such a strange name?”

Lu Yang remarked, Are you sure you should be the one calling someone else’s name strange?

The Everlasting Immortal sighed. “I don’t want this name either, but it’ll take a long time to explain.”

“Take your time.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy conjured a folding stool to sit on, resting her head against her palm as she waited for the Everlasting Immortal’s story.

Yun Zhi and Lu Yang also quietly listened by the side.

The Everlasting Immortal spoke truthfully, “I don’t know where my consciousness came from, nor do I know how I was born. A long time ago, the first trace of my consciousness developed, but it was very faint, barely able to detect my surroundings. It felt like looking at flowers through a fog; everything was obscure.

“I could sense an unknown strength constantly accumulating within me, making me grow stronger bit by bit, but my consciousness remained blurry, and I couldn’t discern the outside world.

“I could also feel many memories being added to my consciousness, but at that time, I didn’t have the ability to think for myself. All I could do was accept those memories passively, unable to organize or process such a massive amount of information.

“As my consciousness gradually grew stronger, I began to hear distant voices calling ‘Everlasting Immortal.’ From then on, the term ‘Everlasting Immortal’ registered in my memory. However, I was still unable to process the memories, and I didn’t know what ‘Everlasting Immortal’ meant.

“I don’t know how much time passed. Perhaps it was hundreds of years, or maybe thousands of years. In any case, my consciousness suddenly became clear, just like a drowning person fished out of the water and regaining their senses of the outside world.

“The first thing I heard when my consciousness became distinct was ‘Great Everlasting Immortal (Brazen-Faced) Bu Yaolian, please save your devoted followers and this world.’ From then on, ‘Bu Yaolian’ became my name. I originally had no name. It was only because the creed leader called me ‘Bu Yaolian’ that I received my name.

“After that, I could finally process the vast flood of memories I had, and I understood what they represented.

“In those memories, I saw someone stumble across a secret domain and accidentally enter it. They learned about an immortal called the Everlasting Immortal who protected the human race in ancient times. The Everlasting Immortal possessed the Everlasting Dao Fruit which allowed this immortal to be resurrected. After the person left the secret domain, he founded the Everlasting Creed and attempted to revive the Everlasting Immortal.

“The Everlasting Creed became stronger with increasingly more followers joining. They tried to please the Everlasting Immortal through slaughter and attempted to call out the immortal’s real name in hopes of resurrecting the immortal.

“It was then that I understood that I was the Everlasting Immortal the Everlasting Creed had revived. As long as someone truly believed in me, prayed to me, and worshipped me, I would be able to obtain their memories.

“Since the creed leader prayed to me, I manifested in the world through a statue to fulfill the creed leader’s expectations. Since I possessed his memories, everything the creed leader knew, I knew too. I saw that he was gravely injured and needed a century of rest. As he was my most devout and powerful follower, I decided to heal him.

“After I received my name, I could sense that I wielded a ball of golden light. Associating it with the memories, I deduced that this was the Everlasting Dao Fruit, and I used a portion of its power to treat the creed leader’s injuries.

“However, I don’t know whether I am the real Everlasting Immortal. My earliest memory originated from the first follower from more than ten thousand years ago. I have not a single memory of the ancient era. For instance, when the creed leader asked me who had refined the sky of stars, I couldn’t give an answer, but neither could I say that I didn’t know, so I told him that this matter was not someone at his level could learn about.

“As I wasn’t sure how the followers would react if they knew about my true situation, I had no choice but to pretend that I had been resurrected from the long ancient past. In reality, I have remained in a soul state all this time.

“I knew this couldn’t go on forever, so I told the creed leader that I wanted to take over a body, return to my peak, and save the world.

“The creed leader believed me and gathered all the Qi Training and Foundation Establishment cultivators, organizing this competition. I would then choose the most suitable candidate to take over their body.”

Lu Yang asked, “Then you chose me?”

The Everlasting Immortal nodded helplessly. Exactly! Of all people, why did I have to choose you? My eyesight was poor, and I selected you, which resulted in me suffering from a horrible beating.

Had it been anyone else, my body takeover would have been successful.

The Everlasting Immortal elucidated a few more matters and clarified some questions, such as why he lacked knowledge of ancient techniques, why he needed to take over a body, and why he was named Bu Yaolian.

However, there were still some questions that even he couldn’t explain. Who exactly was he? Where did he come from? How did the Everlasting Dao Fruit appear?

Lu Yang looked at Yun Zhi and the Everlasting Immortal Fairy expectantly. Now is the time for the experienced and knowledgeable seniors to step in.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy furrowed her brow slightly, looking like she was pondering something, though she didn’t seem reliable.

This whole time, Yun Zhi had been silently listening to the Everlasting Immortal’s tale, trying to discern whether his experiences were true or fabricated. She concluded that the general outline of the story should be true.

Noticing Lu Yang’s gaze, she could tell that her junior brother was brimming with questions which answers he hoped to find from her. “The grand elder of the Heaven Strategy Sect, the Dao Amplification Savant, had posited a hypothesis, saying that there is no Everlasting Immortal or Everlasting Dao Fruit in this world and that the Everlasting Creed is creating an immortal.”

Lu Yang nodded secretly. An old senior is indeed very reliable.

Hearing Yun Zhi’s words, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s head snapped up right away. Which nook did this Dao Amplification Savant come out from? He dares question the existence of my Dao Fruit? Does he not know how much effort I had expended to produce this Dao Fruit?! Even the Heaven Mandate Immortal and the other three envied me so much!

Lu Yang suggested that the Everlasting Immortal Fairy listen to Yun Zhi first and only settle the score with the Dao Amplification Savant later.

Yun Zhi continued, “Where do souls come from? And where do they return to? These are hard questions that remain unsolved in the cultivation world to this day. The Dao Amplification Savant believes that the human consciousness is a form of power. As long as such consciousness is sufficiently strong and abundant, it is possible for a soul to materialize.

“Of course, that’s only a hypothesis. It can’t explicate how the first soul came into being. However, your case aligns with this theory.

“Since the founding of the Everlasting Creed, it has been 14,000 years. Throughout these years, at least a million followers have prayed to a non-existent Everlasting Immortal. With such a long passage of time and an overwhelming amount of consciousness, it’s completely possible to create a soul—and that is you, Everlasting Immortal.

“However, for you to emerge, there might be an additional factor required—killing.

“The power you just used, have you ever thought about where those devil energy filled with resentment came from?

“Humans stand at the pinnacle of all beings and are the favored child of heaven and earth, born with innate ‘spiritual nature.’ What diabolic cultivators do is strip away this ‘spiritual nature’ from humans through slaughter, transforming it into their own power.

“Your followers, in their attempts to please you, engaged in ceaseless slaughter, creating boundless karmic debts. The power derived from these killings then became your power—the power of a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator.”

1. Shameless is “buyaolian” in Chinese. Bu Yaolian’s name is pronounced exactly the same way, including the tones. Another interesting thing is that “bu” acts as a negative prefix here, and “yaolian” means to want face, while “buyaolian” means not wanting face or shameless. ☜

Chapter 198: Mastermind Behind the Scenes

The chasm between immortals and mortals was not something that could be surmounted with sheer consciousness alone. The Everlasting Immortal’s cultivation realm had yet to reach that of a true immortal; he was still at the Transcendent Tribulation Stage. Although he was an incomplete Transcendent Tribulation cultivator due to his lack of a physical body, his possession of the Incipient Everlasting Dao Fruit compensated for his deficiencies in combat power.

Any other Transcendent Tribulation cultivator would have likely found themselves at a significant disadvantage had they encountered the Everlasting Immortal in their mental space. However, of all people, the Everlasting Immortal happened to run into the bona fide Everlasting Immortal Fairy. In the presence of a real Dao Fruit, the Incipient Dao Fruit couldn’t bring out even a modicum of its power.

After being taught a lesson, the Everlasting Immortal realized that he was probably not a true immortal but a mere imitation of the Everlasting Immortal.

“As for how the Dao Fruit came to be, Senior, what are your thoughts?” Yun Zhi tossed the question to the Everlasting Immortal Fairy.

This was precisely the question the Everlasting Immortal Fairy had been pondering earlier. She took out that golden light and surmised, “My initial judgment was correct. This thing can barely be called the Everlasting Dao Fruit. It’s far from becoming mature and is considered to be in its incipient form. The appearance of the Dao Fruit should follow the same principle as how this kid appeared—both relied on consciousness.”

Lu Yang was curious. “Is a Dao Fruit something you can easily conjure with just the consciousness? Wouldn’t that make becoming an immortal too simple?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy shook her head and corrected Lu Yang’s misconception. “It’s not a Dao Fruit but the incipient form of a Dao Fruit. Moreover, this so-called Dao Fruit is the Everlasting Creed’s product from over ten thousand years of accumulation. One will face severe limitations should they try to produce an Incipient Dao Fruit based on consciousness alone.”

A Dao Fruit was the hallmark of immortality, the ultimate product capable of altering the world’s rules. Its very concept far exceeded Lu Yang’s realm of knowledge. This is not something he can grasp now.

“The incipient form of a Dao Fruit and a true Dao Fruit are worlds apart. As long as I want to, I can conjure as many Incipient Everlasting Dao Fruits as I wanted, but there will only ever be one Everlasting Dao Fruit., and that’s the one I have now.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy flashed a confident smile. She believed that her Everlasting Dao Fruit was the strongest, surpassing the Dao Fruits of the Heaven Mandate Immortal and other immortals. As for the Incipient Dao Fruit, she felt that it wasn’t even something worth mentioning.

“But an Incipient Dao Fruit has the potential to replace a true Dao Fruit.” Yun Zhi’s words splashed a basin of cold water on the Everlasting Immortal Fairy. The latter understood what Yun Zhi was getting at and instantly calmed down.

Lu Yang asked, “What does that mean?”

When it came to matters of the Dao Fruit, only the Everlasting Immortal Fairy and Yun Zhi were clear about what was going on; Lu Yang and the Everlasting Immortal were completely in the dark. In fact, the Everlasting Immortal couldn’t even differentiate between a Dao Fruit and an Incipient Dao Fruit. If he hadn’t just heard the explanation, he wouldn’t have known how his own incipient Dao Fruit had come about.

Yun Zhi elucidated, “The Incipient Dao Fruit is a crude prototype that is very simple, and even its internal structure is unstable. If the Incipient Dao Fruit gradually matures, it will grow increasingly similar to a Dao Fruit.

“Furthermore, only one Dao Fruit of the same type can exist at a time. For the Incipient Dao Fruit to fully mature, it must destroy the existing mature Dao Fruit and supersede it.”

Lu Yang was astonished. “That is to say, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s Dao Fruit could be replaced by the Incipient Everlasting Dao Fruit?” He couldn’t help but worry for the Everlasting Immortal Fairy. Although she’s not particularly reliable, rarely helpful, and often causes trouble for me, I still hope that her Dao Fruit won’t be replaced by others.

Yun Zhi shook her head with a grave expression. “Senior commands the highest authority under the realm of ‘Everlasting.’ No one can rival her in this domain, not even an Incipient Dao Fruit that is infinitely close to maturity.

“The only circumstance where an Incipient Dao Fruit supplants a Dao Fruit is if the Dao Fruit is ownerless, while the Incipient Dao Fruit has an owner.”

Lu Yang let out a sigh of relief. “That’s good then. Since the Everlasting Immortal Fairy is still alive, no one can replace her.”

“But she wasn’t originally supposed to be alive.” Yun Zhi’s words struck Lu Yang like a bolt of lightning.

That’s right, if not for me accidentally calling out the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s real name, she might not have been resurrected even after the Battle of the Great Era has ended. Perhaps it’s just as Big Senior Sister has said, without me, it would have taken another three hundred thousand years for someone else to accidentally call out the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s real name.

Wait, that’s not right. If the Everlasting Immortal Fairy hadn’t been revived, the Everlasting Immortal would have been able to let the Incipient Everlasting Dao Fruit mature and replace the original Everlasting Dao Fruit. Once the Battle of the Great Era begins, the Everlasting Immortal could lead the Everlasting Creed to emerge from hiding and spread his name far and wide. At that time, who would dare to jokingly call out the title ‘Everlasting Immortal Fairy’ like I did?

By then, I’m afraid that the Everlasting Immortal Fairy would never have the chance to be resurrected anymore—she would truly and irrevocably die.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy seemed to have also arrived at a similar conclusion, and the possibility left her deeply shaken.

Yun Zhi quickly sorted out her thoughts. “In the ancient era, Senior was ambushed and killed. The Everlasting Dao Fruit lost its owner and became an ownerless item.

“The mastermind behind the scenes revealed the concept of the Everlasting Dao Fruit to the public and fabricated a non-existent Everlasting Immortal. They led the Everlasting Creed’s followers to believe, imagine, and resurrect this Everlasting Immortal. All this while, the Everlasting Immortal was unaware of this matter, and he would try his best to speed up the maturation of the Incipient Dao Fruit. When the time is ripe, the mastermind will strike, seizing the Everlasting Dao Fruit and claiming it as their own.

“The only thing I’m uncertain about now is whether the mastermind plans to seize the Dao Fruit after it fully matures or when it is about to fully mature, or perhaps should I wonder...have they already arrived?” Toward the end, Yun Zhi’s voice grew as cold as a thousand-year-old glacier, its killing intent sending a shiver down Lu Yang’s spine.

Yun Zhi and the Everlasting Immortal Fairy simultaneously let out their spiritual consciousness and scanned every inch of the surrounding space to ferret out the mastermind behind the scenes.

Suddenly, in the corner of the secret chamber, the space rippled. A pitch-black figure emerged unhurriedly, clapping rhythmically as he praised Yun Zhi’s brilliance.

Lu Yang stared at the pitch-black figure. Although the man was clearly there, when Lu Yang scanned the area with his spiritual consciousness, nothing was there. From Lu Yang’s perspective, that person was like a bottomless black hole brimming with ambition and capable of devouring all things. It was utterly terrifying.

Yun Zhi and the Everlasting Immortal Fairy stepped forward, positioning themselves in front of Lu Yang as they warily confronted the intruder.

“As expected of the strongest person from the Five Great Immortal Sects. In the Central Continent, only a few pose a threat to me—and you are by far the greatest!

“Initially, I had come here simply because I wanted to see if the Incipient Everlasting Dao Fruit had truly been formed. Who would have thought that I’d gain so much from just observing for a few days?”

The pitch-black figure turned his gaze toward the Everlasting Immortal Fairy. Although Lu Yang couldn’t see his face clearly, he felt that the person was smiling. “I honestly never expected you would actually be resurrected, Everlasting Immortal Fairy. You’re the unforeseen variable I never anticipated.

“Since you’ve been revived, the plan to replace the Everlasting Dao Fruit with the Incipient Everlasting Dao Fruit is now defunct. What a pity, the Everlasting Creed’s 14,000 years of effort has gone down the drain just like that.” The pitch-black figure shook his head regretfully, though it was unclear whether he pitied the Everlasting Creed or lamented the failure of his plan.

“Heaven Mandate, Qilin, Epoch, Nine-Layers—who are you?! Stop skulking about and show your true face!” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy shouted harshly. This person had sought to completely erase my existence. There’s a life-and-death enmity between us that can never be resolved!

There must be an outcome between me and this pitch-black figure!

The pitch-black figure chuckled and shook his head. “Were there really only five immortals in your era? And was the Nine-Layers Immortal truly the first immortal?

“Immortal Fairy, there are too many things that cannot be ascertained. How can you be so sure that I’m one of those four?”

“Enough with your hocus-pocus!” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy gritted her teeth in anger.

Yun Zhi wasted no words. She acted decisively, unleashing her full power in an attack.

The dark figure’s expression turned solemn. “As I thought, your strength far surpasses what you show to the outside world. Even if my main body were here, it would probably still be hard to defeat you.

“To think that someone like you emerged after the ancient era. Truly, a marvel of heaven and earth.”

Aware that he was no match, the dark figure resolutely decided to self-detonate.

“A pity that my main body won’t be able to learn what transpired here.”

Chapter 199: Who Could Have Done This?

The gulf in strength between the shadowy figure and Yun Zhi was too vast. As the shadowy figure knew that he was no match for Yun Zhi, the chances of him escaping were slim to none. Rather than risk exposing himself, it was better to self-detonate immediately to ensure the safety of his original form. If Yun Zhi discovered his lair, his main body could say goodbye to the Battle of the Great Era.

Damn it! Why does someone like this exist on the Central Continent?! Has all the fortune from heaven and earth amassed on the Central Continent?

And why has the Everlasting Immortal Fairy been resurrected? Apart from the few of us, who else knows of the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s existence, let alone her name?

How on earth did the Everlasting Immortal Fairy get revived?! Her resurrection is only possible if someone calls out her honorific title and real name. Who uttered them?!

Just like how it was described, the Everlasting Dao Fruit was indeed everlasting through the ages, capable of resurrection even after a thorough death.

When the shadowy figure self-detonated, numerous questions streamed into his mind, though none was answered.

His self-detonation was silent and without a trace; his body disintegrated into dust, and the dust dissipated into spirit qi, returning to the heavens and earth.

“He escaped?” Lu Yang was baffled. The shadowy figure’s methods were too profound for him to understand.

Yun Zhi shook her head lightly, her gaze revealing a baleful look and regret. “He didn’t escape but killed himself.”

“Then wouldn’t his main body learn of what happened here? Would he find out about the Everlasting Immortal Fairy?” Lu Yang recalled the shadowy figure’s last words before self-detonating: “A pity that my main body won’t be able to learn what transpired here.”

Was he trying to mislead us, or was it really the truth?

Yun Zhi refuted Lu Yang’s speculation. “The main body won’t know. Its clone also wouldn’t dare to let his main body know. If the clone could relay its situation to the main body, I would have been able to track the main body based on their connection.”

Lu Yang couldn’t fathom his Big Senior Sister’s methods either.

“It’s just that...” Yun Zhi’s eyes held a trace of doubt, as though she was mulling over something.

“It’s just that, what?”

“The shadowy figure felt very familiar. I may have fought him before.”

Both Lu Yang and the Everlasting Immortal Fairy were astounded.

Yun Zhi continued, “It was probably about a hundred years ago. I happened to sense an immortal appearing on the Central Continent, so I asked him to identify himself. He refused me, and a battle ensued between us.

“He likely underestimated my strength. The moment we clashed, he had already fallen into a disadvantage. I pressed my advantage and wounded him. Realizing that he wouldn’t gain anything from continuing the fight, he feigned an attack on a nearby city. While I defended the city, he made use of the opportunity to slip away. By the time I tried to chase after him, he was already gone.

“That person concealed himself from head to toe and enveloped themselves in a mist of primal chaos. The techniques used were also rather generic and prevented others from discerning their origins. These are all very similar to the shadowy figure we encountered today.”

Yun Zhi suspected that the shadowy figure today was the clone of the person she fought a century ago.

Lu Yang mused to himself, If Big Senior Sister’s guess is correct, then the shadowy figure’s comment “As I thought, your strength far surpasses what you show to the outside world” was merely his lie to pretend that he didn’t know about Big Senior Sister’s ability.

The more Lu Yang thought about it, the more plausible it seemed. If the shadowy figure didn’t know about Big Senior Sister’s ability, why would his first reaction be to self-detonate instead of running away? It simply didn’t make sense.

From the beginning to the end, the shadowy figure only spoke a few sentences, and most of them were likely lies.

Wily old fox.

Fear still lingered in the Everlasting Immortal. Although the two fairies didn’t show mercy when they beat me, each person hitting harder than the other, at the very least, they didn’t kill me outright. Had I fallen into that shadowy figure’s hands, not only would my Dao Fruit have been snatched, but the likelihood of being silenced would have been close to a hundred.

Lu Yang asked, “Immortal Fairy, can you guess who he might be?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy knitted her brow, slightly hesitant. “The Nine-Layers Immortal was the most proficient in manipulating clones, but if the other three wanted to imitate him, that’s also doable for them.”

Lu Yang pressed further, “Could there have been other immortals besides the five of you?”

Faced with Lu Yang’s question, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy was no longer certain. Could it be that the Nine-Layers Immortal was really not the first immortal?

“How did you determine that the Nine-Layers Immortal was the first immortal back then?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy searched through her memories. “When the Nine-Layers Immortal ascended to an immortal, the world radiated with immortal light and rang with immortal melodies. Nine-colored rain descended from the skies and brought about blessings and acclaim, showering fortune on all beings. When the four of us ascended to immortals later, nothing like that happened.”

Lu Yang was stunned. “Was that the special treatment for the first to ascend to immortality?”

Yun Zhi nodded. She had read about the Nine-Layers Immortal’s immortal ascension in ancient records, and it matched the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s account, or rather, she should say that the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s description was even more vivid as someone who had experienced it firsthand.

The first to ascend to an immortal was indeed outstanding.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy shook her head. “No, that’s not it. Later, when the five of us were dining together, the Nine Layers Immortal had too much to drink and confessed that all those phenomena back then were his own doing. He had secretly orchestrated everything and expended a huge amount of rare natural treasures.”

Lu Yang, “...”

Yun Zhi, “...”

Why does it feel like every ancient tale I hear from the Everlasting Immortal Fairy completely overturns my understanding of history? Lu Yang felt that the ancient era as portrayed by the Everlasting Immortal Fairy was entirely different from what the shadowy figure had depicted.

~~~

In a mysterious location, a black figure sat atop a throne made from piled-up bones. He opened his immortal eyes, unleashing boundless immortal light that illuminated the surroundings. As the immortal light flashed briefly, it cast an eerie glow on the corpses and bones strewn across the ground, creating an uncanny contrast.

The black figure slowly rose and stretched his body as his eyebrows furrowed slightly. “Why is this chair so hard and uncomfortable?”

“Whose idea was it to use piled-up bones to make a chair? There’s not even a cushion.” The black figure shook his head and decided to find another place to sleep.

Suddenly, he sensed something off and grunted softly.

His attendant asked cautiously, “Your Excellency, what is the matter?”

“The clone I sent to the Everlasting Creed has disappeared?”

The black figure had always been able to sense the connection between him and the clone, thereby allowing him to determine the location of his clone. Just now, the connection was completely severed, indicating that someone had eradicated his clone. He had poured in countless resources and efforts to create this particular clone, yet it was now gone just like that. It would be a lie to say that it didn’t pain him.

“What? Your Excellency's clone has disappeared?!” The attendant’s expression seemed to be of genuine shock.

His Excellency is an immortal, and the clone of an immortal should be sufficient to traverse the world freely. How could it have disappeared in the Central Continent?

The black figure ruminated. “Who could have done this?”

The first suspect he ruled out was the Everlasting Immortal. A soul created from consciousness couldn’t possibly have the power to kill my clone without a trace. There are only so few people who can do that. He had sent his clone to investigate the situation instead of heading there himself because he feared being detected by those few people; he was not ready to expose his identity now.

He had tampered with his clone such that even if it was captured, there was no way for the other party to deduce his identity. Moreover, they might even be misled by the information from the clone and point their suspicion toward other immortals.

It’s best to be cautious in life. Otherwise, if you’re as simple-minded as the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, you won’t know when someone will get rid of you one day.

“Could it be that fellow from the imperial palace? Or is it Yun Zhi from the Dao-Seeking Sect? Or could it be someone else?”

Since my clone has been hiding in the Everlasting Creed, those that came into contact with the Everlasting Creed could only be the Great Xia Dynasty, which is dedicated to cracking down on diabolic creeds, and the Five Great Immortal Sects, which focus on slaying demons and eliminating evil.

Chapter 200: I’m Still a Baby!

“That fellow in the imperial palace stays in a forbidden area and rarely takes action, so the likelihood of him being involved is low.

“Then could it be Yun Zhi from the Dao-Seeking Sect?

“That’s not right either. My clone hid by the Everlasting Immortal’s side, and the Everlasting Immortal has always been cautious. How could anyone have found their way there?

“Or could the Everlasting Immortal have awakened his conscience, turned over a new leaf, and voluntarily turned himself in to the Great Xia Dynasty or the Dao-Seeking Sect to plead for leniency?”

The black figure couldn’t help but feel greatly troubled at the thought of those few people from the Central Continent. Ever since the ancient era ended, he had been planning everything meticulously. Logically, there shouldn’t have been any problems.

According to his plan, the Great Qian and Great Yu dynasties proclaimed that there would be fortuitous opportunities to become an immortal in future generations. They asked people to enter a deep slumber and only wake up during the battle of the Great Era to sow chaos and muddle the situation.

Only when it came to the Great Xia Dynasty did unexpected individuals appear one after another, including immortals. These immortals were no longer pawns but players on equal footing with him, forcing him to revise his plans multiple times.

“Especially that Yun Zhi. She’s so young, yet her talent is unprecedented across all ages.”

“Your Excellency, may I ask who this Yun Zhi is...?” The attendant tried to recall the famous and influential figures from the Central Continent but couldn’t think of anyone called Yun Zhi. His Excellency hardly praises someone. This is the first time he’s so generous with his compliment. How astonishing must Yun Zhi’s talent be?

The black figure sneered. “She’s just a little lass from the Dao-Seeking Sect. A hundred years ago, I headed to the Central Continent, and she personally came to receive me, warmly asking me where I was from. I couldn’t be bothered with her, and there was nothing more she could comment on.

“Subsequently, I saw that she had some skills, so I decided to spar with her and offer a bit of guidance. After the exchange, I wanted to leave, but she kept pursuing me, pressing me for more pointers. I believed that relationships between cultivators should be as bland as water and that things shouldn’t be forced. It would be better for our fate with each other to end there. Giving too much advice would instead hinder her path. Thus, I used some escape techniques, unwilling to get tangled up with her further.”

“Your Excellency’s cultivation is number one throughout the ages.” The attendant cupped his fists in flattery, eliciting a hearty laugh from the black figure.

He was relieved. Staying with His Excellency is still the safest option. In the Battle of the Great Era, even the slightest misstep can lead to eternal damnation. With His Excellency’s unrivaled cultivation and schemes that span the ages, he’ll undoubtedly have the upper hand during the Battle of the Great Era. By following His Excellency, I can pick up some leftover benefits, enough for me to lead a comfortable life. With some luck, I might even become an immortal.

As the black figure recalled his encounter with Yun Zhi a hundred years ago, he couldn’t help but feel a sense of humiliation weighing on him. I can’t just say that I had initiated the attack because I saw how young the little lass was, only to be completely defeated and forced to flee. I’ve lived for countless years, yet a child defeated me? That’s an utter disgrace.

I mustn’t tell this to my subordinates; it’ll undermine my authority.

The black figure remembered that he had planned to visit the Everlasting Creed a hundred years ago to check on how close they were to forming the Incipient Dao Fruit. Before he could even find his way to the Everlasting Creed, however, he bumped into Yun Zhi, and a fierce battle ensued.

At the thought of the power Yun Zhi had displayed, the black figure felt that Yun Zhi could be denominated the strongest in the Central Continent—his biggest obstacle in the Battle of the Great Era. Ever since then, he would only send his clones to the Central Continent to avoid being captured.

“Could it be that the Great Xia Dynasty is favored by fortune?”

The notion of fortune was elusive. To become an immortal, one needed not just talent and strength but also luck. For instance, the Transcendent Tribulation cultivator who mastered Law Follows Words could have become an immortal, but he was unlucky and met Huang Doudou, resulting in his demise.

Despite pondering for half a day, the black figure still couldn’t reach a conclusion, so he decided to just give up. “Whatever, I’ll stop thinking about all this. Since my clone has been eliminated, it implies that the matter of the Incipient Dao Fruit is already out of the bag. Those from the Central Continent will be on their guard against immortals infiltrating their land. Getting discovered would create unnecessary trouble. I just won’t head there for the time being. I shall wait until the Dao Fruit is close to maturity, and that’s when I’ll step in to claim it! If I can obtain the Everlasting Dao Fruit, that will grant me a tremendous advantage during the Battle of the Great Era.

“It’s a pity for the Everlasting Immortal Fairy that her resurrection is destined to be impossible. She only has herself to blame for possessing the Everlasting Dao Fruit. If she doesn’t die, no one else can lay their hands on it.

“I really didn’t expect that she would be the one to form the Everlasting Dao Fruit back then; how enviable...” The black figure’s voice faded into silence as he departed, leaving only a pile of bones behind.

~~~

“What should we do with the Everlasting Creed?” Lu Yang asked. The goal of their mission was already achieved. They had found the headquarters of the Everlasting Creed, captured the Everlasting Immortal, and even forced the mastermind’s clone to self-detonate.

Now, only one question remained: how should they deal with the Everlasting Creed?

If they act carelessly, would they inadvertently alert the mastermind? Could they make use of the Everlasting Creed to lure out the mastermind behind the scenes?

Yun Zhi looked at Lu Yang in surprise, flummoxed about why Lu Yang would ask such a question.

“Of course, we report it to the authorities.”

“Ah?”

“There are so many people. The Dao-Seeking Sect can’t interrogate them all even if we capture them. We might as well let the Great Xia Dynasty handle it.”

Lu Yang almost blurted out, “I didn’t know that the Dao-Seeking Sect has such proper methods.” In Lu Yang’s impression, interrogation under torture, coercion and bribes, infiltrating diabolic creeds, and winning first place in the tournaments of diabolic creeds were all standard operations of the Dao-Seeking Sect.

Oh, right, half of that was my doing.

“When are we reporting the case?” Lu Yang asked eagerly. It feels amazing to be dismantling a large-scale den of illegal activities.

Yun Zhi thought for a moment. “Four days ago?”

“Wut?”

Yun Zhi explained, “Right after we entered the headquarters four days ago, my soul had already left my body and went to the Great Xia Dynasty to report the case. The reason we didn’t act was to wait for the Foundation Establishment and Qi Training cultivators to gather so that we could capture them in one fell swoop.

“Of course, the Everlasting Immortal was an unexpected bonus.”

The Everlasting Immortal felt that he had brought this upon himself. Why did I have nothing better to do than take over someone’s body? As long as I stayed hidden, even if the entire Everlasting Creed was destroyed, the Great Xia Dynasty wouldn’t be able to find me.

Yun Zhi shifted her gaze to the Everlasting Immortal. “As for you...”

The Everlasting Immortal hurriedly implored, “My attempt at the body takeover failed. You can liken it to attempted murder. Surely, that’s not worthy of the death penalty! I have always abided by the law and have never done anything illegal. Look, even the statue is reading a book on criminal law!”

Lu Yang turned his eyes to the statue. The statue of the Everlasting Immortal is really holding a book on the penal code.

The creed leader had acted swiftly, updating the Everlasting Immortal statue’s design to hold a copy of the penal code in a bid to encourage the creed’s members to study the law.

“Besides, my soul only became complete the moment I received my name. It’s just been five days since I got my name, so I am only five days old—I’m just a baby! According to the penal code of the Great Xia Dynasty, I am considered under the age of criminal liability and thus exempted from any criminal prosecution or punishment.

“I’m still a baby! Your Excellencies, please be magnanimous and let me off this once!”

Lu Yang stared at the Everlasting Immortal face, so decrepit that it looked like he should be buried in the ground. His name really does suit him.

You could actually say something so shameless, Bu Yaolian?
